# CLAUDE.md

This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.

## What this repo is

A hybrid: a static HTML/CSS design package **+** a Node.js/Express/Prisma/MySQL backend that is being built incrementally on top of those same design files. All copy is Bahasa Indonesia (`lang="id"`). The build-out is staged:

1. ✅ Skeleton (Express + static serving + sensitive-path block)
2. ✅ Prisma schema + MySQL (MariaDB via XAMPP), seed
3. ✅ Auth + RBAC (JWT cookie + bearer, 8 roles, audit, rate-limit)
4. ✅ Public paket landing + booking (`/p/:slug?a=<slug>`) with agent lock-in
5. ✅ Agen portal `/agen` — Leads CRM (Cold/Warm/Hot/Lunas kanban) + Marketing kit + Wallet/komisi + Analytics
6. ✅ Admin/HQ dashboard `/admin` — Overview / Paket / Manifest / Bunking / Finance tabs, plus Users + Jemaah + Audit + Booking-detail pages
7. ✅ Money flow — Payment recording, status transitions, auto-Komisi on LUNAS, cancel + refund (negative-Payment), editable notes
8. ✅ Ops jobs — daily cron to auto-EXPIRE overdue `JemaahDocument` rows (CLI + HTTP trigger)
9. ✅ Jemaah self-service portal `/saya` — public HTML register + booking claim by `(bookingNo, phone)` + read-only booking detail. Claim flow soft-merges anonymous booking-profiles into the user's canonical profile. Logged-in jemaah booking new paket from `/p/:slug` auto-links to their account (no claim needed). Profile + document self-edit at `/saya/profile`, including per-doc file attachment (5mm) stored in private `private/docs/<jemaahId>/`.
10. ✅ Notifications — pluggable channel queue (`Notification` model) with console sender by default. Booking create / payment received / komisi payout auto-enqueue WA + email notifs. Admin viewer at `/admin/notifications`, processed via `npm run job:send-notifications` CLI or HTTP trigger. Jemaah-side inbox at `/saya/notifications` (5ll) scoped via `recipientUserId`; per-channel opt-out (5jj) on `JemaahProfile.notifEmail/notifWa` marks rows `SKIPPED` instead of suppressing them. Retry with exponential backoff (5nn): FAILED rows auto-retry up to 5 attempts (1m/5m/30m/2h/12h) via the same worker before going terminal.
11. ✅ Payment gateway — Midtrans Snap integration (5pp). `PaymentIntent` model decouples gateway state from realized `Payment` rows. Jemaah pays online via `/saya/bookings/:id` "Bayar online" button → Snap hosted checkout → signature-verified webhook materialises a Payment via `recordPayment` (single source of truth for money math + komisi). Fake mode when `MIDTRANS_SERVER_KEY` absent — full intent/webhook loop testable without external creds.
12. ✅ Crew portal `/crew` (5oo) — read-only muthawwif workspace. M2M `PaketCrew` join (admin-managed from paket edit page). Crew see their assigned paket dashboard + a stripped manifest (jemaah identity / phone / emergency contact / passport / room / doc-pills) with NO money fields — separation of duty.
13. ✅ Mobile experience — PWA shell (`shared/manifest.webmanifest` + `shared/sw.js`), installable `/saya` and `/crew`, mobile bottom-nav for jemaah, responsive @media baseline + per-view tightening. Offline-friendly attendance: IndexedDB queue (`shared/attendance-queue.js`) replays form submits via auto-flush on `online` event + 20 s tick. Crew SOS — `Incident` model + `/admin/incidents` queue with OPEN → ACKED → RESOLVED state machine + EMAIL+WA fan-out to ACTIVE admins on creation. Operational hardening: hot-path indexes (audit + intent compound), weekly `prune` retention job that bounds Notification/JobRun/failed-intent growth (AuditLog + Payment never pruned).
14. ✅ Per-paket × per-agent komisi matrix — `AgentPaketKomisi(agentId, paketId, rate)` join table prepended to the rate chain so admins can declare "ahmad-w gets 15% on VVIP-2026 only" without code changes. Admin UI: panel below Crew on `/admin/paket/:slug/edit`. The rate at LUNAS is still locked into `Komisi.amount` — later edits to the matrix never recompute historical rows.
15. ✅ Cached document thumbnails — uploads auto-generate a 256-px JPEG (`sharp`) at `private/docs/<jemaahId>/thumbs/<docId>.jpg`. Thumb routes `/saya/documents/:docId/thumb` + admin variant serve the cache; **graceful fallback** to the full file when no cached thumb (legacy uploads + non-image mimes still work). Doc panel `<img>` srcs swapped to `/thumb`; click-through `<a>` still hits `/file` for full quality.
16. ✅ Analytics extension — two new panels powered by `getPerPaketPerformance` + `getKomisiMonthly` in `src/services/analytics.js`. Agen Analitik tab gets per-paket leaderboard (revenue + conv% + status counts) + 6-month komisi bar chart (earned vs paid). Admin overview gets cross-agen mirror (`getPerPaketLeaderboard` + `getKomisiMonthlyAdmin`) including `agentCount` (distinct agents per paket) + `directCount` (Kantor Pusat walk-ins). Both komisi-monthly variants share `komisiMonthlyImpl` and exclude CANCELLED rows (undone work, not income).
17. ✅ Web Push for SOS / Incidents — `PushSubscription(userId, endpoint, endpointHash, p256dh, auth)` per (user × browser). `pushToAdmins` fans out to every ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS subscription as a third layer alongside EMAIL+WA in `notifyIncidentCreated`. Service worker `push` handler shows a Notification + `notificationclick` focuses an existing tab. SOS sets `requireInteraction:true` so the toast sticks until the admin clicks. VAPID env-driven; absent → console fake mode (mirror Fonnte/SMTP pattern). Self-cleanup: 404/410 from web-push scrubs the dead subscription row.
18. ✅ Paket clone for next season — `POST /api/paket/:slug/clone` copies Paket row + hotels + days + prices into a fresh DRAFT with `kursiTerisi=0`. Optional `includeAgentOverrides` carries the per-agen rate matrix forward. **Never** copies bookings / payments / komisi / rooms / crew / incidents — clone is a template, not a historical record. `newReturnDate` defaults to `newDeparture + source.durationDays` so trip length stays consistent. Audit row stamps `clonedFromSlug` so lineage is queryable. UI: "Clone untuk musim berikutnya" modal in paket-edit form-footer.
19. ✅ Print-friendly manifest — `GET /admin/manifest/:slug/print` renders an A4 landscape worksheet for airport check-in (`views/print-manifest.ejs`). Active-only bookings sorted by room-first (kamar groupings stay adjacent), with passport / emergency contact / doc pills columns. `@media print` sets A4 landscape + `display: table-header-group` on thead + `page-break-inside: avoid` per row. Cetak button next to Export CSV in the admin Manifest tab.
20. ✅ Per-jemaah booking voucher — pairs with stage 19 (manifest is the admin's list, voucher is the per-jemaah summary handed out at manasik). Routes `GET /admin/bookings/:id/print` (4 admin VIEW roles) + `GET /saya/bookings/:id/print` (jemaah, scoped to `jemaahUserId`, **returns 404 on cross-user access — not 403 — so existence isn't leaked**). Service `src/services/bookingVoucher.js` returns the same shape for both paths so the view doesn't branch. A4 portrait worksheet: hero + jemaah identity + perjalanan (airline + route + hotel cards) + pembayaran (3-cell money strip + history) + condensed itinerary + agen contact footer. "🖨 CETAK VOUCHER" link in the crumb bar of both detail pages.
21. ✅ Payout slip — completes the print trifecta (manifest = admin worksheet, voucher = per-jemaah handout, slip = per-payout accounting receipt). `GET /admin/payouts/:id/print` renders an A4 portrait slip with payoutNo + amount + agen identity + komisi breakdown table + 2 signature boxes (agen + yang membayar). `getPayoutSlip` wraps `getPayoutById` with computed totals + Bahasa method label. **Sanity check**: when `sumKomisi !== amountIdr` (shouldn't happen — createPayout snapshots in a transaction), the slip prints a warn-strip rather than silently masking the discrepancy. "🖨 CETAK SLIP" link in the crumb bar of `/admin/payouts/:id`.
22. ✅ Per-paket profitability — admin leaderboard answers "which paket actually makes money" not just which generates revenue. `Paket.costPerPaxIdr` + `costNotes` (both nullable) carry the fully-loaded vendor cost per pax (hotel + flight + visa + ops). `getPerPaketLeaderboard` extends with `lunasPaxCount + totalCostIdr + komisiLiabilityIdr + netMarginIdr + marginPct`. Komisi liability sums EARNED + PAID (CANCELLED + PENDING excluded). **Null cost → null margin fields** (no misleading 0% / 100% when costs aren't tracked yet). **Negative margins reported honestly** — admin needs to see losses to fix them. Form on paket edit: "Biaya per pax (Rp)" + "Rincian biaya" with 3-state preprocessor so empty input persists as null. Leaderboard card footer colors marginPct by tier (≥20% emerald / ≥5% gold / ≥0% amber / negative ruby).
23. ✅ Pre-departure readiness checklist — `GET /admin/paket/:slug/checklist` answers "who's missing what before departure" at H−30 / H−7 / H−1. 8 boolean checks per active booking: paspor present + paspor valid (`expiry ≥ departureDate + 6 months` — Saudi rule), VISA_UMROH / VACCINE_MENINGITIS / HEALTH_CERT / MANASIK_CERT each VERIFIED, kamar assigned, kontak darurat present. Score = passed/8 × 100; tier ≥100 ready / ≥60 partial / else critical. **Sort = critical → partial → ready, lowest score first within tier** so the worst-of-worst land at the top of the admin's follow-up list. Countdown badge auto-colors by H−days (green ≥30d / amber ≥7d / ruby ≤7d / ink past-departure). Default filter hides ready rows so the page opens straight to actionable items. "✓ Checklist" button in the admin Manifest tab toolbar next to 🖨 Cetak + ⇩ Export CSV.
24. ✅ Departure calendar — `GET /admin/calendar?year=&month=&date=` completes the planning trio (manifest = per-trip detail, checklist = per-trip readiness, calendar = trip-by-trip overview). UTC-aligned month grid (Su-Sa) with paket badges per cell color-coded by status + fill rate (full emerald / semi gold / low ink / draft amber / closed ruby), overflow rendered as "+ N lagi". Optional `?date=YYYY-MM-DD` opens a drill panel below the grid with kursi% + status pill + Manifest/Edit action links. Month-nav crosses the year boundary; "Hari ini" jump shown only when not already on current month. Service excludes ARCHIVED + soft-deleted paket. Sidebar "Kalender" link in Operasional group (above "Cari booking").
25. ✅ Enriched recent activity feed — `src/lib/auditFormat.js` turns raw AuditLog rows into `{sentence, url, badge, amountIdr}` for the admin overview tab. Per-entity copy: Booking CREATE → "Booking baru …", STATUS_CHANGE → CANCEL/REFUND/TRANSFER/CLAIM, KomisiPayout → "Payout … · Rp …", Incident → SOS/INCIDENT badge by type, JemaahDocument → UPLOAD/VERIFY/EXPIRE (respects `autoExpired`), Paket cloned flag → CLONE badge, Retention sweep → PRUNE. Each row clickable into the relevant detail page. Badge tokens map to status color (emerald success / ruby destructive / gold money / sapphire neutral state-change / amber alerts).
26. ✅ Paket waitlist — `PaketWaitlist(paketId, fullName, phone, status, promotedBookingId?)` with composite-unique `(paketId, phone)` so re-submission upserts. Public CTA `/p/:slug` auto-flips to "Daftar waitlist →" when `kursiTerisi ≥ kursiTotal`; POST `/api/waitlist` (rate-limited 8/min/IP). Admin queue at `/admin/paket/:slug/waitlist` with per-row Promote (kelas + paxCount + agentSlug) and Cancel actions. **promote calls `createBooking` via the canonical pipeline** — money math, komisi, notif all converge on the same path. Status machine WAITING → PROMOTED (terminal, carries `promotedBookingId` backref) | CANCELLED. Re-joining after CANCELLED reopens to WAITING (defensive upsert).
27. ✅ Daily activity digest for OWNER — `src/services/dailyDigest.js → buildDailyDigest({now})` aggregates yesterday's revenue + booking + ops state from the **same sources `/admin` reads** (no separate counters / denormalised state). Counts: new + LUNAS bookings, new jemaah, new leads, incidents created + still-open. Money: payments in (IDR-only filter — non-IDR cash rarely happens; mixing currencies would make the line confusing), refunds out, LUNAS revenue, komisi earned + paid, net revenue. 7-day rolling comparison (bookings + LUNAS). `notifyDailyDigest({digest})` fans out one EMAIL row per ACTIVE OWNER (not OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS like other admin alerts — this is strategic, not operational; admins already have real-time access via `/admin`). CLI `npm run job:send-daily-digest` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-daily-digest` + systemd timer at 07:00 daily. `send-daily-digest` registered in `EXPECTED_INTERVAL_MS` so `/api/health` flags a missing digest. **Idempotent**: re-running for the same wall-clock day returns the same numbers — duplicate runs just enqueue duplicate emails, no DB drift.
28. ✅ Yesterday-at-a-glance widget on `/admin` overview — surfaces the same `buildDailyDigest()` output the 07:00 email uses as a 6-cell panel ("Kemarin · {tanggal}") above the status-breakdown chart on the admin overview tab. Cells: booking baru / revenue LUNAS / pembayaran masuk / komisi earned / jemaah baru / insiden (warn-colored when OPEN > 0), plus a 7-day rolling footer. Calls `buildDailyDigest()` from `getAdminOverview` with try/catch — **a digest aggregation failure must NOT bring the overview down** (KPIs + recent activity are independently load-bearing). `yesterday` is null in that case and the view conditionally omits the panel. Same source as the email means UI and inbox never disagree.
29. ✅ Day-over-day delta pills in the yesterday widget — `buildDigestWithComparison({now})` runs `buildDailyDigest` twice (yesterday + day-before) and emits a `deltas` map keyed by metric. Each delta carries `{diff, pct, direction, good, empty}`. **Polarity-aware**: `incidentsCreated` + `refundsOutIdr` are reverse-polarity (more = worse), the rest are forward (more = better). View renders coloured arrow pills per cell: emerald when favourable, ruby when not, muted when flat or empty. Edge cases handled explicitly — `previous=0, current>0` returns `pct=null` so the view picks a `+N` label instead of a "% of zero" lie, and `both=0` flags `empty=true` for a neutral "—". Windowing rules go through `buildDailyDigest` both times so the two surfaces can't drift apart.
30. ✅ Delta arrows in the OWNER digest email — same `buildDigestWithComparison` output now feeds the 07:00 EMAIL fan-out. Each metric line carries an inline suffix (`  ·  ▲ 12%` / `  ·  ▼ Rp 200.000` / `  ·  =` / `''`) so the inbox shows the same trend the dashboard widget shows. CLI + HTTP trigger swapped from `buildDailyDigest` to `buildDigestWithComparison`. **`notifyDailyDigest` is backwards-compatible** — if a caller passes a bare digest (no `deltas` key), every suffix renders as empty string so the template stays string-stable and old smoke scripts keep working. Suffix-rendering format matches the widget polarity: `pct=null → ' · ▲ +N'`, flat → ' · =', empty → ''. Template carries one `{{trend*}}` placeholder per metric so future formatting tweaks live in one file.
31. ✅ Needs-attention panel — `src/services/needsAttention.js → getNeedsAttention()` rolls up stuck operator items in three categories: terminal-FAILED notifs (`status=FAILED AND (nextRetryAt=null OR attemptCount>=5)`), cancel-requests >24h pending (jemaah-side `cancelRequested=true` without admin action), OPEN incidents >24h old. Panel above the yesterday widget on `/admin` (ruby left-border + ageing column), and a `{{needsAttentionBlock}}` section appended to the OWNER digest email so the inbox also surfaces aged items. Block is empty (zero-cost) when nothing is stuck. `buildDigestWithAttention` wraps both into one pipeline call so CLI + HTTP trigger pick up the same payload. **All three categories use a 24h ageing cutoff** — fresh items don't crowd the panel; the SOS surface (`/admin/incidents`) and cancel-request banner (`/admin/bookings/:id`) already handle in-hour triage.
32. ✅ Per-paket weekly recap — `src/services/paketWeeklyRecap.js → getPaketWeeklyRecap({slug})` answers "what happened on THIS paket in the last 7 calendar days?" with new bookings + LUNAS + payments IDR-only + refunds + docs verified + cancelled. Dropdown on `/admin` overview (defaults to first ACTIVE paket; query param `?recapPaket=<slug>` selects another). 6-cell grid + a "Booking baru terkini" list (top 5) + footer links to edit + manifest. Window: previous 7 *complete* calendar days (today-so-far deliberately excluded — recaps that flicker as the day progresses are misleading). Soft-deleted + unknown slugs return `null` so the view conditionally hides.
33. ✅ Weekly summary email — `src/services/weeklyDigest.js → buildWeeklyDigest({now})` aggregates the previous full Mon–Sun + week-before for comparison. Monday-anchored convention (Indonesian work-week). Weekend re-runs idempotent: `resolveLastFullWeek` always returns the most-recent COMPLETED week regardless of day-of-week. Includes a `topPaket` rank (top 3 by new bookings, with paket title attached) and an inline `{{topPaketBlock}}` in the email. `WEEKLY_DIGEST_OWNER` notif type (migration applied), `notifyWeeklyDigest` fan-out, CLI `npm run job:send-weekly-digest`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-weekly-digest`, systemd timer Mon 07:05 (5 min after the daily so they arrive in order). Polarity-aware deltas same as daily — `cancelledBookings` joins `refundsOutIdr` + `incidentsCreated` as reverse-polarity metrics. Local-TZ `weekStart`/`weekEnd` formatting via `localYmd` helper — the ISO `slice(0,10)` UTC-truncation bug from the daily digest is *not* repeated here.
34. ✅ YoY paket comparison on leaderboard — `Paket.clonedFromId` column (migration applied) is now populated by `clonePaket` so clone lineage lives on the row (durable, queryable via FK), not just in AuditLog. `getPerPaketLeaderboard` runs a batched `summariseLifetimeTotals` for distinct parent IDs and attaches `previousSeason: {paketId, slug, title, lunasRevenue, lunasCount, marginPct, revenueDelta, revenueDeltaPct, marginDeltaPp}` per row. Leaderboard card adds a YoY strip — `▲ revenue +40% / ▼ margin −3pp` etc. — colour-coded by polarity. **Pct=null when parent has zero LUNAS revenue** (avoid divide-by-zero); the view falls back to a signed Rp delta. **MarginDeltaPp=null when either side lacks cost data** (can't honestly compare). No N+1 — one batched query per dimension regardless of how many clones are in view.
35. ✅ Refund analytics panel — `src/services/refundAnalytics.js → getRefundAnalytics({days, limit})` answers "where is money leaking?" over the last 90 days (configurable). Default 90d; top 10 per dimension. Two lenses — per paket and per agent (Kantor Pusat walk-ins bucketed under `__kp__` sentinel). Each row carries `{paid, refunded, refundCount, refundRatePct}`; ratePct = refunded ÷ paid × 100, rounded to 0.1. **IDR-only filter** to match the rest of the analytics. Sort by absolute refund amount (largest leak first) — rate-sort would surface tiny paket with a single tiny refund. Header KPI shows total refund + overall rate colour-coded by tier (≥5% ruby / ≥2% amber / >0% gold / 0% emerald). Panel renders on /admin overview between the leaderboard and komisi chart, only when total refunded > 0 (hidden on clean slates).
36. ✅ Per-agent weekly digest — mirror of stage 33 scoped per `AgentProfile`. `src/services/agentWeeklyDigest.js → buildAgentWeeklyDigest({agentId, now})` aggregates the previous full Mon–Sun for one agent: new bookings + LUNAS + cancel + leads (created/converted/lost) + conversion rate + komisi (earned/paid) + top paket sold. Returns null when agent is suspended / soft-deleted (caller skips). `listActiveAgentsForDigest` is the iterator helper. `notifyAgentWeeklyDigest` enqueues one EMAIL per call, indexed by `relatedEntity=AgentProfile` so audits can group by agent. CLI `npm run job:send-agent-weekly-digest` loops every active agent and catches per-row failures so a bad row doesn't abort the batch. New `AGENT_WEEKLY_DIGEST` enum (migration applied). Cron Mon 07:10 (after OWNER weekly at 07:05). Polarity-aware deltas include `cancelledBookings` + `leadsLost` as reverse.
37. ✅ Smart payout reminder — closes the loop on stage 36. `src/services/payoutReminder.js → getOverduePayoutCandidates({thresholdIdr})` aggregates EARNED komisi per agent and surfaces those ≥ Rp 1M (configurable). Includes `ageDays` from the oldest EARNED row so admins can see how long agent X has been waiting. `notifyPayoutReminder` fan-outs to OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — separation of duty same as the payout workspace). **Silent on empty** — quiet weeks don't generate noise. New `PAYOUT_REMINDER_OWNER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-payout-reminder`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-payout-reminder`, cron Mon 07:15 (after agent weekly at 07:10). Body inlines top 10 candidates + "+ N agen lainnya…" for the rest so the email stays scannable.
38. ✅ Refund drill-down page — `GET /admin/refunds?paket=<slug>` or `?agent=<slug>` (sentinel `kantor-pusat` for walk-ins). `getRefundDetails` returns up to 200 REFUNDED Payment rows in the window + each row's booking + jemaah + cancel reason + agen. View shows KPI strip (total + count + average) and a table of clickable bookings. Refund analytics panel rows on `/admin` now link directly to this page. **No filter → redirect to overview** (guard against landing on an empty page from a bookmark). Window respects `?days=N` (capped 1–365).
39. ✅ Profitability gauge on paket-edit — `src/services/paketProfitability.js → getPaketProfitabilitySnapshot(paketId)` returns a lifetime snapshot mirroring the leaderboard math (so editing "Biaya per pax" here moves the leaderboard pill the same way). 4-cell panel inline below the cost input: Revenue LUNAS / Total biaya vendor / Komisi terikat / Net margin (with polarity-colored margin pct). Hidden when no LUNAS bookings exist (no point in showing zeros). Same null-fallback as stage 22 — cost missing → totalCostIdr=null → marginPct=null → cell renders "butuh biaya per pax" instead of misleading 0%. New panel renders only in edit mode (passed via opts); create form skips it cleanly.
40. ✅ Per-paket forecast — `src/services/paketForecast.js → getPaketForecasts({days, now})` computes 14-day booking velocity (mean + stddev of daily counts) and projects days-to-full per ACTIVE future-departure paket. Returns `dtfLowDays / dtfDays / dtfHighDays` (±1 SD confidence band so the UI renders a range, not false precision). Sort: most urgent first (lowest dtf), no-velocity rows last. CANCELLED bookings excluded from velocity (they represent intent that didn't stick). Edge cases explicit: `full=true, dtfDays=0` for paket already full; `noVelocity=true, dtfDays=null` for 14d-idle paket (avoid divide-by-zero). Risk tag flips to `'short'` when projected dtf > daysToDeparture (paket won't fill before takeoff). Panel on /admin overview with PENUH/PEKAN INI/<1 BULAN/AMAN badges color-coded.
41. ✅ Komisi liability aging — `src/services/komisiAging.js → getKomisiAging({now})` buckets EARNED komisi rows by age (`now − earnedAt`) into 0-30/30-60/60-90/90+ day windows. Per-agent rollup with per-bucket amount + count + `oldestDays`. Sort by oldestDays desc (90+ candidates land at the top regardless of Rupiah — agents waiting longest are the bigger trust signal). Panel on /admin overview shows 4 summary cells + a table; the 90+ column is highlighted ruby + bold to draw the eye. Status filter is strict EARNED — PAID/PENDING/CANCELLED excluded. Pairs with stage 37: that reminder says WHO crosses a Rp threshold; this says WHO has been waiting longest regardless of amount.
42. ✅ Waitlist promote nudge on cancel — when `cancelBooking` frees seats AND the paket has WAITING waitlist entries, `notifyWaitlistSlotFreed` fires an EMAIL fan-out to ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — promote action lives in admin queue, not cashier). Body lists up to 5 longest-waiting candidates with `ageDays` so admin can promote without leaving the inbox. **Silent when waitlist is empty** (no signal worth sending). **Fire-and-forget posture**: nudge failure logged but never aborts the cancel (the freed seat is the load-bearing change). New `WAITLIST_SLOT_FREED` notif type (migration applied). Loop closes: jemaah joins waitlist → admin gets nudge on cancel → promotes via existing `/admin/paket/:slug/waitlist` flow.
43. ✅ Manifest close countdown — `src/services/manifestClose.js → getManifestClosing({urgentHours=72})` surfaces ACTIVE paket whose `manifestClosesAt` is either within 72h of now or already overdue. Paket with `manifestClosesAt=null` (admin chose "never close") or already at `kursiTotal` are excluded — close date is moot once full. Panel on /admin overview shows each row with a one-click "+ 24 JAM" form POST → `extendManifestClose` adds N hours (default 24, capped 1–168). **Smart base**: when paket is overdue, extension starts from `now` not from the past date, so "+24 jam" actually buys 24 future hours. Overdue rows get a ruby left-border + bold count in the panel header.
44. ✅ Smart promote deep link — the stage 42 nudge email now includes `?promoteOldest=1` deep link alongside the plain waitlist link. The waitlist route resolves to the oldest WAITING entry, passes `highlightId` to the view, which (a) adds a gold pulse to that row, (b) shows a top banner explaining the highlight, (c) auto-scrolls to and focuses the kelas dropdown so admin can tab through immediately. **Pure UI hint** — actual promotion still goes through the same POST flow, so this stays composable with manual selection. Empty-waitlist case renders a separate banner explaining the jemaah may have been promoted by another admin.
45. ✅ Per-agent sparkline — performa agen table on /admin overview gets a 30-day daily booking trend chart per row. Computed inline from the already-loaded `bookings` array (no extra query — one bucket pass over the existing data). Inline SVG path, 120×28 px, auto-scaled to per-agent max so a slow agent's small spike is still visible. Subtitle shows ▲/▼/= last-7d vs prev-7d trend. Agents with zero recent activity render "—" instead of an empty chart. Trend pill colour: emerald up / ruby down / muted flat. Table column added to header + body; colspan="9" empty state updated.
46. ✅ Stalled hot-leads agent digest — daily 08:00 per-agent EMAIL listing their COLD/WARM leads with `updatedAt > 7 days ago` (cutoff configurable). Most-stalled lead lands first. CONVERTED + LOST always excluded (terminal). New `AGENT_STALLED_LEADS` enum + migration. CLI `npm run job:send-stalled-leads`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-stalled-leads`, cron daily 08:00 (after the OWNER digest sequence at 07:00-07:15). Silent on agents with empty stalled list — no noise on quiet days. Same per-agent-iteration pattern as stage 36: per-agent failures caught, batch continues.
47. ✅ Doc expiry warning — per-doc visual indicator on jemaah edit page when `expiresAt` is approaching (≤60d amber, ≤14d ruby, EXPIRED ruby). Row gets a colored left-border + an "⏱ expire dalam Nh" pill + a one-click "↻ RENEW" button. Renew is a UI-only reset (status → PENDING, refNumber → empty, expiresAt → empty, focus refNumber input + flash highlight) — admin then types the new doc info and clicks SIMPAN, which goes through the existing upsert. REJECTED docs are excluded (not active credentials). No new endpoints — pure UI scaffolding around the existing `/api/jemaah/:id/documents` flow. The global "expiring soon" jemaah filter (`?expiringSoon=1`) already handles cross-jemaah triage.
48. ✅ Paket conversion funnel — new `PaketView(paketId, visitorId, dayKey, agentSlug?)` model with `@@unique([paketId, visitorId, dayKey])` so multi-refresh within the same day stays at one row (migration applied). Public `/p/:slug` route mints a non-httpOnly `rp_vis` cookie (32-hex random, 1-year max-age) on first visit; subsequent visits reuse the same id. Visit upsert is fire-and-forget — landing page render never blocks on the analytics DB write. Admin overview gets a "Konversi paket" panel: per-paket unique visits + non-CANCELLED bookings + `conversionPct = bookings ÷ visits × 100` over last 30 days. **`conversionPct=null` when visits=0 but bookings>0** (avoids divide-by-zero and misleading "∞%" — admin still needs to see those rows because they reveal traffic-blind bookings). Sort by visits desc. Walk-in agents who visit a paket page also get counted — the signal is "someone landed", role-agnostic.
49. ✅ Conversion attribution on Booking — `Booking.firstViewAt` + `viewCount` columns (migration applied) snapshot the visitor's view history at create time. `/api/booking` POST reads `rp_vis` cookie, calls `getVisitorAttribution({paketId, visitorId})` to compute first-touch + visit count from existing `PaketView` rows, and passes the result to `createBooking` via the new `visitorAttribution` param. **Best-effort lookup** — a missing cookie or no prior views just yields null, which createBooking stores as default `viewCount=0` / nulls. Admin booking-detail page renders an "Attribution" strip below the notes when any field is populated: "visit 3× sebelum booking · pertama 5h sebelum · varian hero B · via fb / cpc · ramadhan-2027". Hidden cleanly for admin walk-ins and pre-S48 bookings.
50. ✅ Hero A/B test — optional `Paket.heroTitleHtmlVariantB` column (migration applied) lets admin define a second hero copy. When set, `/p/:slug` deterministically picks A or B per visitor cookie (parity of first hex digit, so refreshes are stable). `PaketView.heroVariant` records which one was served. Paket-edit form gets a second textarea labeled "VARIAN B (opsional)" and a live A/B breakdown panel showing per-variant conversion%, with winner declared only when combined sample ≥30 visits (below that the noise dominates the signal — declaring a winner early would mislead). `pickHeroVariant` exported helper makes the bucketing testable. Booking row also snapshots which variant the converting visitor saw via `heroVariant` column — preferring the most-recent non-null in case admin paused the test mid-flight.
51. ✅ UTM attribution — `PaketView.utmSource/utmMedium/utmCampaign` columns (migration applied) capture campaign tags from `?utm_source=`/`?utm_medium=`/`?utm_campaign=` on first visit. **First-touch wins** — later visits within the same day are no-ops via the upsert update-no-op, and `getVisitorAttribution` pulls UTM from the oldest row. Booking also snapshots these so admin booking-detail and analytics queries can answer "which campaign drove this LUNAS". Admin overview gets a "Sumber kampanye (UTM)" panel grouping all paket × all visits by (source, medium, campaign) with visit / booking / conversion% columns. Direct/no-UTM bucket rendered italic to distinguish from real campaigns. Length-capped at field write (80/80/120 char) so a malformed URL can't blow up the column.
52. ✅ CTA A/B test — extends stage 50 hero A/B to the booking submit button text. New `Paket.ctaTextVariantA/B` columns (migration applied) carry the override text per variant. **Reuses heroVariant bucketing** so one A/B run tests both surfaces simultaneously per visitor — admin attribution gets cleaner read of "B converted better because of which copy". Both null → fall back to hardcoded "Kunci kursi saya →" so existing paket without test config don't suddenly read different copy. Waitlist label always wins when paket is full (variant text shouldn't override "Daftar waitlist"). Form-reset JS reads `data-cta-default` attr so error recovery keeps the bucketed variant visible.
53. ✅ Traffic anomaly alert — daily 08:30 email to OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS when a paket's yesterday visit count drops ≥50% vs 7-day rolling mean AND baseline ≥5 visits/day (so sleepy paket don't fire). New `TRAFFIC_ANOMALY_OWNER` notif type. CLI `npm run job:send-traffic-anomaly`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-traffic-anomaly`, cron daily 08:30 + systemd timer. **Silent when no anomalies** — quiet days don't generate noise. Email body suggests likely root causes (ads paused, landing broken, campaign expired, competitor outranked).
54. ✅ Jemaah cohort retention — `src/services/cohortRetention.js → getJemaahCohortRetention({months=12})` groups jemaah by month of first non-cancelled booking, computes % who had a 2nd non-cancelled booking within 365 days. Per-month table on admin overview shows cohort label / total jemaah / retained / retention% / mature flag. **Mature flag**: cohort is "mature" only when its end-of-month + 365 days < today (the 12-month window has fully elapsed). Immature cohorts render dimmed because their retention pct is still trending up. Header KPI averages across mature cohorts only (the only honest number). CANCELLED + REFUNDED excluded from cohort + retention math — those don't reflect a real customer relationship. PENDING/DP_PAID/LUNAS all count as a real second booking.
55. ✅ Cohort retention by acquisition channel — same service extended with `byChannel` rollup. `channelFor(booking)` resolves to `utm:<source>` when set, `agen:<slug>` when `agentSlugCap` is present, `direct` otherwise. Per-channel rollup across all cohorts in the window, filtered to channels with ≥5 jemaah (avoid showing volatile single-jemaah percentages alongside real channels). Sorted by total desc. Surfaced as a sub-table inside the cohort panel — admin sees which acquisition channel actually brings back repeat customers, not just which channel volume-wise dominates.
56. ✅ Landing speed budget — `PaketView.renderMs` column added; `/p/:slug` route measures end-to-end via `res.on('finish')` so the DB write is post-response (no added latency). `getLandingSpeed({days=7})` computes p50/p95/p99 globally + per-paket worst-5 by p95 (≥5-sample minimum for stable percentiles). Budget 800 ms — `overBudget=true` when global p95 crosses it, panel border turns ruby. `lowSample` flag when total < 50 visits in the window so admin knows the percentiles are still noisy. Repeat visits within a day overwrite `renderMs` so the metric reflects the latest experience; other fields stay first-touch. New `LANDING_SLOW_OWNER` enum (migration applied) reserved for a future alert job.
57. ✅ Auto-archive stale leads — wired into the existing weekly `prune` job (no new cron entry). `archiveStaleLeads(now, days=180)` soft-deletes COLD + LOST leads with `updatedAt < cutoff` by setting `deletedAt = now`. **WARM stays forever** (still workable — agent should follow up) and **CONVERTED stays forever** (booking history). Soft delete means rows survive in DB for retrospective queries; the agent's pipeline view already filters `deletedAt: null` so archived leads disappear from active CRM. Window tunable via `RETENTION_STALE_LEAD_DAYS` env var. Counts surface in the prune job's audit row.
58. ✅ Landing slow alert — wires the `LANDING_SLOW_OWNER` enum from S56. Daily 08:45 job `send-landing-slow` reads `getLandingSpeed` snapshot and emails ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — perf is engineering, not cashier) when **p95 > 800ms AND not lowSample**. Silent on healthy days OR when the sample is too small to be meaningful (lowSample). Body shows p50/p95/p99 + worst 5 paket by p95 + suggested root causes (DB query, large hero asset, CPU saturated, connection pool). CLI `npm run job:send-landing-slow`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-landing-slow`, cron + systemd timer 08:45 (after traffic-anomaly at 08:30).
59. ✅ Lead reactivation hint — on `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`, query soft-deleted leads matched by the jemaah's phone (last 8 digits, so country-code mismatches don't hide matches). Gold-bordered panel above the booking history shows up to 5 archived leads with `deletedAt` date + agent + last status + truncated notes. Surfaces prior CRM context that S57 auto-archive removed from the active pipeline. **No new endpoints** — pure read on the existing Lead table.
60. ✅ Paket-edit view sparkline — `getPaketDailyViews({paketId, days=30})` returns zero-filled per-day visit counts (so quiet days are visible dips, not x-axis collapses). Inline SVG sparkline (320×36 px) renders above the hero-title field on `/admin/paket/:slug/edit` with total + last-7d + week-over-week arrow. Hidden when total=0 (no signal to show). Admin sees traffic trend in the same field where they edit the copy that drives it — context for the A/B copy decisions in S50/S52.
61. ✅ ROI on cross-agen leaderboard — new `Paket.adsSpendIdr` + `adsNotes` columns (migration applied). `getPerPaketLeaderboard` now computes `roiX = lunasRevenue ÷ adsSpendIdr` (multiplier form, more intuitive than % for marketing teams) and `netPostAds = netMarginIdr − adsSpendIdr`. Renders as a third row below the cost/margin strip on each card, colour-coded (≥5× emerald / ≥3× gold / ≥1× amber / <1× ruby). **roiX=null when adsSpendIdr unset** — leaderboard renders "—" rather than "0×" to avoid misleading "no ads → infinite ROI" reading. Form on paket-edit uses the same 3-state preprocessor pattern as `costPerPaxIdr` so empty input persists as null.
62. ✅ Booking-detail audit timeline — replaced the flat list on `/admin/bookings/:id` with a vertical timeline grouped by category. `categorise()` view-side helper maps each audit row to `{created, money, cancel, notes, other}` with corresponding icon (●/$/✕/📝/•) and color (emerald/gold/ruby/sapphire/ink-100). Bullets sit on a connecting line; each event shows action + entity + time + actor email/role + a compact snapshot of changed fields (status, paid, method, kamar, cancel reason, merged fields, etc.). No service change — pure view reorganisation. Reads as a narrative instead of an undifferentiated list.
63. ✅ Public testimonial CRUD — new `Testimonial(paketId?, jemaahName, body, rating, photoUrl?, status, sortOrder)` model with `TestimonialStatus` enum DRAFT|PUBLISHED (migration applied). Admin CRUD at `/admin/testimonials` (list with status filter + new/edit/delete forms). Service validates min 10-char body + 2-char name. **Nullable paketId** lets admin author either paket-specific testimonials (shown on that paket's `/p/:slug` only) OR generic ones (shown on every paket). Public-side: `getPublishedTestimonialsForPaket(paketId)` returns PUBLISHED rows matching `paketId OR null`, rendered as cards between trust strip and FAQ on `/p/:slug`. Sidebar link in admin Tools group. No file upload baked in — admin pastes a path under `/uploads/testimonials/` for the photoUrl (the existing public uploads dir).
64. ✅ Testimonial KPI in conversion panel — `getPaketConversion` returns a `testimonialSplit` rollup grouping active paket into "with PUBLISHED testimonial" vs "without". Lift % shown when both buckets have ≥10 visits (sample size guard). **Generic testimonials count as "everyone has one"** — admins running a generic-only setup see no split (correct: there's no controlled variable). Two-cell strip with per-bucket conversionPct + paket count + visit/booking counts, rendered above the per-paket table on the admin conversion panel.
65. ✅ Per-crew (MUTHAWWIF) weekly digest — Monday 07:20 email per ACTIVE crew with their previous-week attendance activity (marks count / present / absent / paket touched) + upcoming paket assignments within 30 days. New `CREW_WEEKLY_DIGEST` notif type (migration applied). `recipientUserId` set so the row would scope correctly if a /crew/notifications inbox is added later. **Silent on idle weeks** — when both attendance count = 0 AND upcoming assignments = 0, the email doesn't fire. CLI `npm run job:send-crew-weekly-digest`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-crew-weekly-digest`, cron + jobRunner interval registered. Per-crew failures caught so a bad row doesn't abort the batch.
66. ✅ Public conversion modal — soft WA modal on `/p/:slug` fires once per visitor (24h localStorage cooldown). **Trigger**: scrolled past 80% of viewport AND idle 30s with no input (no scroll/touch/mousemove). WA-first because most Indonesian conversions land in chat first, form second. Pre-fills the message with paket title + agent name; defaults to office WA when no agent is resolved. CTA click also persists the dismiss key so a converted visitor doesn't see the modal on their next page within cooldown. Pure client-side — no backend changes, no DB writes, no analytics ping (intentional: this is a nudge, not a metric).
67. ✅ Crew weekly digest deltas — extends S65 with previous-week aggregation + delta arrows on each metric (mirrors S29/S33 for the OWNER digests). New `aggregateCrewWeek({userId, start, end})` helper used for current and previous windows in parallel. Polarity-aware: `absentCount` is reverse (more = bad), the rest forward. `fmtEmailDelta` from notifications.js reused so the visual style stays consistent across all weekly emails. Template gets `{{trend*}}` placeholders per metric.
68. ✅ Speed tier badge on leaderboard — `getPaketSpeedMap({days=7})` returns per-paket p95 latency map (single batched query). `getPerPaketLeaderboard` attaches `speedTier ∈ {fast, acceptable, slow, unknown}` per row based on the S56 800ms budget (fast ≤400 / acceptable ≤800 / slow >800). **Unknown when sample < 5** — admin sees nothing rather than a misleading badge. Renders as a small mono-font pill next to the revenue figure in each leaderboard card; title attr shows `p95 + sample` for hover details. Falls through gracefully when no PaketView rows have renderMs (pre-S56 dev DB).
69. ✅ Jemaah self-service testimonial submit — `GET/POST /saya/bookings/:id/testimonial` (jemaah only, owns booking, booking must be LUNAS — DP-only doesn't earn a public voice). Form lets jemaah pick rating (1–5 stars), write body (20–2000 chars), optional city. **Always lands DRAFT** — admin still controls what appears on /p/:slug. Re-submit policy: existing testimonial for (paketId × jemaahName) is updated in place + flipped back to DRAFT for re-review (mirrors S47 doc re-verify behaviour, prevents duplicate rows on form refresh). Audit row marks `selfSubmit: true` for grep. `/saya/bookings/:id` view shows a gold-bordered CTA when status=LUNAS and a green success banner after submit. 5 HTTP-integration tests cover the gates.
70. ✅ Testimonial published notif — new `Testimonial.submittedByUserId` FK (S69 + S70 migration) populated by the jemaah self-submit route. When admin's `updateTestimonial` flips DRAFT→PUBLISHED AND `submittedByUserId` is set AND the submitter is ACTIVE, fires a `TESTIMONIAL_PUBLISHED` EMAIL with `recipientUserId` set so the jemaah's `/saya/notifications` inbox + unread badge pick it up. **Fire-and-forget** — admin save never blocked by notif failure. Skips silently on admin-authored testimonials (null submittedByUserId) and on PUBLISHED→DRAFT (unpublish). New `TESTIMONIAL_PUBLISHED` enum.
71. ✅ Crew public profile page — `CrewProfile` extended with `slug` (unique, nullable), `titlePrefix` ("Ustadz", "H.", "KH."), `bio` (Text), `photoUrl`. Public route `/c/:slug` renders crew bio + upcoming-12-months assigned paket + last-4-months past paket. **Opt-out by default** — crew with no slug, no bio AND no photoUrl returns 404, so a muthawif who hasn't filled their profile isn't accidentally surfaced. `/p/:slug` landing pulls assigned crew with public slugs and shows a "Ditemani tim berpengalaman" strip with circular photo cards linking to the profile. Strip hidden when no crew has a public profile.
72. ✅ ICS calendar export — `GET /saya/bookings/:id/calendar.ics` returns a RFC 5545 VCALENDAR with one VEVENT (all-day DTSTART/DTEND covering departure→return, +1 day on DTEND per spec). DESCRIPTION carries booking ref + kelas + maskapai + route + deep link back to `/saya/bookings/:id`. Stable UID = `<bookingId>@religio-pro` so re-imports update the calendar event rather than duplicating. VALARM 3 days before departure for prep reminder. Special chars escaped per spec (`\;` `\,` `\\` `\n`); long lines folded at 70 chars with `CRLF + space`. Ownership enforced via `getMyBooking`'s `jemaahUserId` filter (404 on cross-user). Status-gated: cancelled/refunded bookings hide the CTA. "📅 + KALENDER" link sits next to "🖨 CETAK VOUCHER" in the booking detail crumb bar.
73. ✅ Admin crew profile editor — extends the existing /admin/users/:id/edit MUTHAWWIF panel with `crewSlug` + `crewTitlePrefix` + `crewBio` + `crewPhotoUrl` inputs. UserAdmin schema + service handle 3-state (undefined = no change, "" = clear → null, value = stored) so admin can wipe a public profile by clearing the slug. Slug lowercased on write; whitespace stripped. Hooks into the S71 `getCrewPublicProfile` opt-out rule — clearing all fields takes the crew off the public `/c/:slug` directory in one form save.
74. ✅ Public agen profile — `/a/:slug` mirror of S71 for `AgentProfile`. Added `AgentProfile.photoUrl` column (migration). Form panel extended with `agentPhotoUrl` + `igHandle` inputs. Public route + `agent-public.ejs` view renders bio + verified badge + stats (lifetime LUNAS count, active paket count, years with Religio Pro) + upcoming paket cards. **Three-condition opt-in**: profile must have `isVerified=true` AND active user AND (bio OR photoUrl). All paket links carry `?a=<slug>` so referral attribution flows back. WA + IG action buttons in hero.
75. ✅ First payment thanks — fires once per booking when the first PAID Payment row lands (counts prior PAID rows excluding the current one, == 0 means this is the first). Onboarding tone — "thanks + here's what's next" (doc checklist, manasik schedule, agen contact) — distinct from the neutral kuitansi `notifyPaymentReceived`. New `FIRST_PAYMENT_THANKS` enum (migration applied). `recipientUserId` set when booking is linked so the notif also shows in `/saya/notifications` with unread badge. Anonymous bookings still get the email but skip the inbox. Subsequent partial payments DP→PARTIAL→LUNAS don't re-trigger.
76. ✅ Public agen leaderboard — `GET /agen-leaderboard` lists top 10 verified agents by lifetime LUNAS count. Three-condition opt-in (`isVerified=true` AND active user AND bio OR photoUrl) so suspended/private agents don't surface. Stable sort by lunasCount desc then displayName. Rendered with rank badges (🥇🥈🥉 for top 3) + photo + tier + years active + lunas counter. Social proof for the network: links to /a/:slug for each row. Empty state shows when no verified agents qualify yet.
77. ✅ Email click tracking — new `EmailClick` model (`@@unique([notificationId, targetUrl])` so repeat clicks bump `clickCount` instead of duplicating rows). `lib/emailClickToken.js` signs URLs via HMAC-SHA256 of `(notifId, url)` truncated to 16 hex chars; `/r/<notifId>.<b64>.<sig>` redirects via constant-time-compare token verify. **Wrap happens inside `dispatchNotification`** for EMAIL channel only — body is mutated in-flight so the DB row stays unchanged (admin viewer shows original URLs). Conservative URL whitelist: absolute http(s) + root-absolute paths under known prefixes. mailto/tel/anchors pass through unwrapped. Open-redirect proof via the signature requirement. Pruning excluded — admin needs full history for arbitrary CTR windows.
78. ✅ WA fallback on email bounce — when EMAIL channel hits terminal FAILED (`nextRetryAt=null` after max 5 attempts) AND notif type is in the critical set (BOOKING_CREATED, PAYMENT_RECEIVED, BOOKING_LUNAS, REFUND_ISSUED, FIRST_PAYMENT_THANKS, PAYOUT_CREATED) AND `recipientPhone` is set, auto-enqueues a WA duplicate. Admin digests (DAILY/WEEKLY/CREW/etc.) deliberately excluded — those land in the queue dashboard if email bounces; bulk fallback would worsen UX. **Idempotent**: enqueue checks for an existing WA row with the same (recipientPhone, type, relatedEntity, relatedEntityId) to avoid double-firing on retried terminal failures. Payload carries `fallbackFromEmail: <emailNotifId>` for the audit trail. Best-effort — fallback failure never blocks the original failure recording.
79. ✅ Email CTR dashboard — `getEmailCtrByType()` in `src/services/emailCtr.js` joins Notification with the S77 EmailClick rows (`clicks: { some: {} }` predicate) and groups by notif type to report sent / clicked / CTR% per type. **`lowSample` flag when sent < 5** so the panel can dim noisy rows (one click on three sent = 33% CTR isn't actionable). Sorted by sent desc — types with the most volume bubble to top. Surfaced on `/admin` overview between needs-attention and S51 UTM panel. Read-only — admin uses it to spot dead templates (DAILY_DIGEST_OWNER with 0% CTR over 90 days = nobody opens the email link).
80. ✅ SOS auto-escalate — `Incident.escalatedAt` column + new `escalateStaleIncidents({olderThanMin=60})` service. Cron `*/15 * * * *` finds OPEN incidents older than 60min with `escalatedAt=null`, EMAILs only OWNER tier (tighter than stage 13's initial OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS fan-out — assumes admin desk missed the first alert), then stamps `escalatedAt` so the next run skips the row. **`escalatedAt` is set-once** — ACK/RESOLVE never clear it; re-escalation isn't a thing. New `INCIDENT_ESCALATED` enum + template. CLI `npm run job:send-incident-escalate` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-incident-escalate` + systemd timer + jobRunner interval (15 min). The state machine still flows OPEN → ACKED → RESOLVED — escalation is orthogonal, just a louder ping.
81. ✅ Booking note @-mentions — `updateBookingNotes` parses `@email@domain` tokens out of the notes text and fires `BOOKING_NOTE_MENTION` EMAIL to matching ACTIVE users. **Diff by-email, not by-token-position** — adding context around an existing mention doesn't re-fire ("@cs@religio.pro" already in old notes → present in new notes → no notif). New mentions only. Self-mentions filtered (actor's own email skipped). Unknown emails silently no-op (no enqueue for typos). `recipientUserId` set so if the mentioned user has a `/saya` inbox they see it. Mention parser exported as `extractMentionEmails` for future inline-highlight surfaces. Hint text added to the admin notes textarea: `@email@domain untuk mention`.
82. ✅ Mention autocomplete — typing `@` in the booking notes textarea triggers a dropdown of matching ACTIVE staff. `GET /admin/bookings/mention-search?q=<2+ chars>` returns up to 10 (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS/KASIR/SALES) — AGEN/MUTHAWWIF/JEMAAH excluded since the @-mention surface is staff-only. **Min 2 chars** to prevent full-table scans from backspace hammering. Same RBAC as notes-edit (CANCEL_ROLES — KASIR can't edit notes so they don't get the dropdown either). Pure browser JS, no framework: ArrowUp/Down to navigate, Enter/Tab to commit, Escape closes. Inserts `@email@domain ` at the trigger position so the existing S81 mention parser picks it up unchanged.
83. ✅ Incident response SLA report — `src/services/incidentSla.js → getIncidentSlaReport({weeks=8})` aggregates Incident rows per Mon-Sun cohort (created in that week) with ack/resolve p50+p95 latency + escalation rate. Panel above the queue on `/admin/incidents`. **Cohorting is by `createdAt` week**, not `resolvedAt` — the question is "how responsive were we to incidents that arrived in week X". Open-but-aging rows count toward `created` (denominator) but NOT toward the percentile pool — mixing nulls would distort latencies. **`escalationRatePct=null` when created=0** (no divide-by-zero). Current week excluded — it's still accumulating. Uses `localYmd` helper (not `toISOString().slice(0,10)`) to avoid the TZ-truncation bug that bit the daily digest.
84. ✅ Email click heatmap — `getEmailClickHeatmap({type, days=30})` joins EmailClick → Notification (filtered by `type` + `sentAt`) and aggregates per **normalised URL** (scheme + host stripped via `new URL()`, path+query kept). Lets `https://prod/admin?tab=ops` and `http://localhost:3001/admin?tab=ops` collapse to one row so dev + prod don't fragment the data. Sorted by clicks desc + `sharePct` per URL. Drill-down view at `/admin/email-ctr/:type` — accessed by clicking a type row in the S79 panel (link only rendered when `clicked > 0`). **Defensive against unknown enum**: bookmarked-but-since-renamed type returns empty rows instead of 500 (Prisma's enum rejection caught + downgraded).
85. ✅ WA click tracking — S77's `/r/<token>` redirect was always channel-agnostic; the gap was that `dispatchNotification` only wrapped EMAIL bodies. S85 extends the wrap to WA. `wrapUrl` now prepends `PUBLIC_BASE_URL` when configured (required for WA — chat clients only auto-detect absolute http(s) URLs); without the env it falls back to a path which is fine for HTML email but silently no-op for WA. `getEmailCtrByType` groups by `(type, channel)` so the CTR panel shows EMAIL + WA side-by-side. `getEmailClickHeatmap` accepts optional `channel` query so the drill-down can lens to one channel or combine both. EmailClick model name kept (not renamed to MessageClick) — the click semantics are channel-agnostic and a rename would invalidate every existing row without functional benefit.
86. ✅ Notes mention history — `BookingMention(bookingId, userEmail, userId, mentionedById, mentionedByEmail, createdAt)` denormalised table (migration applied) populated by `notifyBookingNoteMention` alongside the EMAIL fan-out. Indexed by `(userEmail, createdAt)` for fast per-user lookups. Surfaced on `/admin` overview as "Anda di-mention" panel showing the viewer's last 30 days of mentions with deep links to each booking + age + actor email. **Best-effort insertion** — failure to write the BookingMention row never blocks the notif enqueue (the notif is the load-bearing signal; the index is convenience). Why denormalised over querying Notification queue: S14 retention prunes notif rows, the inbox-style surface needs a separate persistence layer.
87. ✅ Incident SLA targets + alerts — `src/services/incidentSlaAlert.js → SLA_BUDGETS` constants per IncidentType (SOS ack 5min/resolve 30min, MEDICAL 15min/1h, LOST_JEMAAH 30min/4h, SECURITY 1h/24h, LOGISTICAL+OTHER 2h/48h). `getIncidentSlaBreaches({minSample=3})` runs over the previous full Mon-Sun week, returns one row per (type, metric) where p95 > budget. **Skips low-sample types** — fewer than 3 incidents can't make a statistical claim. **Silent on healthy weeks** — no breach = no email. `notifyIncidentSlaBreach` fans out to OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded). New `INCIDENT_SLA_BREACH_OWNER` enum (migration applied). Cron Mon 07:25 (after the OWNER digest sequence). Budgets are code constants (not DB) — there's one correct set per role/operation, not a per-admin tweak surface.
88. ✅ Mention shortcodes — `MentionShortcode(code, userId)` table (migration applied) maps short tokens like `:cs` → a staff user. Expansion happens at save in `updateBookingNotes` BEFORE the S81 parser runs, so stored notes carry the full `@user.email` and the existing diff-by-email + audit flow is unchanged. **Unknown codes left as-is** (admin typo visible, not silently dropped). **Codes targeting suspended/deleted users skip expansion** — the code stays as `:cs` so admins notice the stale link instead of mentioning the wrong person. Admin CRUD at `/admin/users/shortcodes` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN). Autocomplete extended: `:` triggers `/admin/bookings/shortcode-search` (min 1 char), `@` continues to fetch staff (min 2 chars). Codes lowercased + validated `[a-z0-9_-]{1,40}`.
89. ✅ Incident timeline UI — view-only enhancement on `/admin/incidents/:id`. Each leg shows elapsed time (`+10m`) and the budget reference (`/ budget 5m`); breached legs flip ruby + bold. Added visual SLA bar above the timeline: emerald/amber/ruby track shows current age vs `slaBudget.resolveMs`, with gold marker lines at the ack budget and resolve budget. Includes pending-state rows ("⏱ belum di-ack — sudah 20m melewati budget 5m") when an OPEN/ACKED incident is past its budget without the next state transition. Escalation event (S80) gets its own timeline row. Route resolves `SLA_BUDGETS[incident.type]` from S87 and passes to the view.
90. ✅ WA consent audit trail — `JemaahProfile.notifWaConsentAt` + `notifWaWithdrawnAt` columns (migration applied; **no backfill** — old profiles keep null because stamping NOW() would be a dishonest "consented just now" claim). Register flow stamps `consentAt = now` so new accounts have an authoritative first-opt-in date. `updateJemaah` watches for `notifWa` flips: opt-out → stamps `withdrawnAt`; opt-in → stamps `consentAt` AND keeps the last `withdrawnAt` (durable history). No-op + omitted-field paths leave both timestamps alone. Surfaced on jemaah self-profile + admin jemaah-form. Useful when a jemaah complains "I never agreed to WhatsApp" — the timestamp + register-flow tie shows otherwise.
91. ✅ Mention-driven follow-up tasks — `Task(bookingId, assigneeEmail, body, dueAt, status)` + `TaskStatus` enum (migration applied). Parser `extractTodos` reads `@email TODO body [by YYYY-MM-DD]` from notes and `upsertTodosForBooking` creates Task rows alongside the S81 mention fan-out. **Idempotent on (bookingId, email, body)** — re-saving same notes creates no duplicates. Date parsing limited to explicit `by YYYY-MM-DD` (NLP is brittle); malformed dates → dueAt null. "Tugas saya" panel on `/admin` overview lists OPEN tasks for the viewer's email, overdue first, with one-click DONE/CANCEL forms. POST `/admin/tasks/:id/complete` + `/cancel` — any 4 admin roles can clear queues for each other; `completedByEmail` records who did it.
92. ✅ Per-paket cost vendor breakdown — `PaketCostLine(category, amountIdr, vendorNote, sortOrder)` + `CostCategory` enum (HOTEL/FLIGHT/VISA/MEALS/GROUND_OPS/GUIDE/INSURANCE/OTHER; migration applied). When at least one line exists, the auto-sync trigger writes `SUM(lines)` back to `Paket.costPerPaxIdr` so the leaderboard margin math (S22) keeps working unchanged. **Deleting the LAST line does NOT clear the column** — preserves the prior sum as a manual estimate fallback (admin who deletes all lines didn't necessarily want margin to disappear). JSON CRUD at `/api/paket/:slug/cost-lines`. Cross-paket per-category rollup helper for future leaderboard insight. Inline JSON-driven panel on paket-edit lets admin add/delete lines without leaving the page.
93. ✅ PWA push for jemaah — extends S17 admin web-push to JEMAAH role. New `pushToUser(userId, payload)` mirrors `pushToAdmins` but scoped by userId. Jemaah subscribe surface at `/api/saya/push/{config,subscribe,unsubscribe}` (parallel to `/api/admin/push`). `notifyBookingCreated` + `notifyPaymentReceived` now fire push to the jemaah's installed `/saya` PWA when subscribed. **Best-effort** — push failure never blocks the EMAIL/WA queue writes (those remain load-bearing). **`pushToAdmins` still excludes jemaah** via the role filter in the WHERE clause — same PushSubscription table, role-based selection per fan-out kind. Silent when jemaah hasn't installed the PWA / disabled notifications.
94. ✅ Jemaah PWA subscribe UI — `shared/push-jemaah.js` mirrors `push-admin.js` against the `/api/saya/push/*` endpoints. Toggle bar on `/saya` dashboard (icon + status text + AKTIFKAN/MATIKAN buttons) auto-paints based on `Notification.permission` + current `PushManager` subscription. Browser-not-supported / permission-denied paths render an explanatory line + hide the buttons (no broken-button confusion). Same DOM contract as admin (`#rp-push-{bar,status,enable,disable}`) so styling can be reused. HTTP integration tests cover auth gating + payload validation.
95. ✅ Per-category cost benchmarks — `getCostBenchmarks({paketId})` compares this paket's per-category total spend (from S92's lines) against the network median across non-archived paket. Flags 'high' when amount ≥ 2× median, 'low' when ≤ 0.5×, null when within range. **Sample guard**: skips flag when fewer than 3 peer paket in the category — too few to make a statistical claim. **Aggregates per (paketId × category)** before computing median so multi-line paket (Hotel Madinah/Mekkah/Aqsa as 3 rows) compare apples-to-apples with single-line paket. Surfaced as a gold-bordered warning strip above the lines panel on paket-edit; only renders when ≥1 flag exists. Median (not mean) so a single outlier doesn't drag the benchmark for everyone.
96. ✅ Task SLA escalation — `getOverdueTasks({graceHours=48})` finds OPEN tasks past `dueAt + grace`. Daily cron at 09:00 fans `TASK_OVERDUE_ESCALATION` EMAIL to OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — task workflow is ops, not cashier). **7-day per-recipient cooldown**: notif dedup query checks if same admin email got the same notif type within last 7 days; if so, skip enqueue. Avoids inbox spam on long-stuck tasks while still surfacing them weekly. Silent on healthy days (zero overdue → zero email). New `TASK_OVERDUE_ESCALATION` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-task-overdue` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-task-overdue` + systemd timer + jobRunner interval.
97. ✅ Push debug page — `/admin/push-debug` lists every PushSubscription (admin + jemaah) with user, role, user-agent, endpoint preview, lastUsedAt, and a per-row "TES KIRIM" button. `listAllPushSubscriptionsForDebug` flags subs owned by suspended/deleted users as stale (dimmed in the table). `sendTestPushToSubscription(subId)` reuses the same `sendOne` path as production fan-outs so a successful test confirms VAPID config + the SW push handler end-to-end. Page header shows current push mode (web-push vs fake) + whether `VAPID_PUBLIC` is configured. Closes the observability gap: previously a stale subscription was invisible until "nobody got the alert" was reported.
98. ✅ Booking activity feed — `getBookingActivityFeed(bookingId, {limit=150})` merges AuditLog, Payment, Komisi, BookingMention, Task, Notification, JemaahDocument, AttendanceMark rows into one chronological feed (newest first). Renders as a unified vertical timeline above the audit-only timeline on `/admin/bookings/:id`. Per-row kind badge color-codes the source. Each kind has a one-line `label` (e.g. "Pembayaran PAID · Rp 5jt · TRANSFER", "Task → @cs: verify passport"). **Bounded at 150 rows** so the page doesn't blow up on long-lived bookings; deep history still lives in `/admin/audit`. Best-effort render — feed failure is logged but the booking detail still loads from the existing panels.
99. ✅ Agent commission forecast — `getAgentCommissionForecast({agentId, windowDays=90})` projects expected komisi from non-LUNAS active bookings using `total × rate × statusProbability` where probability is PENDING 30% / BOOKED 50% / DP_PAID 70% / PARTIAL 85% (LUNAS excluded — has a real Komisi row). Rate chain mirrors `payment.js` S22 (matrix > agent override > paket rate > DEFAULT). Returns per-month buckets + per-status breakdown + total. Surfaces as a gold-bordered "Proyeksi komisi" panel on `/agen` Wallet tab when an agent has any non-LUNAS active booking. Helps agents plan; pairs with S37 payout reminder for the admin side. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded — undone commitment, not pipeline.
100. ✅ Cross-agent komisi forecast — `getAllAgentsCommissionForecast({windowDays=90})` rolls up S99 across every ACTIVE agent. Returns `perAgent` (sorted by expected desc), `perMonth` (chronological + unscheduled last), and grand totals. Panel on `/admin` overview shows top 10 agents + per-month buckets side-by-side so OWNER can plan cash-flow outflow. Agents with zero active bookings skipped (only those with pipeline contribution appear). Sequential per-agent fetch — fine at typical scale (≤50 agents), revisit if it grows.
101. ✅ Voucher PDF download — `pdfkit` (~100KB pure-JS, no Chromium) renders a programmatic A4 voucher with header / jemaah / perjalanan / pembayaran / agen / itinerary blocks. `streamVoucherPdf(voucher, res)` pipes directly to the HTTP response with `Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="voucher_<bookingNo>.pdf"`. Filename sanitised — `[^A-Za-z0-9_-]` stripped so no path traversal even if `bookingNo` is corrupted. Routes: `GET /admin/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf` (4 admin VIEW roles) + `GET /saya/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf` (jemaah, scoped via `jemaahUserId`). CTA: "⇩ PDF" button next to existing "🖨 CETAK" on both detail pages. **Why pdfkit not playwright/puppeteer**: no native Chromium binary, no manual `playwright install`, no 2-3s cold start.
102. ✅ Inactive jemaah prune — `pruneInactiveJemaah` (wired into the weekly S14 prune) soft-deletes JEMAAH users that meet ALL: role=JEMAAH, deletedAt=null, createdAt < cutoff, lastLoginAt < cutoff OR null, AND `bookings: { none: { status: notIn [CANCELLED, REFUNDED] } }`. Bookings FK is SetNull on User delete so any historical paid bookings keep their `JemaahProfile` link (the profile is the customer record; the user row is just the login). Default 365 days; tunable via `RETENTION_INACTIVE_JEMAAH_DAYS`. CANCELLED-only history doesn't save the account (no real customer relationship). OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS/KASIR/AGEN/MUTHAWWIF excluded by role gate.
103. ✅ Voucher PDF branding + i18n — header is now a centered ornamental brand mark with gold rule + diamond divider; footer has gold-rule + per-locale blessing line + fineprint. `?lang=id|en|ar` query (default `id`) flips section labels + footer through a `LANGS` table. **Arabic is romanised** ('AL-HAAJ', 'Baarakallahu fiikum…') — embedding Amiri TTF (~400KB) would dwarf the rest of the repo for marginal voucher benefit; if real Arabic glyphs become hard-required later, register a font via `doc.registerFont`. Unknown lang falls back to `id`. Filename suffix `_en` / `_ar` so admin can save multiple variants without overwrite. Booking detail page gets an `ID/EN/AR` dropdown next to the PDF button.
104. ✅ Soft-deleted users viewer — `listUsers` extended with `deleted: 'ACTIVE'|'DELETED'|'ALL'` (default ACTIVE — no behaviour change for existing callers). `/admin/users?deleted=DELETED` surfaces what S102 (and admin manual deletes) removed. Rows render dimmed with ruby `[DELETED]` tag; the action column shows the `deletedAt` date + a `RESTORE` form that POSTs to `/admin/users/:id/restore`. `restoreUser` is idempotent (no-op + no audit on already-active rows) and writes a labelled audit row (`after.restored = true`) when it does flip.
105. ✅ Booking export bundle — `GET /admin/bookings/:id/bundle.zip` packages `voucher.pdf` (S101) + `calendar.ics` (S72) + each jemaah document under `docs/<doc-id>__<sanitized-name>.<ext>` + a human-readable `MANIFEST.txt` listing what's inside. Streamed directly via `archiver` v8 (ZipArchive) — no temp file on disk; pdfkit pipes into a PassThrough shim that archiver consumes. **Missing files on disk are logged in MANIFEST under "NOT INCLUDED" rather than aborting the zip** — partial bundles are more useful than no bundle. Filename sanitised against path traversal. New `archiver` dep (pure ESM). "📦 BUNDLE" CTA on admin booking detail crumb.
106. ✅ CSV export in bundle — `?format=csv` query on `bundle.zip` swaps `voucher.pdf` for three CSVs: `booking.csv` (1 row of booking + jemaah + paket + totals), `payments.csv` (full payment history), `docs.csv` (doc metadata regardless of file presence). All CSVs are UTF-8 BOM-prefixed so Excel auto-detects encoding; RFC 4180 quoting. `calendar.ics` is dropped in CSV mode (accounting flow ≠ calendar import). Filename suffix `_csv.zip` so admin can keep both variants side-by-side. MANIFEST.txt reflects format in its title.
107. ✅ Bulk dossier export from manifest — `POST /admin/manifest/:slug/bundles.zip` with form-encoded `bookingIds[]` checkboxes packages each selected booking under `bookings/<bookingNo>/` (voucher.pdf + calendar.ics + docs/ — or CSVs when `?format=csv`). Cross-booking `BUNDLES_MANIFEST.txt` at the zip root lists who's included. **Per-booking shape mirrors single-bundle exactly** so a vendor handed one subfolder gets a standalone dossier. Capped at 200 bookings per request to avoid runaway zips. Per-booking lookup failure is logged + skipped, not fatal.
108. ✅ Outbound webhooks — `Webhook(url, secret, events[], status)` model (migration applied) + `dispatchEvent(name, payload)` service. Six canonical events: `booking.created`, `booking.lunas`, `booking.cancelled`, `payment.received`, `refund.issued`, `komisi.payout`. Each subscription gets a 32-byte hex secret; payload is HMAC-SHA256 signed and sent via `X-Religio-Signature: sha256=<hex>` header so partners can verify authenticity. **Per-row 8s timeout via AbortController** so a slow partner doesn't tie up the caller. Admin CRUD at `/admin/webhooks` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN). Wired into `createBooking`, `recordPayment` (payment.received + booking.lunas on transition), `issueRefund`.
109. ✅ Webhook delivery log + retry — `WebhookDelivery(webhookId, event, payload, signature, status, attemptCount, nextRetryAt)` model (migration applied). Each `dispatchEvent` call now inserts a pre-attempt row, fires once, then either marks SUCCEEDED or queues PENDING with backoff 1m/5m/30m/2h/12h (mirrors notif retry S77). **Payload + signature stored verbatim** so a retry re-uses the SAME signature the original used — receivers comparing a timestamp inside the body don't see drift on retry. `processPendingDeliveries` (CLI `npm run job:retry-webhooks` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/retry-webhooks` + cron every 2 min) picks PENDING rows whose nextRetryAt elapsed and re-fires. **SUSPENDED subs are skipped without burning a retry**. After 5 attempts the row is terminal FAILED. Per-webhook `LOG` link opens `/admin/webhooks/:id/deliveries`.
110. ✅ Manifest bulk-select UI — wires S107's `POST /admin/manifest/:slug/bundles.zip` into the Manifest tab. Checkbox column + select-all master (indeterminate when partial) + floating gold-bordered action bar at the bottom (hidden until ≥1 row checked) with "⇩ PDF dossier" / "⇩ CSV dossier" / "×" clear. Pure browser JS — no service change. Today the bulk endpoint goes from "exists but unreachable from UI" to "one click per dossier set".
111. ✅ Inbound webhooks — `POST /api/webhook-in/:source` accepts signed partner payloads (Fonnte delivery receipts, Zapier triggers, generic). `InboundWebhook(source, headers, payload, signatureValid, status)` model (migration applied) records every hit regardless of validity — failed-signature attempts stored as REJECTED for audit. Per-source verifier registry reads secrets from env (`WEBHOOK_IN_<SOURCE>_SECRET`) so rotation is ops-only. **No verifier configured = accept-anything dev mode** (signatureValid=null, status=RECEIVED). Per-source handler registry runs AFTER persistence; handler failure stamps `HANDLER_ERROR` for replay. Only `x-*` + content-type + user-agent headers kept (cookies/auth stripped). Admin viewer at `/admin/inbound-webhooks` with source+status filter + per-row REPLAY button. CSRF skip added for `/api/webhook-in/`.
112. ✅ Fonnte delivery handler — wired into S111's HANDLERS map. Match-by-phone strategy (no provider message id is stored): latest WA Notification with same `recipientPhone` (normalised — strip non-digits, leading 0 → 62), status=SENT, sentAt within last 24h. On status=failed → flip Notification.status to FAILED + stamp reason + clear nextRetryAt (message left our side; downstream failure, not worth re-queuing). On status=delivered/read → leave SENT + annotate `payload.fonnteDelivery` so the admin viewer can see receiver-side state. Silent on no match (late receipt for an older message → harmless).
113. ✅ API key auth — `ApiKey(name, hashedKey, scopes JSON, status)` model (migration applied) for partner-facing read APIs. Token format `rp_<id>.<secret>` where id is the cuid (non-secret, drives O(1) lookup) and secret is 32-byte hex bcrypt-hashed. Plaintext shown ONCE at creation. `requireApiScope('read:bookings')` middleware: 401 on bad/missing token, 403 on scope miss, attaches `req.apiKey` on success + stamps `lastUsedAt` fire-and-forget. SUSPENDED keys fail auth without deletion (rotation-friendly). Admin CRUD at `/admin/api-keys` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN). Three scopes today: `read:bookings`, `read:paket`, `read:notifs`.
114. ✅ Partner booking export API — `/api/v1/bookings`, `/api/v1/bookings/:id`, `/api/v1/paket`. Gated by S113 API key with respective scopes. List endpoint supports `?from=&to=&status=&page=&limit=` (cap 100, default 50). Returns paginated `{data, pagination, filters}` envelope with same field naming as the CSV bundle (S106). Single-booking endpoint adds `payments[]` inline. Versioned `/v1/` prefix so future breaking changes ship under `/v2`. CSRF skip added for `/api/v1/` (Bearer auth, no cookies).
115. ✅ API key rate limiting — `ApiKey.rateLimitPerMin` column (default 60, clamped 1..6000). `apiKeyRateLimit` middleware (mounted AFTER `requireApiScope`) reuses the shared S2 rate-limit store (in-memory or Redis depending on `REDIS_URL`) so per-key buckets share infra with the human-side limiter. Per-key bucket key = `apikey:<id>`. 429 with `Retry-After` + `X-RateLimit-Limit`/`-Remaining`/`-Reset` headers; under-limit calls populate the same headers so well-behaved clients can pace. **Fail-open on store errors** (Redis blip doesn't lock partners out). New `getRateLimitStore()` export from the middleware lets other limiters share the singleton.
116. ✅ OpenAPI spec for /api/v1 — `GET /api/v1/openapi.json` returns a hand-written OpenAPI 3.1 spec covering all three v1 endpoints (paths, parameters, response schemas, security with Bearer + per-endpoint scopes). `GET /api/v1/docs` serves a Swagger-UI HTML bootstrapper that pulls the bundle from a CDN. Both unauthenticated — discovery surface; partners need the spec to know how to authenticate. Spec auto-fills `servers[]` from `PUBLIC_BASE_URL` env or the request's `X-Forwarded-Host` / `Host`. Hand-written (not reflected from code) so accuracy stays a public contract — three endpoints make this the right cost/benefit.
117. ✅ Webhook test-fire — admin button on `/admin/webhooks` row + `POST /admin/webhooks/:id/test-fire` posts a synthetic signed event payload (`test.ping` by default; six sample shapes registered per canonical event name) to the partner URL. Renders HTTP response (status + first 500 chars of body + duration) inline as a result page. **Does NOT insert a WebhookDelivery row + does NOT bump lastFiredAt** — manual probe kept out of diagnostic surfaces. Adds `X-Religio-Test: true` header so partners can short-circuit logging. Closes the "did the partner actually receive my webhook?" gap during onboarding.
118. ✅ Webhook secret rotation — `POST /admin/webhooks/:id/rotate-secret` mints a fresh secret + archives the previous one as `prevSecret` with a `prevSecretExpiresAt` (default 24h, clamp 1..168). During the grace window every outbound POST carries BOTH `X-Religio-Signature` (new) and `X-Religio-Signature-Prev` (old) so partners can verify against either while they roll their config. New plaintext shown ONCE via query-flash; admin row shows an amber ROTATING badge with the grace expiry. Cleaner than "delete + recreate" which would break the integration mid-flight. Migration applied: `Webhook.prevSecret + prevSecretExpiresAt`.
119. ✅ Idempotency-Key on webhooks — `attemptDelivery` now sets `Idempotency-Key: <WebhookDelivery.id>` on every POST. Retries reuse the SAME header value (since the delivery row id is stable across attempts), so partners can dedupe replays that arrive after their endpoint actually succeeded but timed out responding. Industry-standard pattern from Stripe. No schema change — leverages S109's existing delivery row id.
120. ✅ Partner audit log API — `GET /api/v1/audit?entity=&entityId=&page=&limit=` returns paginated AuditLog rows scoped to one entity. New `read:audit` scope (added to `KNOWN_SCOPES`). 400 when entity/entityId missing — keeping payloads bounded by requiring caller to name the resource. Lets partner CRMs surface "who changed what" inline without raw DB access. OpenAPI spec updated.
121. ✅ API request log + per-key analytics — `ApiRequestLog(apiKeyId, path, method, statusCode, durationMs, scope, ip, ts)` model (migration applied). `apiRequestLog` middleware mounted at TOP of `/api/v1` (before auth) so failing-auth requests also leave a trail. Fire-and-forget via `res.on('finish')` — log write failures never block the request. `getApiKeyAnalytics({days=7})` rolls up per-key: requests / 5xx count + rate / p50+p95 duration / top 5 paths. Surfaces on `/admin/api-keys` as the top panel for keys with traffic. Pruned by weekly retention (60d default; tunable via `RETENTION_API_REQUEST_LOG_DAYS`).
122. ✅ Scope-use audit on token use — `ApiRequestLog.scope` column captures the scope each route required (`requireApiScope` stashes it as `req.apiUsedScope`). Analytics panel splits per-key usage into "scope used" (emerald pills with count) + "granted but unused" (ruby pills marked ⤬). Compliance + scope-down workflow: admin can see partner X has `read:audit` permission but only ever calls `read:bookings` → safe to revoke the unused scope without breaking their integration.
123. ✅ OpenAPI codegen check — `npm run check:openapi-sdk` runs `buildOpenApiSpec()` through `openapi-typescript` to generate a `.d.ts` of operation + schema types, then `tsc --noEmit` against a smoke `.ts` that references the key types (Booking shape, Pagination, all 4 paths). Any spec drift that breaks a partner-side codegen (renamed field, dropped endpoint) → tsc error → exit 1 → catches breaking change pre-merge. **Programmatic codegen via JS API** rather than the CLI binary — the CLI choked on spaces in our local dev path. tsc runs with `cwd=tmpDir` + relative project arg for the same reason. Two devDeps added: `openapi-typescript`, `typescript`.
124. ✅ API key scope-down digest — weekly Monday 07:23 cron mails OWNER+SUPERADMIN listing ACTIVE API keys that have ≥1 granted scope which produced ZERO ApiRequestLog rows in the last 30d (AND ≥1 request total — abandoned keys are a separate problem). Silent on healthy weeks. New `API_KEY_SCOPE_DOWN_OWNER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-api-scope-down`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-api-scope-down`, jobRunner interval registered.
125. ✅ Rate-limit headers on human routes — the shared `rateLimit` middleware now sets `X-RateLimit-Limit/Remaining/Reset` on every response (under-limit AND 429) + `Retry-After` on 429. Same header set as the partner API (S115) so docs + monitoring share one convention. Login/register get the headers for free. Defensive `setHeader` so test fixtures with plain-object res don't crash production-shaped code.
126. ✅ Webhook delivery replay — `POST /admin/webhooks/:id/deliveries/:deliveryId/replay` re-fires a stored delivery immediately via `attemptDelivery`. Re-uses the persisted payload + signature so partner sees identical bytes (no clock drift on retry). Bumps attemptCount like cron retries do — manual replay still counts toward the 5-attempt cap. Refuses on SUSPENDED webhook + max-attempts-reached + missing-row with friendly reason codes. Per-row `↻ REPLAY` button on `/admin/webhooks/:id/deliveries`; row replaces button with "max attempts" pill when terminal.
127. ✅ Webhook event expansion (ops events) — added 4 finer-grained events to `EVENT_NAMES` so partners can subscribe to operational lifecycle without re-deriving it from the money events: `booking.status_changed` (every forward transition — fires from both `cancelBooking` and `recordPayment` on any partial → DP_PAID/PARTIAL/LUNAS leg), `booking.notes_updated` (with first-400-char `notesPreview` + `actorEmail`), `incident.created` (with crew identity + paket + location), `incident.resolved` (with `resolution` + `resolvedByEmail`). **`booking.cancelled` still fires alongside `booking.status_changed` on cancel** — partners on legacy subscriptions don't break, new partners can pick the generic one and skip the specific. The no-op short-circuit in `updateBookingNotes` means re-saving identical notes doesn't fire `booking.notes_updated` (mirrors the audit-log skip-on-no-op rule). Test-fire `samples` extended with shapes for all four so admin can probe them from `/admin/webhooks`.
