128. ✅ Per-paket webhook subscription filter — `Webhook.paketId` nullable FK (migration applied) lets admin scope a subscription to ONE paket. `dispatchEvent` filters subs by `(s.paketId == null OR s.paketId === payload.paketId)`. **Global subs (paketId=null) keep receiving every event** — fully back-compat with pre-S128 rows. **Paket-scoped subs skip events that lack `paketId` in the payload** — the dispatcher can't infer scope from "untagged" events (e.g. `test.ping`), so refusing to deliver is safer than guessing. Every existing dispatch site updated to include `paketId` in the payload: `booking.created` (booking.js), `payment.received`/`booking.lunas` (payment.js), `refund.issued` (refund.js); `booking.cancelled`/`booking.status_changed` already had it. Admin form gets a "Filter per paket (opsional)" dropdown listing non-archived non-soft-deleted paket; row table shows a gold `🎯 PAKET: <slug>` pill when scoped. `createWebhook` validates the paketId exists before insert (BAD_PAKET 400) rather than letting FK opaque-fail.
129. ✅ Webhook delivery health digest — `src/services/webhookHealthDigest.js → getWebhookHealthDigest({days=7})` builds per-webhook health snapshot from `WebhookDelivery` rows in the window: `{total, succeeded, failed, pending, stuckPending, successRatePct, topError, attemptInflation}`. **Success rate only counts terminal rows** (SUCCEEDED+FAILED) — pending is "we don't know yet" and counting it as either would skew the read. **Stuck pending = PENDING > 1h old** (most retry cycles complete by then; lingering rows usually mean partner endpoint is down). **attemptInflation = total attempts / row count** — values >1 flag partners that need retries to succeed. Rows sorted worst-first. Weekly cron Monday 07:30 fans `WEBHOOK_HEALTH_OWNER` EMAIL to ACTIVE OWNER+SUPERADMIN (MANAJER_OPS/KASIR excluded — webhook config is a partner-integration concern, same RBAC as `/admin/webhooks`). **Silent when nothing is unhealthy** — quiet weeks generate no email. **Latency tracking deferred** — `WebhookDelivery` doesn't carry `durationMs` today; the simpler "X% delivered + top error" signal covers the actionable cases without a migration. New `WEBHOOK_HEALTH_OWNER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-webhook-health`, HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-webhook-health`, jobRunner interval registered so `/api/health` flags a missing run.
130. ✅ Inbound webhook replay gate — replay was previously offered on every row regardless of state, which double-fired side effects (HANDLED) or pretended to "revalidate" bad-signature rows (REJECTED). New `canReplayInbound({status, source})` only allows replay when status=HANDLER_ERROR AND a handler is currently registered. Refusal reasons surface explicitly: `already_succeeded` (HANDLED), `bad_signature` (REJECTED), `no_action_needed` (RECEIVED — passive source with nothing to run), `no_handler_for_source` (handler was removed since the failure — degenerate but reachable). Admin view computes the gate per-row server-side: actionable rows get the `↻ REPLAY` button, non-actionable rows render a muted reason hint (`✓ done` / `bad sig` / `passive` / `no handler`) so admin understands why no button. Flash messages localised to Bahasa Indonesia per refusal code. **No new endpoint** — same `POST /admin/inbound-webhooks/:id/replay`, just tighter pre-conditions. The S111 `no_handler_for_source` reason is now reachable only when status=HANDLER_ERROR (status gate runs first); the existing test for that path updated to assert the new `no_action_needed` behavior on RECEIVED rows.
131. ✅ Per-subscription webhook burst rate-limit — `Webhook.rateLimitPerMin` column (default 30, clamp 1..600; migration applied). `dispatchEvent` runs `checkRateLimit` per matched sub against the shared S2/S115 rate-limit store (`webhook:<id>` bucket key, 60s window). Over-quota events DON'T fire the HTTP POST — instead the `WebhookDelivery` row is created with `status=PENDING`, `nextRetryAt = end-of-window`, and `lastError='rate_limited (>N/min)'`. The retry job (S109 `processPendingDeliveries`, every 2 min) picks them up naturally once the window resets — no separate replay path needed. **Fail-open on store errors** (Redis blip shouldn't drop legitimate traffic): a thrown `.hit()` is caught, the dispatch proceeds normally. Per-row admin update at `POST /admin/webhooks/:id/rate-limit`; admin form has a "Rate limit (req/menit)" field on create and inline number-input on each row. Other webhook fields stay non-editable post-create (URL/events/paket are partner contracts) — only the throttle is tunable.
132. ✅ PaketView referrer attribution — `PaketView.referrerHost VARCHAR(120)` column (migration applied) captures `req.headers.referer` host on first visit (same first-touch semantics as `utm*`). `parseReferrerHost(referer, ownHost)` strips `www.` so `fb.com` and `www.fb.com` collapse to one bucket, drops same-origin URLs (in-site nav isn't useful attribution), and caps at 120 chars defensively. `recordPaketView` threads the value through; the route reads `req.get('x-forwarded-host') || req.get('host')` so a proxy-fronted deployment correctly identifies same-origin. New `getReferrerBreakdown({days=30})` groups visits by `referrerHost` (null → `(no referrer / direct)` bucket); renders as a sub-section inside the existing "Sumber kampanye (UTM)" panel on `/admin` overview so admin sees both lenses together. **Visits with UTM tags also have referrerHost** — the sub-section deliberately overlaps with the UTM table (the question "where did the audience come from?" wants the union, not the disjoint set). Conversion% deferred to S133.
133. ✅ Booking referrer + conversion% — closes the S132 deferral. `Booking.referrerHost VARCHAR(120)` column (migration applied) snapshots the first-touch referrer at create time via the same `visitorAttribution` plumb that already carries `utm*` (S51). `getVisitorAttribution` returns `referrerHost` from the oldest matching `PaketView`. `getReferrerBreakdown` now joins visits + bookings per host with `conversionPct`, mirroring the UTM panel exactly. **conversionPct=null when visits=0 but bookings>0** — avoids divide-by-zero and the misleading "∞%" reading; admin still sees those rows because they reveal traffic-blind conversions (e.g. pre-S132 bookings, direct API calls). Admin panel rendering adds Booking + Konv % columns; colour-coded by tier same as UTM (≥5% emerald / ≥2% gold / ≥1% amber / <1% ruby).
134. ✅ Webhook delivery latency p95 — closes the S129 deferral. `WebhookDelivery.durationMs` column (migration applied) captured by `attemptDelivery` on every fire (incl. timeouts — they take exactly `DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_MS` and that signal is what admin needs to see). Rate-limited PENDING rows (S131) have `durationMs=null` and naturally skip the percentile pool. `webhookHealthDigest` adds per-sub `{p50, p95, sample, overBudget}` where overBudget = `p95 > 2000ms`. **Sample guard ≥3** so one slow outlier on a quiet webhook doesn't generate a misleading percentile. **Slow-but-working flags row unhealthy too** — a partner doing too much synchronous work in the handler is a signal worth surfacing even at 100% success rate. Digest email body inlines `latency: p50 Xms · p95 Yms ⚠ over 2s budget (n=Z)` per unhealthy sub.
135. ✅ API key IP allowlist — `ApiKey.allowedIps Json?` column (migration applied) carries a CIDR/IP allowlist. `requireApiScope` rejects 403 `IP_NOT_ALLOWED` (NOT 401 — the token IS valid, just the source isn't authorised) when the request IP doesn't match any entry. **Empty/null = any IP** (back-compat with every pre-S135 row; no migration data write needed). Supports IPv4 CIDR (`192.168.1.0/24`, `0.0.0.0/0`) + bare IP exact match. IPv6 CIDR deferred — partners with IPv6 egress can list each address explicitly. `clientIpFrom(req)` honours `X-Forwarded-For` first entry then `req.ip`, strips `::ffff:` IPv4-mapped-IPv6 prefix so partners can list a plain IPv4 entry and have it match regardless of node's mapping. `normaliseAllowedIps` accepts comma/newline-separated string OR array → trimmed array (cap 50 entries — paste-bomb guard); malformed entries are NOT rejected at save (silently ignored at lookup) so a typo surfaces as "I keep getting 403s" during onboarding rather than blocking the save. Admin form has IP allowlist textarea on create + per-row inline edit (`POST /admin/api-keys/:id/allowed-ips`). Defense-in-depth alongside the bearer secret — a leaked token is useless without the partner's static egress IP.
136. ✅ Waitlist auto-promote on cancel — extends S42's nudge into a hands-off action when the oldest WAITING entry is from a "verified" jemaah (active JEMAAH user account AND ≥1 prior LUNAS booking). `findVerifiedWaitlistForPaket({paketId})` filters via cheap DB endsWith(last-4-digits) then JS-normalises the full phone for exact match (handles dashes/spaces/+62 prefix variants the same way S59 lead-reactivation does). Prior LUNAS counted via BOTH the direct `jemaahUserId` link AND the profile's user (covers older pre-S5p.2 anonymous-then-claimed bookings). When verified candidate found, `cancelBooking` calls `promoteWaitlist` with the freed booking's `kelas + paxCount` (we just made room for that shape; if jemaah wanted something different they refuse via existing manual cancel + re-promote flow) AND skips the S42 nudge (admin doesn't need "freed seats, here are candidates" email when we already handled it). Decorator audit row stamps `autoPromoted: true` + `trigger: 'cancel.auto_promote'` + `verifiedSignal: {userEmail, priorLunasCount}` so admin can distinguish from a hand-clicked promote. **Fire-and-forget** — auto-promote failure logs but doesn't abort cancel + falls through to the nudge fallback so the queue isn't silently dropped.
137. ✅ Crew SOS rate-limit — `createIncident` caps non-SOS incidents at 5 per 10 min per crew (HttpError 429 `SOS_THROTTLED`). Uses the shared rate-limit store with `incident:<crewUserId>` bucket key. **SOS type bypasses the limit entirely** — life-safety alerts always land regardless of how many MEDICAL/LOGISTICAL/etc. the same crew has filed recently. **Fail-open on store errors** — a Redis blip must NOT silently drop a lifeline; we'd rather a duplicate page than a missed real one. Error message in Bahasa surfaces seconds-until-retry + reassurance that "SOS tetap bisa dikirim kapan saja". Per-crew bucket isolation means one panicking crew can't lock out another's queue.
138. ✅ Audit CSV export — `GET /admin/audit/export.csv?from=&to=&entity=&action=&actorEmail=` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN, same gate as audit list). Streaming export — service pulls rows in 1000-row cursor batches and writes directly to the HTTP response, so a 50k-row download never holds the table in memory. **7-day default, 90-day cap, 50k row hard ceiling** (capped flag exposed in self-audit so investigator knows result was truncated). Window clamp keeps the recent end — "last 90 of requested" is more useful than "first 90" for compliance asks. UTF-8 BOM + CRLF (Excel-compatible, mirrors S106 convention). Filter inputs match the audit-list page so the "Export ⇩ CSV" button preserves whatever filter the admin already narrowed to. **Export is itself audited** (`action=EXPORT, entity=AuditLog`) with `{rowsWritten, capped, rangeFrom, rangeTo, filters}` snapshot — investigator never disputes "did anyone pull the log?". Day-count uses `floor((to - from)/msPerDay) + 1` so a same-day request resolves to 1 inclusive day, not 2.
139. ✅ Audit retention archive — `archiveAuditLog({retentionDays=730})` streams AuditLog rows older than 2 years to a gzipped CSV under `private/audit-archive/audit_<timestamp>_pre_<cutoff>.csv.gz`, then deletes them from DB. **Reverses the historic "AuditLog kept forever" rule** — operators grep the `.gz` files via `zcat` for long-tail compliance asks; bounded growth on the live table. CSV format is identical to S138 export so an investigator opening the archive gets a consistent shape. **One file per run** named with timestamp + cutoff date — no overwrites, no append; partial-failure recovery is just "next run picks up what's still in DB" (acceptable duplicate across files if DB delete failed mid-way). Wired into the weekly prune job (env `RETENTION_AUDIT_ARCHIVE_DAYS`; set to `0` to disable archival for deployments that prefer KEPT-FOREVER). `private/` is in SENSITIVE_PREFIXES so archive files aren't publicly served. Best-effort in the prune wrapper — a failing archive run doesn't abort the rest of the sweep.
140. ✅ Per-paket attendance trend sparkline — `buildAttendanceTrend(days, totalActive)` rolls up the existing day-level `presentCount + markedCount` into `{ticks, avgPct, markedDayCount}`. **Days with zero marks naturally render as 0%** with `hasData=false` so the view dims them (an unmarked day is "we have no data", not "0% present"); avgPct deliberately excludes them so the rolled-up number stays honest. Both crew `/crew/paket/:slug/attendance` (`listAttendanceDays`) and admin `/admin/paket/:slug/attendance` (`getPaketAttendanceReport`) return the same `trend` shape. Inline SVG sparkline partial `views/partials/attendance-sparkline.ejs` renders 320×40px bars colour-coded by tier (≥80% emerald / ≥60% gold / <60% ruby; no-data ink at 0.25 opacity). Per-bar `<title>` tooltips carry the raw counts ("H3 · 12/18 hadir (67%)") so admin can hover for detail without scrolling the table. Average pct rendered next to the chart with the same colour tier — crew + admin spot collapsing attendance at a glance.
141. ✅ Manifest close jemaah nudge — `Booking.manifestCloseNotifiedAt DateTime?` column + `MANIFEST_CLOSE_NUDGE` enum (migration applied). `getManifestCloseNudgeCandidates({windowHours=72})` finds active bookings on paket whose `manifestClosesAt` is within 72h (or overdue) AND whose jemaah has ≥1 required item missing (passport / visa umroh / vaksin meningitis VERIFIED / kontak darurat present). Health cert / manasik cert / room assignment are nice-to-haves and don't trigger a nudge alone — keeps the signal actionable, not nagging. **Idempotent** via `manifestCloseNotifiedAt` stamp: query already excludes bookings where the field is set, and `notifyManifestCloseNudge` stamps `now` after enqueue so the daily cron doesn't pile up duplicates. Fires both EMAIL + WA (per-channel opt-out via `JemaahProfile.notifEmail/notifWa` respected via existing `enqueueNotification` mechanism). `recipientUserId` set when booking is linked so `/saya/notifications` inbox + unread badge pick it up. Stamp fires even when the jemaah has NO email/phone — prevents the cron re-evaluating contact-less rows every run. Daily cron + CLI `npm run job:send-manifest-close` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-manifest-close` + jobRunner interval registered. Silent on quiet days — empty candidates → no email.
142. ✅ Admin manifest close nudge mirror — `getManifestCloseNudgeAdminSummary({windowHours=24})` reads recent S141 `MANIFEST_CLOSE_NUDGE` notif rows and aggregates by paket so admin can do manual WA follow-up without grep'ing the queue. Per-paket row carries the bookings that got nudged (deduped by bookingId so EMAIL+WA collapse into one entry with `channels: ['EMAIL','WA']`) + `missingSummary` rollup (`{label, count}` desc — "8 jemaah missing Visa umroh, 3 missing Kontak darurat"). Sorted by `manifestClosesAt` asc so the soonest-closing paket lands at the top. Panel on `/admin` overview between manifest-closing countdown and paket forecast. Each booking row gets a `wa.me/<phone>` link generated from the existing jemaah phone (digits-only + 0→62 normalisation, same convention as the Fonnte adapter S5kk). Collapsed by default via `<details>` so a paket with 20 nudged jemaah doesn't dominate the overview.
143. ✅ Webhook signature replay protection (timestamped HMAC) — `hmacVerifier` extended with `requireTimestamp:true` opt-in. Reads `X-Webhook-Timestamp` header (epoch seconds), rejects requests outside ±5min skew window (`REPLAY_SKEW_SEC=300`, Stripe-style). **Signed body is `<ts>.<rawBody>`** (Stripe-style), so an attacker swapping the header timestamp to dodge the skew check fails the HMAC verify — both checks have to pass together. New `generic-ts` source registered as the model integration for partners that support it; legacy `fonnte`/`zapier`/`generic` keep no-ts behavior (per-source opt-in so existing partners aren't suddenly broken). **Outbound side mirrored** — `signWithTimestamp(secret, body, tsSec)` + every `attemptDelivery` POST now sends `X-Webhook-Timestamp` + `X-Religio-Signature-V2` (timestamped) alongside the legacy `X-Religio-Signature` (body-only), so partners can opt into replay protection on their receive side without breaking existing partners. **Per-attempt fresh timestamp** — retries get a new ts so a partner's narrow skew window doesn't cause our cron retries to be rejected. Secret rotation grace (S118) covers both signature variants — `X-Religio-Signature-V2-Prev` ships during the grace window.
144. ✅ Booking no-show detection — `Booking.noShowAt DateTime?` + index (migration applied). Daily `detectNoShows({now, dryRun})` finds active bookings (PENDING/BOOKED/DP_PAID/PARTIAL/LUNAS) on paket whose `departureDate` has passed AND zero `AttendanceMark` exists for `dayNumber=1`, then stamps `noShowAt=now`. **Marked-absent ≠ no-show** — any mark (present OR absent) means crew was tracking the jemaah; the no-show signal is specifically "we never knew if you showed". Paket without an itinerary day 1 skip (we'd be guessing). CANCELLED/REFUNDED exclude. Idempotent via the stamp itself — query filters `noShowAt: null` so re-runs are no-ops; admin clears the field manually if a late correction reverses the verdict. Per-row audit row (`STATUS_CHANGE entity=Booking after={noShowAt, trigger:'noshow.daily_detection'}`) so the timeline shows when the system flipped a particular booking. `/admin/no-shows` queue page (`listNoShows`, paginated 50/page, OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS gate via `/admin` mount) with 3-cell KPI (total, LUNAS no-show count, sum paid) + per-row `wa.me/<phone>` link for follow-up. `⚠ NO-SHOW` badge in the header of `/admin/bookings/:id`. CLI `npm run job:detect-no-shows` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/detect-no-shows` + jobRunner daily interval registered.
145. ✅ No-show refund guard rail — `issueRefund` accepts `acknowledgeNoShow:boolean`. When `booking.noShowAt` is set AND `amount >= currentPaid` (full refund) AND `!acknowledgeNoShow` → throws 409 `NOSHOW_REFUND_NEEDS_ACK` with a Bahasa explanation ("Mungkin jemaah terbang dengan operator lain"). **Partial refunds bypass the guard** — goodwill 30%/50% rebates don't carry the "they may have flown with someone else" risk, only full refund does. Audit row carries `wasNoShow:true` + `noShowAcknowledged:bool` for every refund on a stamped booking (durable trail for compliance — "did we knowingly refund all the no-shows last quarter?"). `cancelBooking` mirrors the audit annotation (`wasNoShow:true` + `noShowFlaggedAt:<iso>` when present), so a no-show being formally closed out is also traceable. Refund modal in `/admin/bookings/:id` shows a ruby warning banner + an explicit checkbox when `b.noShowAt` is set; checkbox value flows through the existing FormData → JSON path so no JS change beyond the markup. Zod preprocessor on the refund route accepts `true`/`"true"`/`"1"`/`"on"` so form-encoded + JSON callers both work.
146. ✅ No-show rate analytics — `getNoShowAnalytics({days=90})` returns per-paket + per-agent rollup mirroring the S35 refund analytics shape. **Numerator** = bookings with `noShowAt` stamped within window. **Denominator** = bookings on paket whose `departureDate` falls within window AND status NOT IN (CANCELLED, REFUNDED) — only "resolved-active" bookings count (we don't dilute the rate with future bookings whose verdict is still pending). `ratePct` is null when denominator=0 so a no-show on a future-departing paket (theoretical, shouldn't happen post-S144 but defensive) renders as "—" not "∞%". Walk-in bookings bucket under `__kp__` sentinel with `displayName='Kantor Pusat'`, mirroring S35 convention. Sort: `noShowCount desc` so the heaviest leakers land at the top. Panel on `/admin` overview between refund analytics and komisi monthly with 2-cell KPI strip + two columns (per-paket + per-agent, top 10 each). Colour-coded by tier (≥10% ruby / ≥5% amber / ≥2% gold / <2% emerald). Only renders when `totalNoShow > 0` so quiet weeks don't waste real estate.
147. ✅ Jemaah cancel deadline lock — `requestCancelByJemaah` accepts `now` param + checks `booking.paket.manifestClosesAt < now`. Past the deadline, throws 409 `CANCEL_DEADLINE_PASSED` with a Bahasa explanation directing the jemaah to admin/agen. **Paket without `manifestClosesAt` never locks** — admin chose "never close" or hasn't set the date yet; jemaah can still cancel anytime. **Admin flow (`cancelBooking`) bypasses the guard entirely** — admin can still cancel post-deadline (e.g. as a manual override after commercial dispute). `/saya/bookings/:id` view surfaces three distinct states: (a) `cancelRequested` (existing pending request banner — unchanged), (b) `deadlinePassed && active` (new ruby-bordered "Deadline pembatalan sudah lewat" panel directing to admin), (c) the existing request-cancel CTA — now decorated with a `⏱ Batas pengajuan: <date> (Nh lagi)` countdown amber-flagged when ≤72h. `getMyBooking` paket select extended with `manifestClosesAt`. Prevents the "I want to cancel" coming in 2 hours before departure when the seat can't be resold.
148. ✅ Unread notif badge on `/agen` + `/crew` — extends the S5rr jemaah inbox pattern to the other portals. The existing `countUnreadForUser` / `markAllReadForUser` / `listMyNotifications` helpers from `jemaahPortal.js` are **role-agnostic** (queries filter by `recipientUserId` only), so reusing them across portals required zero service-layer changes — just import + add the routes. New routes: `GET /agen/notifications` + `GET /crew/notifications` (same pattern as `/saya/notifications`: render list then `markAllReadForUser` so the badge clears on next paint while the current paint still shows the gold left-border + dot on unread rows). Topbar badges on `/agen` (next to saldo wallet) + `/crew` (next to logout button) render a gold pill with the unread count when `unreadCount > 0`, hidden otherwise. Shared `views/partials/notification-list.ejs` extracted from the original `jemaah-notifications.ejs` so the three inbox views (`jemaah-notifications`, `agen-notifications`, `crew-notifications`) stay in sync without copy-paste drift on the row markup. The function names stay slightly jemaah-flavored (`countUnreadForUser`) because renaming would touch the existing `/saya` paths without functional benefit.
149. ✅ Booking voucher PDF cache — content-addressed cache under `private/voucher-cache/<bookingId>__<lang>__<hash>.pdf`. **Hash** is a SHA-256 truncated to 16 hex chars over every displayed field of the voucher (bookingNo / status / total / paid / kelas / paxCount / paket times+title+days+route / jemaah identity / room / agent / payments). Any change to a displayed field → new hash → cache miss → fresh render → old hash file cleaned up for the same `(bookingId, lang)`. **Per-language variants stored separately** (id / en / ar / `_<lang>` suffix). Refactor extracts `renderVoucherIntoDoc(doc, voucher, lang)` from `streamVoucherPdf` so the layout serves both the stream-to-res path and a new `renderVoucherPdfBuffer` returning a Promise<Buffer>. Routes (`/admin/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf`, `/saya/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf`) + the bundle paths (`streamBookingBundle` single + `streamBookingBundles` bulk) all route through `getOrRenderVoucherPdf`. **Best-effort** — a cache write failure logs but still returns the freshly-rendered buffer to the caller. Bundle paths keep an inline-stream fallback when the cache helper throws so a broken cache disk never breaks zip exports. `X-Voucher-Cache: HIT|MISS` response header on the standalone routes lets ops observe hit rate without instrumentation. Big bulk-dossier flows (100+ vouchers) reuse PDFs already rendered by individual admin downloads.
150. ✅ Per-agent monthly komisi statement PDF — new `KomisiStatement(agentId, periodYM, totalEarnedIdr, totalPaidIdr, lineCount, pdfPath, generatedAt)` model (migration applied) with composite-unique `(agentId, periodYM)`. `generateAgentStatement({agentId, periodYM})` queries EARNED + PAID komisi where `earnedAt` OR `paidAt` falls in the period, renders a programmatic A4 PDF (pdfkit, same pattern as S101 voucher), persists under `private/komisi-statements/<agentId>__<YYYY-MM>.pdf`, and records the row. **Idempotent**: re-running for the same period returns the existing row + PDF without re-rendering (the statement is supposed to be an immutable monthly artifact — changes to underlying data don't retroactively update old statements). CANCELLED komisi excluded (undone work, not income). `generateAllAgentStatements` iterates every ACTIVE agent + catches per-agent failures so a bad row doesn't abort the batch. CLI `npm run job:generate-komisi-statements` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/generate-komisi-statements` + jobRunner monthly interval. Cron Mon 1st generates the previous-month statement per active agent. Agent download route `/agen/statements/:id.pdf` enforces ownership via `agentProfile.userId` chain (cross-agent access 404s). Wallet tab on `/agen` shows up to 24 most-recent statements as compact cards with EARNED + PAID totals + line count.
151. ✅ Admin statement regenerate override — escape hatch for the S150 immutability rule when a late komisi adjustment lands after the original cron pass. `regenerateAgentStatement({agentId, periodYM})` captures the prior `{totalEarnedIdr, totalPaidIdr, lineCount, pdfPath}` for audit, deletes the existing row + PDF (best-effort `unlink`), then re-invokes `generateAgentStatement`. Audit row carries `UPDATE entity=KomisiStatement before=<prior> after={regenerated:true, ...}` so a compliance scan can answer "did the statement amount change retroactively?". POST `/admin/agents/:slug/statements/regenerate` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN), form lives on `/admin/users/:id/edit` as a panel below the komisi rate override field in the AGEN profile section. Empty `periodYM` defaults to the agent's latest existing statement (409 `NO_EXISTING_STATEMENT` when none — direct admin to run generate/backfill first). Flash banner on `/admin/users` surfaces the diff inline ("Total lama: EARNED Rp X · PAID Rp Y") so the admin sees what changed without leaving the page. PDF filename pattern `<agentId>__<period>.pdf` stays stable across regenerate so the agent's download URL keeps working.
152. ✅ Statement email delivery — new `KOMISI_STATEMENT_READY` enum (migration applied) + `notifyKomisiStatementReady` helper. Fires one EMAIL per `generateAgentStatement` create with a download link to `/agen/statements/:id.pdf` + the period's earned/paid totals. **Silent on three cases**: zero-line statement (no point notifying about a quiet month), agent has no email, agent user suspended/deleted. **Idempotent re-runs don't duplicate** — the early-return on existing statement short-circuits before the notif fire. `recipientUserId` set so the S148 `/agen/notifications` inbox + unread badge surface the message. **Fire-and-forget** — notif failure logs but never aborts statement creation (the PDF is the load-bearing artifact). Regenerate flow (S151) also benefits — re-creating after delete fires a fresh notif (admin presumably wants the agent to know the numbers changed).
153. ✅ Komisi statement backfill CLI — `backfillKomisiStatements({months=6})` walks backwards from `previousMonthYM()` for N periods and calls `generateAllAgentStatements` per period. **Idempotent** via the existing skip-if-exists in `generateAgentStatement` — re-running a backfill is safe + usually a no-op after the first pass. **Cap 24 months** (beyond two years is a one-off backfill that should be done deliberately; floor 1 month). CLI `npm run job:backfill-komisi-statements -- --months=6` (the `--` is required so npm forwards the arg to node) parses `--months=N` from argv. Per-month breakdown + grand totals logged to stdout. **NOT registered as a recurring cron** — this is a deliberate first-install / new-deployment seeding tool, not a scheduled job. Existing S152 email fires for newly-created statements during backfill but skips for the ones already there.
154. ✅ Statement zero-line opt-out — env-gated `KOMISI_STATEMENT_SKIP_ZERO_LINES=true` makes `generateAllAgentStatements` skip agents with zero lines for the period (no DB row, no PDF). Keeps the agent wallet tab tidy for agents who didn't sell anything that month — the previous behavior generated "Rp 0 / 0 baris" PDFs they never wanted. **Check is at the cron/batch layer**, not inside `generateAgentStatement` — the direct service call (used by admin regenerate S151) **always produces** regardless of flag, since explicit admin intent overrides the quiet-month policy. Pre-check via `getStatementLines` avoids rendering the PDF + creating the row when we'd skip anyway. **Existing rows are preserved** even when flag is on (idempotency wins over the policy — once a row exists the SKIP gate stops mattering). Reads env at call time (not module load) so runtime toggles + tests work without restart. New `zeroSkipped` counter in the result shape so admin can see how many quiet months were elided per run.
155. ✅ Statement YTD running totals — `computeYtdTotals({agentId, periodYM})` returns three slices over the calendar year: **before** (Jan 1 → period start, exclusive), **during** (the period itself), **after** (Jan 1 → period end, inclusive). Each carries `{earnedIdr, paidIdr, count}`. **Suppressed on January with no prior signal** — empty before-window in January means no rollover from last year, so the YTD block adds no signal; February onwards always renders even with zero before-totals so the agent sees the running tape start fresh. PDF gets a new "YTD <year> (komulatif)" block below the period totals: 3-row table with Window / EARNED / PAID columns, "Setelah periode ini" row bolded + green-tinted so the cumulative-so-far number stands out. `generateAgentStatement` wraps `computeYtdTotals` in try/catch so a compute failure just drops the block without aborting PDF render. Lets agents see "I earned 300k this year so far" at a glance without flipping through 12 monthly PDFs.
156. ✅ Admin note on statement — `KomisiStatement.adminNote Text?` (migration applied). `generateAgentStatement` + `regenerateAgentStatement` accept an `adminNote` arg, trim + cap at 2000 chars (empty → null), persist on the row, and render as a gold-bordered "CATATAN DARI RELIGIO PRO" block at the end of the PDF body. **Three-state semantics** on `regenerateAgentStatement`: `undefined` (omitted arg) **preserves** the prior note; `''` or `null` **clears** it; non-empty string **replaces**. Achieved by dropping the destructuring default — `adminNote` arg with no value passed gets `undefined`. Route `POST /admin/agents/:slug/statements/regenerate` reads `req.body?.adminNote ?? null` so an empty textarea clears (form behaviour) while an omitted field would preserve (API behaviour). Audit row carries both prior + new `adminNote` so retroactive note edits show up in compliance scans. Wallet-tab card on `/agen` gets a gold pill (`✎ ada catatan`) when set, with the full note in `title` for hover-tooltip; the agent then opens the PDF for the full bordered block.
157. ✅ Agent statement prefs self-service — `AgentProfile.notifKomisiStatement Boolean @default(true)` (migration applied). `notifyKomisiStatementReady` checks the flag (default `true` for back-compat — legacy callers omitting the field still fire) and returns `{skipped:true, reason:'opted_out'}` when off. `generateAgentStatement` select includes the field + passes it to the notif helper so the opt-out is honoured without an extra round-trip. **Statement row + PDF still created when opted out** — opt-out only suppresses the email; the artifact stays available via `/agen` wallet tab download. New `/agen/profile` page with identity strip + preferences panel (currently just the statement toggle, but the page is the natural place to add more agent-level prefs). `POST /agen/profile/prefs` normalises unchecked HTML checkbox to explicit `false` (mirrors S5jj jemaah-side pattern — checkbox absent from `req.body` would otherwise leave the flag unchanged). Topbar link added to `agen-crm.ejs` so agents can find the page.
158. ✅ Statement annual recap email — `AGENT_ANNUAL_RECAP` enum (migration applied) + `buildAgentAnnualRecap({agentId, year})` aggregates KomisiStatement rows where `periodYM startsWith <year>-` into totals + sorted-asc per-month breakdown. Returns null when agent has zero statements in scope so caller silently skips. `notifyAgentAnnualRecap` fires one EMAIL with month-by-month table inline. **Three skip reasons**: `no_email`, `no_statements`, `opted_out` (same flag as S152 — conceptually the same kind of message, no separate toggle). `sendAgentAnnualRecaps({year})` batch entry loops `listAgentsWithStatementsForYear` (excludes suspended/deleted agents — they don't get retro emails). **No idempotency** — expected cadence is once-per-year so accidental double-run sends duplicates; operators pre-purge by year before re-runs. Jan 5 cron + CLI `npm run job:send-agent-annual-recap` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-agent-annual-recap` (accepts `year` body param for re-runs) + jobRunner yearly interval registered.
159. ✅ Per-paket komisi statement (dispute resolution) — `getStatementLines` accepts optional `paketId` arg that adds `where.booking.paketId = paketId` to the komisi query. New `renderPaketScopedStatementBuffer({agentId, periodYM, paketId})` builds a transient PDF for a single (agent × paket × period) tuple. **Does NOT persist a KomisiStatement row** — purely read-only snapshot for admin to share during back-and-forth like "I think you under-counted my Ramadhan-2026 komisi, show me only that paket's lines". Header subtitle decorated with `· scope: <paket title>` so it's obvious this isn't the canonical monthly artifact; PDF carries a transient `adminNote` explaining the scope. Admin route `GET /admin/agents/:slug/statement-paket.pdf?periodYM=YYYY-MM&paketSlug=X` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN) streams the buffer inline. Query-param URL is shareable. Filename pattern `komisi_<agent-slug>_<period>_<paket-slug>.pdf` sanitised against path traversal.
160. ✅ PDF watermark for preview statements — `renderStatementPdfBuffer` accepts a `watermark` arg that renders a 72pt diagonal text overlay at -30° across the page at 10% ruby opacity. Applied AFTER all body content so it sits on top of every block. **S159 `renderPaketScopedStatementBuffer` passes `'PREVIEW · TIDAK KANONIK'`** so dispute-resolution PDFs look visually distinct from the canonical S150 monthly artifact even at a glance. Canonical S150 path **never** sets the watermark (no visual ambiguity for the official statement). Tests use buffer-size delta rather than literal-byte-search because pdfkit zlib-compresses content streams — bytes of "PREVIEW" don't survive the compression, but the watermark draw call adds ≥200 bytes of compressed content reliably. Pattern is ready to reuse for future preview surfaces (e.g. backfill dry-run, draft statements before admin approval).
161. ✅ Cross-paket range statement — `renderRangeStatementBuffer({agentId, from, to})` aggregates komisi across all paket within a date window. Same transient + watermarked posture as S159 (no `KomisiStatement` row, S160 PREVIEW overlay). **Window capped at 90 days** (`RANGE_TOO_WIDE` 409) — beyond a quarter, agent should be using the canonical monthly statements. **Validation chain**: `BAD_AGENT` → `BAD_RANGE` (from/to missing) → `BAD_DATE` (unparseable) → `BAD_RANGE_ORDER` (to<from) → `RANGE_TOO_WIDE` (>90d) → `AGENT_NOT_FOUND`, so a malformed request returns the most specific error possible. Synthetic `periodYM = '<from> → <to>'` reuses the existing PDF render's "Periode" line without misleadingly anchoring to a single month. Admin route `GET /admin/agents/:slug/statement-range.pdf?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN) streams the buffer inline; filename `komisi_<agent-slug>_<from>_to_<to>.pdf` sanitised against path traversal. Answers "show me all komisi for agent X for Q1 2026" without forcing admin to open three monthly PDFs.
162. ✅ Statement download counter — `KomisiStatement.{agentDownloadCount, agentLastDownloadAt, adminDownloadCount, adminLastDownloadAt}` columns (migration applied; defaults 0/null). `recordStatementDownload({statementId, surface})` increments the matching counter pair atomically via Prisma `{increment:1}` + stamps `now()`. **Per-surface tracking** so admin can distinguish "agent never opened the PDF" from "admin pulled it for an audit" — different signals, different follow-up. `/agen/statements/:id.pdf` bumps `agent*` via `res.on('finish')` (fire-and-forget AFTER the response so latency isn't affected). New admin route `GET /admin/agents/:slug/statements/:id.pdf` streams the same canonical PDF + bumps `admin*` — lets admin pull a copy without impersonating the agent. Counter writes are best-effort (try/catch + log) so a DB hiccup never breaks the actual download. Surfaced on `/admin/users/:id/edit` as a 6-row table showing recent periods + per-surface counts; agent zero counts highlighted amber so "agent hasn't opened the last 3 months" jumps out for follow-up. Invalid surface arg → no-op; missing statementId → no-op; non-existent row → silently swallowed.
163. ✅ Stale statement WA nudge — daily cron + CLI `npm run job:send-statement-unread-nudge` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-statement-unread-nudge` finds ACTIVE agents who have at least one KomisiStatement in the last 3 months with `agentDownloadCount=0` AND haven't been nudged within `cooldownDays=14`. Sends a soft WA "Anda punya N statement belum dibuka (terlama: YYYY-MM)" via existing `enqueueNotification`. New `STATEMENT_UNREAD_NUDGE` enum (migration applied). **Per-agent cooldown via the Notification table itself** — no extra state; query checks for a prior STATEMENT_UNREAD_NUDGE within `cooldownCutoff`. Skips zero-line statements (no point nudging about a quiet month) + respects the S157 `notifKomisiStatement` opt-out (statement WA and statement EMAIL are conceptually the same kind of message — no separate WA toggle). 14-day cooldown means monthly statements get at most two nudges before silence. Sort: oldest-unread-first so the most-stale agents bubble to the top of a future per-run quota. `notifyStatementUnreadNudge` is the per-row helper; `sendStatementUnreadNudges` is the batch entry that loops candidates with per-agent failure isolation. **Silent on empty candidate list** — quiet days produce zero enqueues.
164. ✅ Agent statement history page — `/agen/statements` paginated list (20/page) of the agent's full statement history beyond the 24-month wallet-tab cap. `listAgentStatementsPaginated({agentId, page, pageSize})` returns rows + `lifetime: {earnedIdr, paidIdr, lineCount, statementCount}` (a single `aggregate(_sum)` call for the totals — no per-row math in JS). Page size clamped to [1..100], page clamped to ≥1 (negative values floor to 1). 4-cell lifetime KPI strip + table of (periode, EARNED, PAID, lines, opened/unread badge, generated date, PDF+CSV download). The wallet-tab card-grid still shows the last 24 months at a glance; this page is the "all the way back" surface for long-tail review. Linked from a "RIWAYAT LENGKAP →" link in the wallet-tab panel header.
165. ✅ Statement CSV export — `buildStatementCsv({agentId, periodYM})` reuses the same `getStatementLines` source as the PDF so the spreadsheet and the printable both reflect identical numbers. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 quoting + CRLF row separators (Excel mojibake-proof, matches the S138 audit export convention). Columns: bookingNo / jemaahName / paketTitle / paketSlug / earnedAt / paidAt / amountIdr / status / currency, plus a TOTAL footer row carrying separate EARNED + PAID sums so the CSV is self-contained as an audit artifact. Routes: `/agen/statements/:id.csv` (agent) + `/admin/agents/:slug/statements/:id.csv` (admin) — both honour the existing ownership chains and bump the matching surface download counter on `res.on('finish')`. CSV downloads count toward the same `agentDownloadCount`/`adminDownloadCount` as the PDF — opening the CSV is just as much "looked at the content" as the PDF would be.
166. ✅ Agent payout banking details — `AgentProfile.{preferredPayoutMethod, bankName, bankAccountNumber, bankAccountName}` columns (migration applied, all nullable so pre-S166 agents stay valid). Self-service via `POST /agen/profile/payout-details` (3-state preprocessor: `undefined` preserves, `''` clears, value stores). `updateAgentPayoutDetails` enforces a Zod schema + skip-audit-on-no-op so re-saving identical values doesn't pollute the log. **Account number is masked in audit snapshots** (first 2 + last 2 chars only, rest `*`) — the live DB row keeps the full value, but the audit table is a secondary surface admins grep through, so partial masking limits damage if logs leak. `/admin/payouts/new?agentId=<id>` reads the stored details and pre-fills `method` + injects a "Bank: BCA · No 1234567 · a/n Ahmad" snippet into the `reference` field, plus renders an amber banner above the form so KASIR sees who they're paying. KASIR still has full edit control — pre-fill is convenience, not a lock. Closes the loop on the S37 payout reminder: admin sees WHO needs payment AND how to pay them in one workflow.
167. ✅ Booking duplicate phone warning — `findRecentBookingsByPhone({phone, windowDays=90})` returns active bookings (NOT IN CANCELLED/REFUNDED) matching the phone within window. **Normalisation** mirrors S59 (lead reactivation): digits-only, leading `0` → `62`, so `+62 822-3399`, `082233 99`, and `622339911` collapse to one key. **Cheap DB prefilter via `endsWith` on last 8 digits**, then JS re-checks the full normalised form to avoid tail-match false positives (`082155667788` doesn't trigger for `081155667788`). On `POST /admin/bookings`, when admin hasn't ticked `confirmDuplicate`, re-renders the form with an amber warning panel listing each match (bookingNo + jemaah + paket + status + agent + date) with deep links. Admin ticks "Lanjut tetap" → second POST bypasses the check entirely. `findRecentLeadsByPhone({phone, agentId})` mirrors the same logic for the agen CRM lead-create flow (excludes terminal CONVERTED/LOST). Empty/short phone → empty result (no point asking the DB for 3-digit prefixes).
168. ✅ Lifetime komisi CSV — `buildAgentLifetimeKomisiCsv({agentId})` exports every Komisi row across the agent's entire history (PENDING/EARNED/PAID/CANCELLED, all paket, all periods). Distinct from S165 (per-period statement CSV) — that's scoped to one periodYM and matches the PDF; this is the full lifetime ledger for personal accounting / tax prep. Sorted oldest-first so spreadsheet running-total formulas read naturally. Columns: createdAt / earnedAt / paidAt / bookingNo / jemaahName / paketTitle / paketSlug / amountIdr / status / currency / payoutNo. TOTAL footer carries EARNED + PAID sums + rowCount. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 quoting + CRLF, matching the S138/S165 convention. Route `/agen/komisi-lifetime.csv` (agent ownership via `userId → AgentProfile.id` chain); filename `komisi_lifetime_<slug>.csv` sanitised against path traversal. Linked from the Wallet tab below the KPI strip, only when `komisi.total > 0` (no point on empty wallets).
169. ✅ Lead duplicate phone warning — mirrors S167's booking dup check for the agen CRM lead-create flow. `POST /api/leads` runs `findRecentLeadsByPhone` + `findRecentBookingsByPhone` upfront when phone is set; returns 409 `DUPLICATE_LEAD` with `{duplicates: {leads[], bookings[]}}` envelope when either fires. Client (agen-crm modal) shows inline warning panel + sets `leadConfirmDuplicate=true` so the next submit carries `confirmDuplicate: true` in the JSON body to bypass the check. Confirmed-state resets on modal close so re-opening the modal triggers a fresh check. **JSON 409 + client-side warning** rather than re-render (S167 pattern) because the lead flow is fetch-driven, not form-POST. Both lead AND booking dupes surface — an agent who sees "this jemaah already has a booking" might decide the lead is unnecessary entirely. Excludes terminal CONVERTED/LOST lead statuses + CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings — past closed signals shouldn't block re-engagement.
170. ✅ Agent payout history CSV — `buildAgentPayoutHistoryCsv({agentId})` exports every `KomisiPayout` disbursed to the agent (one row each, ordered oldest-first). Columns: paidAt / payoutNo / amountIdr / currency / method / reference / komisiLines (bundled count from `_count.komisi`) / paidByEmail / notes. TOTAL footer with sum + count. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 / CRLF matching the S168 lifetime ledger convention. Distinct from S168 — that's per-Komisi-row, this is per-payout-receipt for bank-statement reconciliation. Route `/agen/payout-history.csv` (agent ownership chain); filename `payout_history_<slug>.csv` sanitised against path traversal. "⇩ CSV LENGKAP" link in the Wallet tab "Riwayat payout" panel header, only when `payouts.length > 0`.
171. ✅ Agent KPI scorecard — `getAgentKpiScorecard({agentId})` aggregates the agent's lifetime state from Booking + Komisi + Lead in three parallel queries (no N+1). Returns `{counts: {total, active, lunas, cancelled}, conversionPct, revenue, lastBookingAt, komisi: {pending, earned, paid, cancelled, lifetime}, leads: {cold, warm, converted, lost, total}, topPaket[3]}`. **conversionPct = lunas / active × 100** — denominator EXCLUDES CANCELLED/REFUNDED (undone work, not a real outcome). **conversionPct=null when active=0** to avoid divide-by-zero / misleading "no bookings → 0% conversion" reading. **komisi.lifetime sums PENDING + EARNED + PAID, NOT CANCELLED** — cancelled is undone, not part of lifetime earnings. Top 3 paket by LUNAS revenue (the agent's specialty / over-reliance signal). Surfaced on `/admin/users/:id/edit` as a 4-cell KPI panel above the statement counters table; hidden when agent has zero bookings AND zero leads (new agent, nothing to summarize). Best-effort compute — exception logs but doesn't 500 the edit page.
172. ✅ Payment reminder cron — daily nudge to jemaah with unpaid balance on bookings whose paket departs within `windowDays=14`. `getPaymentReminderCandidates` filters active bookings (PENDING/BOOKED/DP_PAID/PARTIAL — LUNAS owes nothing, CANCELLED/REFUNDED are dead), then JS-filters those with `paidAmount < totalAmount` (Prisma can't compare two columns in `where` without raw SQL). **Per-booking cooldown** via the Notification table — checks for prior `PAYMENT_REMINDER` notif within `cooldownDays=5`, so jemaah don't get the same nudge every single day until takeoff. Sort by soonest-departing first so urgent rows surface to any per-run quota. `notifyPaymentReminder` fires BOTH EMAIL + WA when both are present (each respects the jemaah's per-channel opt-out via `enqueueNotification`). New `PAYMENT_REMINDER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-payment-reminder` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-payment-reminder` + jobRunner daily interval. Silent on quiet days.
173. ✅ Document expiring soon email — daily cron emails jemaah whose tracked `JemaahDocument` rows have `expiresAt ≤ now + 30d`. Pairs with the S47 admin-side visual signal (per-doc colored border + RENEW button) so jemaah see the same warning in their inbox without admin manually nudging. **Groups all expiring docs into ONE email per jemaah per run** (rather than N separate inbox hits when a passport + visa + vaksin expire close together). **Excludes REJECTED + EXPIRED status** — REJECTED needs full resubmission not renewal, EXPIRED is covered by a different surface (admin manual follow-up). Excludes docs with no `expiresAt` (e.g. marriage cert). Per-jemaah `cooldownDays=7` via the Notification table. Soonest-expiring jemaah surface first; docs within each jemaah row also sorted soonest-first. New `DOC_EXPIRING_SOON` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-doc-expiring` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-doc-expiring` + jobRunner daily interval. Per-channel opt-out via `JemaahProfile.notifEmail` (DB filter, not just enqueue-time skip — saves a roundtrip).
174. ✅ Waitlist CSV export — `buildWaitlistCsv(paketSlug)` exports every `PaketWaitlist` row for offline outreach campaigns (admin pulls the CSV, works through phone calls in a spreadsheet, marks promote/cancel via admin UI as they reach each jemaah). **Includes ALL statuses** (WAITING/PROMOTED/CANCELLED) — historical context "we already tried this person" is useful, the view's status filter is UI hygiene not data hygiene. Columns: createdAt / status / fullName / phone / kelas / paxCount / notes / promotedBookingId / promotedAt / cancelledAt. Footer carries per-status counts. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 / CRLF matching the convention. Route `/admin/paket/:slug/waitlist.csv` (inherits the existing `paketAdminRouter` RBAC gate). "⇩ CSV Outreach" button in the waitlist page header, only when `rows.length > 0`.
175. ✅ Cancel reason categorization — new `BookingCancelReason` enum + `Booking.cancelReasonCode` nullable column (migration applied + composite index for the analytics scan). 7 categories: JEMAAH_REQUEST / PAKET_CANCELLED / PAYMENT_NOT_RECEIVED / DOCUMENT_INCOMPLETE / NO_SHOW / GOODWILL / OTHER. Admin picks from dropdown in the cancel modal; `cancelBooking({reason, reasonCode})` validates against the enum (case-insensitive normalisation, BAD_CANCEL_REASON_CODE 400 on typo) and persists alongside the free-text `cancelReason`. **Nullable** → historical cancels (pre-S175) stay valid; `null` codes bucket under `__UNSET__` in the analytics so admin sees the categorisation backlog. `getCancelReasonBreakdown({days=90})` aggregates CANCELLED + REFUNDED bookings by code with count + sharePct + paidIdr. **Sort by count desc, __UNSET__ always last** regardless of size so the categorised data dominates the visual ranking. Panel on `/admin` overview between no-show analytics and komisi monthly; hidden when `total === 0`. Audit row also carries `cancelReasonCode` when present so compliance scans can answer "how many goodwill cancellations did we issue last quarter?".
176. ✅ Per-paket break-even tracker — `getPaketBreakEven({paketId})` projects "N more LUNAS bookings until cost is covered" using existing S22/S39 cost + komisi math. **Per-pax formula**: `marginPerPax = avgRevenuePerPax − costPerPaxIdr − avgKomisiPerPax`; `booksNeeded = ceil(−netSoFarIdr / marginPerPax)` when net is negative. Uses LUNAS-bookings averages so the projection reflects the agent mix actually selling the trip (high-komisi-rate agents pull marginPerPax down). **Day-one fallback** — when zero LUNAS yet, falls back to featured `PaketHarga.priceIdr` + paket `komisiRate` so the widget still surfaces on a fresh paket. Returns `hasCost=false` when `costPerPaxIdr` is unset (no break-even target exists). **`booksNeeded=null` when marginPerPax ≤ 0** — surfaces a "tidak mungkin: naikkan harga / turunkan biaya" warning instead of a misleading positive number. `feasible` flag compares against `seatsLeft` so admin sees "need 20 more but only 5 kursi left → won't fill". Panel on `/admin/paket/:slug/edit` below the existing profitability gauge.
177. ✅ Last-login sort on user list — `listUsers({sortBy='lastLogin'})` orders by `lastLoginAt asc nulls:last` (oldest-logged-in first, never-logged-in lands at the very bottom). `/admin/users?sortBy=lastLogin` toggle in the table header preserves the existing q/role/status/deleted filter state. Column shows the date + relative `Nh lalu` subtitle; color tier (>30d amber, >90d ruby). **Admin roles get an extra ⚠ warning glyph** when login >60d (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS/KASIR/SALES — these accounts shouldn't be dormant). Never-logged-in admin gets a ruby "admin tdk pernah login" tag. Pairs with S102/S104 (inactive jemaah prune + soft-deleted viewer) — same observability theme, different angle (sort vs filter).
178. ✅ Bunking room swap — `swapBookingRooms({bookingIdA, bookingIdB})` swaps two bookings' room assignments in one transaction; saves the 4-step manual flow (unassign A, unassign B, reassign each). **Cross-paket pair rejected** (PAKET_MISMATCH) since "operationally meaningless and would muddy the audit trail". **Symmetric validation**: kelas check on each destination + capacity check that excludes the two swap participants (they cancel each other in occupancy math). **Same-room → no-op return** (no audit pollution). **Three-phase transaction** (detach A → attach B → attach A) avoids per-row constraint hits mid-swap. Two-click UI in admin Bunking tab: per-slot ⇄ button selects source (gold-highlighted), click another booking's ⇄ swaps. Floating bottom banner shows current source + cancel link. Each booking gets its own audit row stamping `swap: true` + `swappedWith: <other-bookingNo>` so the booking-detail timeline shows both legs.
179. ✅ Admin team sticky note — single-row `AdminTeamNote(id='singleton', body, updatedById, updatedByEmail, updatedAt)` (migration applied) for cross-admin team communication. Visible to all admin sessions on `/admin` overview header; collapsible read view + inline edit form (any admin role can edit). **Singleton pattern** — `id='singleton'` lets us always upsert by known PK without tracking row ids. **Skip-audit-on-no-op** (mirrors `updateBookingNotes` convention) so re-saving identical text doesn't pollute the audit log. `getAdminTeamNote()` returns null when empty (view shows "belum ada catatan" placeholder). `updateAdminTeamNote()` cap 4000 chars + clears to null on empty string. POST `/admin/team-note` (any of the 4 admin roles).
180. ✅ Booking note templates — `BookingNoteTemplate(name UNIQUE, body, sortOrder)` (migration applied) for reusable common phrases (lansia / mahram / diet khusus). Quick-insert `<select>` dropdown above the notes textarea on `/admin/bookings/:id` — picking an option appends the template body to the existing text (with `\n` separator when needed) so admin can stack multiple templates + handwrite. **Listing readable by 4 admin VIEW roles** so the dropdown surfaces for MANAJER_OPS + KASIR too; **mutations OWNER+SUPERADMIN only** via `/admin/bookings/note-templates` CRUD page. P2002 unique-name collision → 409 `TEMPLATE_NAME_TAKEN` (more actionable than the opaque Prisma error). Each CRUD operation writes an audit row with before/after diff. Dropdown hidden when `noteTemplates.length === 0` so first-time admins don't see a confusing empty control.
181. ✅ Notification inbox pagination — `listMyNotificationsPaginated(userId, {page, pageSize=50})` returns `{rows, total, pagination: {page, pageSize, pageCount}}`. Page clamped to ≥1 (negatives floor to 1), pageSize clamped to [1..100]. Wired into `/saya/notifications` + `/agen/notifications` + `/crew/notifications` — all three routes pass `?page=N` through. **mark-all-read still runs on every visit regardless of page** so the unread badge clears even when viewing older history. Shared `views/partials/notification-list.ejs` gets a footer with prev/next pagination links + "Halaman N dari M · total notif" copy; hidden when `pagination.pageCount === 1`. `jemaah-notifications.ejs` has its own inlined row markup (predates the partial) — got a matching pagination footer block. The legacy unpaginated `listMyNotifications` export is kept for callers that just want the recent slice (KPI count, badge, etc.).
182. ✅ Bookings cancel reason filter — `searchBookings({cancelReasonCode})` accepts the S175 BookingCancelReason enum values, `'__UNSET__'` sentinel (for cancelled rows without a category yet — admin's categorisation backlog), or `'ALL'` (default, no filter). `__UNSET__` implicitly scopes to `status IN (CANCELLED, REFUNDED)` since `cancelReasonCode` is only set on those. **Unknown codes silently fall through to no filter** (defensive — a bookmark with a renamed enum value shouldn't crash the page). New dropdown in the `/admin/bookings` filter bar between Agen and Dari; pagination URL preserves the cancel reason just like other filters. Pairs with S175 panel on `/admin` overview: admin sees "5 GOODWILL cancels last quarter" in the analytics, clicks through, lands on filtered list.
183. ✅ Refund preset percentages — quick-action buttons (25% / 50% / 75% / BALANCE 100%) above the refund amount input on `/admin/bookings/:id` refund modal. Click computes `Math.floor(paid * pct / 100)` and fills the amount field. **`Math.floor`** avoids fractional Rupiah (refund Decimal(15,2) is whole-cent strict). BALANCE button visually emphasised (gold border) since 100% is the full-refund signal that interacts with the S145 no-show ack checkbox. Pure UI — no service or schema changes. Pinned the percentage math in a test so any future server-side preset API stays consistent.
184. ✅ Booking notes text search — `searchBookings({notes})` adds a substring filter on `Booking.notes`. **Minimum 3 chars** required (silently ignored below) so the filter doesn't quietly match every row when admin types 1-2 chars in the input. Whitespace trimmed before matching. New "Cari di catatan" input in the `/admin/bookings` filter bar between bookingNo search and Status. Pagination preserves the filter across pages. Useful for "show me all bookings with 'wheelchair' note" type follow-up questions; pairs naturally with the S180 note templates (templates emit the standard phrases, search finds them later).
185. ✅ Inactive AGEN dormant flag — `AgentProfile.dormantSince DateTime?` column (migration applied). Daily cron `scan-agent-dormancy` flags ACTIVE agents with no booking + no lead activity in last `inactiveDays=60`. Auto-clears (back to null) on the next run when fresh activity is detected — agent doesn't have to manually un-flag themselves by closing a deal. **Activity = booking via the agent in window OR lead with `updatedAt >= cutoff`** (covers both new leads and follow-ups on stale ones). SUSPENDED/soft-deleted users excluded from the scan (already inactive by definition). Walk-in / Kantor-Pusat agents (no agent FK) not considered — signal is per-salesperson, not per-channel. One audit row per transition (flagged OR cleared) so compliance scans can answer "when did agent X go dormant?". 💤 red badge on `/admin/users` agent profile column when set. CLI `npm run job:scan-agent-dormancy` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/scan-agent-dormancy` + jobRunner daily interval.
186. ✅ Lead bulk mark-as-LOST — `bulkMarkLeadsLost({agentId, leadIds})` flips selected COLD/WARM leads to LOST in one shot. **Per-row ownership enforced** but cross-agent IDs **silently skipped** (not 403) — the kanban filter already scopes by agent, so a cross-agent ID arriving here is a stale browser tab or someone fuzzing; aborting the whole batch would be hostile UX for the legitimate part. Already-LOST and CONVERTED rows skipped (terminal — no transition to write). **Payload capped at 500 IDs** defensively against runaway clients. One audit row per actually-flipped lead (matches `updateLead` single-row shape so the timeline reads consistently). Floating bottom action bar in `/agen` kanban appears when ≥1 checkbox checked; "Tandai LOST" POSTs to `/api/leads/bulk-lost`. Checkbox per-card via `lead-card.ejs` partial.
187. ✅ Crew per-jemaah notes — `CrewJemaahNote(paketId, jemaahId, crewUserId, body)` model (migration applied) for crew to leave private notes per jemaah on the assigned manifest (e.g. "lansia perlu pendamping", "alergi laut"). **Composite unique on `(paketId, jemaahId, crewUserId)`** so re-save upserts in place rather than stacking rows — two different muthawwif on the same paket can each leave their own note. **Empty body deletes** the row (treated as "remove my note"). `assertJemaahOnPaket` tuple-guard: jemaah must be on this paket via a non-CANCELLED booking (anti-enumeration). Unassigned crew gets 404 NOT_ASSIGNED (mirrors the manifest access pattern). Inline `<details>` editor per row on `/crew/paket/:slug`; read-only roll-up grouped by jemaah on the admin manifest tab with "📝 from <muthawwif name>" attribution. Best-effort load on the admin side — failure to fetch crew notes doesn't 500 the whole manifest page.
188. ✅ User list AGEN tier filter — `listUsers({tier='BRONZE'|'SILVER'|'GOLD'|'PLATINUM'|'ALL'})` filters AGEN by `AgentProfile.tier`. **Implicitly narrows `role` to AGEN** when tier is set (otherwise the join would silently return nothing for non-AGEN). **Case-insensitive normalisation** so a stored lowercase tier still matches uppercase dropdown selection. **No canonical-validation** — unknown tiers (e.g. future "DIAMOND") still filter; no rows match, but the query doesn't error. New dropdown next to the existing deleted-filter on `/admin/users` filter bar; RESET link appears when any non-default filter is applied. Pairs with the S185 dormant badge so OWNER can scan "GOLD agents who went dormant" in one query.
189. ✅ Lead reactivation button — `reactivateLead({leadId})` un-archives a soft-deleted lead from the S59 hint panel on `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`. Clears `deletedAt` + **flips status back to COLD** (re-engagement is fresh contact, not continuation of WARM heat). Already-active leads return `{reactivated:false, reason:'already_active'}` idempotently — no audit pollution. CONVERTED leads blocked with 409 `LEAD_TERMINAL` even when soft-deleted (already became a booking). **`agentId` stays the same** — reactivation keeps the original ownership; admin acts on behalf of the agent, doesn't re-attribute. Audit row stamps `reactivated: true` so timeline scans can answer "which leads came back from the dead?". Per-row "↻ Aktifkan" button in the archived-leads table; CONVERTED rows show "terkunci" placeholder instead of the button.
190. ✅ Per-paket FAQ — `PaketFaq(paketId, question, answer, sortOrder)` model (migration applied) for admin-curated Q&A per paket. JSON CRUD via `/api/paket/:slug/faqs` (3-role gate). Inline table editor on paket-edit form with per-row Save/Delete + footer add-row; rendered as collapsible `<details>` accordion on `/p/:slug` below the hero. **Falls back to hardcoded defaults** when no curated FAQs exist (so empty fresh paket still gets a sensible "paspor harus aktif berapa bulan?" et al.). Sort by `sortOrder asc, createdAt asc` so admin controls priority + ties broken by creation order. First-entry auto-open via `i === 0` so jemaah sees one answered question without clicking. CRUD operations write audit rows with before/after diffs.
191. ✅ Manifest age-bracket counts — `computeAgeBuckets({bookings, departureDate})` pure-JS pass over already-loaded bookings; counts pax into Anak (<12y) / Dewasa (12-59y) / Lansia (≥60y) / Unknown (missing birthDate) buckets. **paxCount-aware**: a 3-pax family booking with adult lead jemaah counts 3 toward dewasa (matches "one row per booking" manifest convention). **Excludes CANCELLED + REFUNDED** so the strip reflects "who's actually going". **Age computed at paket `departureDate`**, not "now" — a 59-year-old today departing next year shows as 60 (lansia) which matches what crew needs to plan for at the time of the trip. Same-day birthday counts as that year. Lansia cell gold-bordered + bold (operationally significant — wheelchair / ihram help / slower walks). Loaded inside `getManifestForPaket` as a best-effort attached field so a compute error doesn't 500 the manifest page.
192. ✅ Per-paket announcement banner — `PaketAnnouncement(paketId, title, body, publishedAt, expiresAt, authorId)` model (migration applied) for admin pinned messages to jemaah on this paket. Multiple announcements per paket allowed. `listActiveAnnouncements({paketId, now})` filters `publishedAt <= now AND (expiresAt == null OR expiresAt > now)` — admin can schedule future announcements + set expiry to auto-hide stale ones. JSON CRUD via `/api/paket/:slug/announcements` (3-role gate). Banner renders on `/saya/bookings/:id` above the info panel as gold-bordered card with 📢 prefix; multiple banners stack newest-first. `null` expiresAt means "never expires" (sticky pinned). Per-CRUD audit rows; `authorId` FK uses SetNull on User delete so deleting an admin doesn't cascade-delete their announcements.
193. ✅ Push notif for paket announcements — `createAnnouncement` fires a push notif to every active jemaah on the paket via the S93 `pushToUser` fan-out. **Gated on `publishedAt <= now`** — scheduled-future announcements don't push until they go live (admin would need a separate cron to handle that handoff, deferred). Distinct `userIds` deduplicated (one jemaah with multiple bookings on the same paket gets one push, not N). Anonymous bookings (`jemaahUserId=null`) skipped — no push target. **Fire-and-forget** posture: a push failure logs but doesn't abort the announcement create transaction; the on-page banner is the load-bearing surface and push is purely additive. Body preview truncated to 140 chars (browser notification body limit). Payload includes `data.announcementId` so the SW handler can wire deep-link to `/saya` on click.
194. ✅ Public paket SEO/OG meta tags — `buildPaketSeo(paket, agent, {baseUrl, dateFormatter})` returns `{url, title, description, image, locale}` for the `<head>` block of `/p/:slug`. **Description sanitisation**: strips HTML tags, collapses whitespace, truncates to 160 chars (Twitter cuts around 200, Facebook 300 — 160 keeps the preview clean across all surfaces). Falls back to a generic "Paket X bersama Religio Pro. Berangkat YYYY-MM-DD, N hari." line when `heroDescription` is unset. URL uses `PUBLIC_BASE_URL` env when set (absolute), otherwise relative `/p/<slug>` (still valid for crawlers landing through a direct link). Agent slug URL-encoded into `?a=` param for referral attribution. Includes Open Graph (`og:type`, `og:url`, `og:title`, `og:description`, `og:image`, `og:site_name`, `og:locale=id_ID`) + Twitter Card (`summary_large_image`). Default OG image at `/shared/og-default.jpg` (admin uploads to override).
195. ✅ Booking voucher QR code — `drawQrCode(doc, text, {x, y, size, errorCorrectionLevel='M', dark, light=null})` renders a QR code into a pdfkit document using the `qrcode` package's synchronous `create()` API + filled rectangles per module. `errorCorrectionLevel='M'` (~15% recovery) is the sweet spot for printed vouchers — survives small coffee spills and folds. `light=null` keeps the QR background transparent so the voucher's cream background shows through. Wired into `bookingVoucherPdf.js` at top-right (460,140) as an 80pt square encoding `${PUBLIC_BASE_URL}/admin/bookings/<id>` so crew/admin scans at airport check-in to pull up the admin booking detail. Caption "SCAN UNTUK CEK-IN" below. **Best-effort** — QR generation failure logs but doesn't abort the voucher PDF (the voucher is the load-bearing artifact). New `qrcode` dep (~50KB pure-JS, no native bins). **S197 updated** the QR URL to point at the public verification page.
196. ✅ Per-paket pickup points — `PaketPickup(paketId, label, address, departTime, notes, sortOrder)` model (migration applied) for multiple bus pickup locations per paket (Bekasi/Bogor/Tangerang). JSON CRUD via `/api/paket/:slug/pickups` (3-role gate). Inline table editor on paket-edit; rendered as 240px-wide card grid on `/saya/bookings/:id` with ⏰ time + 📍 address + optional italic notes. **`departTime` is a freeform `VarChar(5)`** rather than strict TIME — admin might type "05:00" or "5:30" and we accept both; tighter validation can come later. Sort by `sortOrder asc, createdAt asc` so admin controls display order, ties broken by creation. Empty `departTime` stored as null (not empty string). Per-CRUD audit rows.
197. ✅ Public QR verification page — `/v/<bookingId>?sig=<hex16>` route. `buildVerifyUrl(bookingId)` signs the booking ID via HMAC-SHA256 (key=`env.JWT_SECRET`, payload=`voucher:<id>`, truncated to 16 hex chars matching the S77 emailClickToken convention). `verifyVoucherSig` uses `timingSafeEqual` to prevent timing attacks. View shows MINIMAL info on valid scans: bookingNo + paket title + **first-name only** + departureDate + kelas/pax + status (no PII reveal even on a leaked URL). Invalid signature → "VOUCHER PALSU" page explaining the likely causes (edited photo, manual URL entry, deleted). `<meta name="robots" content="noindex,nofollow">` so verify URLs don't pollute search results. NO auth required — the QR is the credential. S195's voucher PDF QR now encodes this URL instead of the admin booking URL, so anyone (airport staff, crew without app, jemaah confirming their own voucher) can verify authenticity.
198. ✅ Voucher print history — `Booking.voucherPrintCount` + `lastVoucherPrintedAt` + `lastVoucherPrintedByEmail` columns (migration applied). `recordVoucherPrint({bookingId, actorEmail})` bumps the counter + stamps `now()` + records the actor's email on each voucher download. Wired into both `/admin/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf` (admin email) and `/saya/bookings/:id/voucher.pdf` (jemaah email) via `res.on('finish')` (fire-and-forget AFTER the response so latency isn't affected). **Counter pattern** chosen over a full history table — the count is enough signal for the support workflow ("voucher printed 3× already, ask before reissuing"). Best-effort: missing booking row → swallowed by the helper's try/catch (defensive). Surfaced on `/admin/bookings/:id` as a small `Nx` badge on the PDF download button + `title` hover with timestamp + actor email.
199. ✅ Print manifest age column — `getPrintManifest` now attaches `jemaah.age` + `jemaah.ageBracket` (`ANAK`/`DEWASA`/`LANSIA`/`UNKNOWN`) per row using S191's `computeAge` helper. Age computed at `paket.departureDate` (not "now") — matches what crew needs to plan for at the time of the trip. New "Umur" column in the print worksheet shows `{age}y` + bracket label; **Lansia rows gold-bordered + gold background** for operational planning (wheelchair, ihram help). Anak rows get subtle blue tint. Header KPI strip now includes `Nlansia · Manak` when either is >0; hidden when only dewasa. UNKNOWN bracket (null birthDate) renders as "—" plain. CANCELLED/REFUNDED already excluded by the existing query so they don't pollute the age math either.
200. ✅ Bulk room assignment by floor — `bulkAssignRoomsByFloor({paketId, floor})` greedy first-fit: for each unassigned booking (createdAt asc — earliest jemaah get first dibs), find the first room on `floor` with matching kelas + remaining capacity ≥ paxCount, assign. **Whole call non-transactional** — each assign is its own DB write + audit row; partial success is fine (admin re-runs to pick up freed rooms). Returns `{assigned[], skipped[], errors[]}` per-row so the UI shows "5 assigned, 2 skipped (capacity), 1 error". CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings ignored (closed). Per-assigned audit row stamps `bulkAssignByFloor: true` + `floor: N` so timeline scans can answer "which bookings did bulk-assign touch?". Per-floor `⇣ Bulk-assign` button in the bunking-tab `<h3>` — only rendered when there are unassigned bookings AND the floor is numeric.
201. ✅ Audit log content search — `listAudits({q})` adds substring matching across `entityId` + `before` JSON + `after` JSON. **Two-phase query**: raw `$queryRaw` finds matching audit IDs via `CAST(\`before\` AS CHAR(8000)) LIKE pattern` + same for after (backticked since `before`/`after` are MariaDB reserved keywords), then the regular Prisma `where: { id: { in } }` applies the rest of the filters (entity/action/actorEmail/date) over that bounded set. **≥3 chars required** (silently ignored below) to avoid scanning the whole table on stray keystrokes. LIKE wildcards (`%`/`_`/`\\`) escaped so literal underscores in IDs/UUIDs match correctly. **Hard cap 5000 candidate IDs** so a too-broad query can't OOM. New "Cari konten (≥3 char)" input in the `/admin/audit` filter bar; preserved across pagination + export CSV. Useful for compliance ("find every audit mentioning UUID X" / "find every booking note containing 'wheelchair'").
202. ✅ Booking pickup choice — `Booking.pickupId` FK to `PaketPickup` (S196), `onDelete: SetNull` so removing an obsolete pickup falls back to "TBD" rather than cascading the booking away. `setMyBookingPickup({userId, bookingId, pickupId})` validates: booking owned by user, pickup belongs to booking's paket (PICKUP_MISMATCH on cross-paket), CANCELLED/REFUNDED rejected. **Idempotent re-pick** returns `{updated:false}` so no audit pollution from double-tap. **null clears** the choice (also idempotent). Per-pick audit row stamps `pickupChosen: true` + label so the timeline reads "jemaah chose Bekasi". Jemaah-side UI: click-a-card on `/saya/bookings/:id` posts to `/api/saya/bookings/:id/pickup`; current selection gold-bordered; "batalkan pilihan" link clears with confirm.
203. ✅ Passport renewal reminder — daily cron emails + WAs jemaah whose `JemaahProfile.passportExpiry` is within 90 days (Saudi rule: passport must be valid ≥6 months after departure, so 90 days early gives queue time). **Distinct from S173 `DOC_EXPIRING_SOON`** — that one walks `JemaahDocument.expiresAt`, but many jemaah carry passport metadata on the profile (`passportNo`+`passportExpiry`) without a `JemaahDocument` row, so doc-expiring sweep misses them. This service walks the profile directly. Per-jemaah 30-day cooldown via the Notification table — 90d window with 30d cooldown means jemaah gets at most 3 nudges before actual expiry. **Walks JemaahProfile not Booking** so re-bookings don't generate duplicate nudges per jemaah. Respects `notifEmail` opt-out at the DB filter (saves a roundtrip). Suspended/soft-deleted users excluded. Soonest-expiring first. New `PASSPORT_RENEWAL_REMINDER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-passport-renewal` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-passport-renewal` + jobRunner daily interval.
204. ✅ Per-user audit activity timeline — `getUserActivityFeed({userId, limit=50})` returns recent `AuditLog` entries where this user was the actor. Rendered as a compact table panel on `/admin/users/:id/edit` (Owner asks "what has this kasir been doing?" without leaving the page). Shows action / entity / target ID / IP / timestamp. **Action color-coded** (CREATE emerald, UPDATE gold, DELETE ruby). Last-8 chars of `entityId` shown to keep the column compact; Booking entityIds get a deep link to `/admin/bookings/<id>` for one-click drill-down. Limit capped at 200 (default 20 on edit page); negative or zero limit floors to 1. Footer link to `/admin/audit?actorEmail=<email>` for full pagination of older history. Empty state when user has no audited actions. Best-effort load — a query failure dims the panel via null, doesn't 500 the edit page.
205. ✅ Pickup summary + manifest filter — `getManifestForPaket` now attaches a `pickupCounts` array (one row per pickup label + `paxCount` + `count`) computed in JS from already-loaded bookings (no extra query). CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded. **TBD bucket always rendered last** regardless of size so admin always sees the "who hasn't picked yet" backlog. `filterManifestByPickup(result, pickupId)` returns a shallow copy with `bookings` narrowed; `'__TBD__'` sentinel targets unchosen. Admin manifest tab gets a clickable count strip (per-pickup card + reset link); URL preserves `?manifestPickup=` so paging/exports stay scoped.
206. ✅ Booking note pin/unpin — `Booking.notesPinned` boolean column (migration applied, default false). `toggleBookingNotesPinned({bookingId, pinned})` flips the flag; **idempotent re-pin** returns `{updated:false}` (no audit pollution from double-tap); **EMPTY_NOTES 409** when trying to pin a booking with no notes (no point pinning empty content). Per-flip audit row stamps `field: 'notesPinned'`. Pinned notes render at the very top of `/admin/bookings/:id` as a gold-bordered banner with 📌 prefix + "Unpin" button; above all other panels so urgent context (VIP, prior dispute warnings, special handling) isn't buried. "📌 Pin catatan ini" button next to SIMPAN on the notes form when notes exist + not yet pinned. Same RBAC as note editing (CANCEL_ROLES).
207. ✅ Crew portal task list — crew's `/crew` dashboard now shows their own open `Task` rows (S91) via `getMyOpenTasks({assigneeEmail: crew.email})`. Read-only on this surface — admin still owns create/complete/cancel; crew sees the work assigned to them at a glance. Sorted by `dueAt asc, createdAt asc` so overdue/imminent bubble to the top. **Overdue rows ruby-bordered**; count surfaced in panel header ("8 tugas terbuka · 3 overdue"). Each row shows bookingNo + jemaah name + paket title + due date + createdByEmail. Best-effort load — task query failure dims the panel via null, doesn't 500 the dashboard.
208. ✅ Pickup roster CSV — `buildPickupRosterCsv(paketSlug, {pickupId})` per-paket export grouped by pickup point so bus drivers download a roster before departure to verify who they're picking up. Reuses S205's pickup grouping + same `__TBD__` sentinel for jemaah without a choice. Rows sorted by pickup `sortOrder asc` (admin-controlled display order), `TBD bucket always last` regardless of size. CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 quoting + CRLF (matches the convention). Per-pickup footer summary line (e.g. `Bekasi=2; Bogor=1; TBD=3`). Optional `pickupId` query (or `__TBD__`) narrows to one bus route so each driver only downloads their own list. Filename `pickup_roster_<slug>[_<pickup>].csv` sanitised against path traversal. Route `/admin/manifest/:slug/pickup-roster.csv` inherits the existing 3-role gate via `/admin` mount. "🚌 Roster pickup" button in the manifest tab toolbar preserves the active pickup filter from the URL.
209. ✅ Booking dup-check by NIK — extends S167's phone-based dup warning to also check `JemaahProfile.nik` so walk-in admins catch duplicate bookings even when the jemaah uses a different phone (family-shared phones make phone-only matching noisy). New `findRecentBookingsByNik({nik, windowDays=90})` does exact equality match (NIK is a 16-digit national ID, no fuzzy/endsWith needed). Returns empty when NIK <10 digits (avoids partial-NIK scans matching too much). `POST /admin/bookings` runs parallel phone + NIK lookups, merges results via a `flagsById` Map (booking flagged 'phone', 'nik', or both). **Severity coloring**: NIK matches get ruby border ("kemungkinan jemaah yang sama") since NIK is a unique person ID; phone-only stays gold (family share is plausible). Per-row badge shows TEL / NIK / TEL+NIK flag chips. `NewBookingSchema` accepts optional `nik` field with 3-state preprocessor (whitespace cleanup, 16-digit pattern validation).
210. ✅ Jemaah dietary preferences — `JemaahProfile.dietary` enum (REGULAR / VEGETARIAN / HALAL_STRICT / SOFT_TEXTURE / DIABETIC / OTHER, migration applied) + `dietaryNotes VARCHAR(500)` for catering / hotel meal planning. **REGULAR is default** (back-compat — existing rows + new anonymous bookings stay neutral). SOFT_TEXTURE for elderly jemaah who can't chew well; DIABETIC for sugar control; OTHER + notes for everything else (allergies, vegan-strict, kosher-equivalent). Wired into both admin (`/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`) and jemaah self-service (`/saya/profile`) form panels. **3-state preprocessor** for the schema: `undefined` (form omitted) → no change; explicit empty → clear (dietary resets to REGULAR, notes to NULL); value → set. Manifest table on admin overview renders a colored dietary pill **only when non-REGULAR** (REGULAR is the default — catering doesn't need a callout for the silent majority) with hover tooltip carrying the free-text `dietaryNotes`. Pill colors: emerald VEG / gold HALAL+ / amber SOFT / ruby DIAB / sapphire other. Crew manifest also includes the fields so muthawwif can flag special meals to hotels on arrival.
