Voucher PDF deliberately omits dietary — not part of the customer-facing handout, lives only in operational surfaces.
211. ✅ Dietary roll-up CSV — `buildDietaryRollupCsv(paketSlug)` per-paket export for catering / hotel kitchen brief. Two sections in one file: per-jemaah list of non-REGULAR diets (bookingNo / name / kelas / room / dietary / notes), and a footer line with per-category pax tally (`REGULAR=120; VEGETARIAN=3; DIABETIC=1`). **REGULAR rows excluded from per-jemaah list** — kitchen only cares about the exceptions; the tally still counts them so the standard-meal volume is visible. **Sort by dietary code then jemaah name** so all DIABETIC rows group together (kitchen processes one category at a time). CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded (already off the trip). UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 + CRLF matches the convention. Route `/admin/manifest/:slug/dietary.csv` inherits the 3-role gate. "🍽 Diet CSV" button in the manifest tab toolbar alongside the export + pickup roster + cetak buttons.
212. ✅ Pickup point capacity — `PaketPickup.maxCapacity` column (migration applied) caps total pax per bus. **NULL = no cap** (back-compat default — existing rows + admin who hasn't set a limit work unchanged). Clamped 1..200 at schema validation. S202 `setMyBookingPickup` adds an aggregation check: sum of `paxCount` on the target pickup (excluding the current booking when re-picking) + current booking's pax must not exceed cap, else 409 `PICKUP_FULL` with the occupied/cap numbers in the message. **Excludes current booking from the sum** so re-picking the same pickup at cap is a clean no-op (idempotent) and switching FROM a full pickup TO another is allowed (jemaah's own seat doesn't count against the destination). CANCELLED/REFUNDED don't occupy a seat. New `listPickupsWithOccupancy(paketId)` decorates each row with `occupiedPax` + `isFull` via one `groupBy` aggregation (no N+1). Jemaah-side: `/saya/bookings/:id` renders a "PENUH" ruby pill on full pickups, dimmed + non-clickable; capacity `N/M pax` line shows under the address when cap is set. Paket-edit pickup table gets a "Cap" number input column for inline edit.
213. ✅ Crew dietary brief email — Monday morning email per (assigned MUTHAWWIF × paket departing within `windowDays=14`) listing every non-REGULAR jemaah on the paket so muthawwif can brief the hotel kitchen on arrival. New `CREW_DIETARY_BRIEF` enum (migration applied). Body groups specials by dietary code (DIABETIC section, VEGETARIAN section, etc.) with one row per jemaah carrying full name + room + free-text dietary notes. Header summary: total pax / special pax / per-category tally. **Silent on three cases**: crew has no email (no point queueing), zero specials on the paket (all-REGULAR brief carries no signal — kitchen doesn't need an empty list), enqueue failure. SUSPENDED + soft-deleted crew excluded; ARCHIVED + soft-deleted paket excluded. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings not in specials. Crew with multiple near-departure paket get one email per paket — keeps each brief focused on one hotel. CLI `npm run job:send-crew-dietary-brief` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-crew-dietary-brief` + jobRunner weekly interval. Pattern: per-crew failure caught in batch so a bad row doesn't abort the run.
214. ✅ Crew portal dietary panel — `getAssignedManifest` decorates the return value with `dietarySummary: {tally, specials, totalPax, specialPax}` so muthawwif sees the S213 brief inline on `/crew/paket/:slug`, not just in the Monday email. Tally counts ALL pax including REGULAR (gives standard-meal volume); specials list excludes REGULAR (kitchen brief only cares about exceptions). Panel renders gold-bordered above the booking table, grouped by dietary code with one row per jemaah carrying full name + room + free-text notes. **Hidden when zero specials** so all-REGULAR trips don't waste real estate. Mirrors S211 CSV / S213 email layout so crew + admin + kitchen see the same numbers in three places.
215. ✅ Manifest dietary filter — `filterManifestByDietary(result, dietary)` narrows the admin manifest table by `?manifestDietary=` query param. Supports exact codes (REGULAR / VEGETARIAN / etc.), `__SPECIAL__` aggregate (all non-REGULAR — useful for "show me everyone the kitchen needs to know about"), and `ALL` / empty to clear. **Unknown codes silently fall through to unfiltered** (defensive against bookmark with renamed enum). **Null/missing dietary counts as REGULAR** — pre-S210 jemaah rows show up under the REGULAR filter, not vanish into a separate bucket. Composes on top of the S205 pickup filter (both shallow-copy the bookings array, so filter order doesn't matter). Dropdown in the manifest tab toolbar; active filter renders a gold chip with reset link next to the pickup reset.
216. ✅ Announcement EMAIL broadcast — `createAnnouncement` now also enqueues one EMAIL per distinct active jemaah on the paket alongside the existing S193 push fan-out, so jemaah who haven't installed the `/saya` PWA still get the announcement in their inbox. Belt+suspenders for critical messages (visa updates, schedule changes). Uses **GENERIC** notif type (admin body is final text — no template variables to interpolate). **Dedupe by (userId or jemaahProfileId)** so one jemaah with multiple bookings on the same paket gets one email, not N. Anonymous bookings without email skipped. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded. `recipientUserId` set when booking is linked so `/saya/notifications` inbox + unread badge surfaces the row. **Gated on `publishedAt <= now`** (same condition as the push) so scheduled-future announcements don't fan out until they go live. **Fire-and-forget** — email failure logged but doesn't abort the announcement create transaction (announcement row is the load-bearing artifact). `relatedEntity='PaketAnnouncement'` + `relatedEntityId` so admin can grep notif queue per-announcement.
217. ✅ Dietary in manifest CSV — `exportManifestCsv` extended with two new columns at the end: `Dietary` (enum code) + `Dietary Notes` (free-text). Pairs with S210/S211 — the dedicated dietary CSV (S211) is a tightly-filtered kitchen brief; this exposes the same data on the full manifest export so admin can grep/pivot a single file. **`null` dietary renders as REGULAR** (pre-S210 jemaah default — keeps the column non-blank and honest about the default). **`null` notes render as empty cell** (not literal `"null"` string). Notes containing commas are quoted per RFC 4180 (same convention as the rest of the export).
218. ✅ Crew portal: paket announcements visible — `/crew/paket/:slug` route loads admin-posted announcements (S192 `listActiveAnnouncements`) and renders them gold-bordered above the dietary panel so crew gets the same heads-up jemaah do ("visa delayed", "pickup time moved"). Crew often needs the same operational news — no role-specific surface for it before. Active-only filter (publishedAt ≤ now AND (expiresAt null OR > now)) matches the jemaah-side `/saya/bookings/:id` panel. Best-effort load — query failure dims the panel via empty array, doesn't 500 the manifest page. **No write surface** — admin still owns CRUD via paket-edit panel.
219. ✅ Pickup choice reminder cron — daily email + WA reminder for active bookings on a soon-departing paket (≤14d default) where the jemaah hasn't picked a pickup yet. New `PICKUP_REMINDER` enum (migration applied). Per-booking 5-day cooldown via the Notification table — 14-day window with 5-day cooldown means max ~3 nudges before takeoff. **Silent on three cases**: paket has zero curated pickup points (admin hasn't set up routes yet — can't remind about something that doesn't exist), jemaah has neither email nor phone, recently-nudged within cooldown. Fires BOTH EMAIL + WA when contacts present (each respects per-channel opt-out via `enqueueNotification`). Soonest-departing first so a future per-run quota hits the urgent ones. `recipientUserId` set when booking is linked so `/saya/notifications` inbox surfaces it. CLI `npm run job:send-pickup-reminder` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-pickup-reminder` + jobRunner daily interval. Walks Booking (not JemaahProfile) since pickup choice is per-booking.
220. ✅ Per-pickup driver info — `PaketPickup.driverName + driverPhone + plateNumber` columns (migration applied; all nullable, admin may not know driver at create). Jemaah sees driver contact below the address on their **chosen** pickup card only (other pickups in the picker don't leak the driver phone to non-passengers). S208 pickup roster CSV gains 3 columns at the start so each driver self-identifies on the roster spreadsheet they download. PickupSchema **uppercases plate** at write (canonical `B 1234 CDE` format). Empty string at all three preprocessors → `null` clear. Paket-edit pickup table gains a sub-row beneath each main row with `driverName / driverPhone / plateNumber` inputs; the Save button reads both rows via shared `data-pickup-id`.
221. ✅ Admin sets pickup on booking — `adminSetBookingPickup({bookingId, pickupId})` mirrors the S202 jemaah self-pick but **without the `jemaahUserId` ownership requirement** (admin route enforces RBAC via `CANCEL_ROLES`). Walk-in / phone bookings can now get a pickup assigned without the jemaah needing a `/saya` account. Same guards: cross-paket pickup rejected (`PICKUP_MISMATCH`), capacity full rejected (`PICKUP_FULL` — S212), CANCELLED/REFUNDED rejected (`BOOKING_CLOSED`). Audit row stamps `adminSet: true` (vs S202's `pickupChosen: true`) so the timeline can distinguish admin assignment from jemaah self-pick. `POST /admin/bookings/:id/pickup` route + form on booking-detail with dropdown showing each pickup's occupancy `(N/M)` and `· PENUH` tag (disabled option) so admin sees the cap state inline. Idempotent re-set + null-clear are both no-ops (no audit pollution).
222. ✅ Per-paket WhatsApp group link — `Paket.waGroupUrl VARCHAR(500)` column (migration applied; nullable). Admin curates the invite URL on paket-edit (validated as http(s) URL via Zod). **Jemaah sees a "Gabung grup WA" emerald CTA on `/saya/bookings/:id` only when LUNAS** — speculative bookings that might cancel don't get group access. Crew sees a "Grup WA" button on `/crew/paket/:slug` regardless of attendance state (they need it for trip coordination). Both surfaces open in a new tab with `rel="noopener nofollow"`. Same 3-state preprocessor as `costPerPaxIdr` / `adsSpendIdr` — undefined preserves, empty clears, value sets.
223. ✅ Per-paket required documents — `Paket.requiredDocs Json` column (migration applied; nullable JSON array). Different paket types need different visas (Saudi umroh needs VISA_UMROH + VACCINE_MENINGITIS; Turkey/Aqsa doesn't). S23 `getPreDepartureChecklist` now resolves the per-paket list via `resolveRequiredDocs(paket.requiredDocs)` instead of hardcoding 4 doc checks. **Always-present checks** (passport identity + room + emergency contact = 4) survive regardless; **variable checks** (one boolean per required doc) extend the total. **Score weights all checks equally** so trimming docs lifts the score — admin who configures a Turkey paket without manasik doesn't see jemaah penalised for a missing cert that doesn't apply. NULL / empty array → fall back to `DEFAULT_REQUIRED_DOCS` (`['VISA_UMROH','VACCINE_MENINGITIS','HEALTH_CERT','MANASIK_CERT']`) for back-compat with pre-S223 paket. Schema preprocessor accepts CSV string OR array; empty array → null (clear); unknown enum strings + PASSPORT (handled as identity check, not doc upload) filtered out at read. Paket-edit form gets a checkbox grid + helper text explaining what each doc is for.
224. ✅ Decline jemaah cancel request — admin can explicitly decline a pending S5ff cancel request without cancelling the booking. `declineCancelRequest({bookingId, reason})` clears the 3 `cancelRequest*` fields, writes an audit row with `cancelRequestDeclined: true` + admin's reason, and fires a GENERIC EMAIL+WA notif to the jemaah explaining the decline. **Closes the loop on hanging requests** — pre-S224 the only outcomes were approve (cancelBooking) or leave indefinite, which confused jemaah (their /saya kept showing "pending") and polluted the needs-attention surface. Refuses on no pending request (`NO_PENDING_REQUEST` 409), already-closed booking (`ALREADY_CLOSED` 409), and missing reason <3 chars (`DECLINE_REASON_REQUIRED` 400 — admin must justify the decline). `POST /admin/bookings/:id/cancel-request/decline` route (`CANCEL_ROLES` gate). Inline `<details>` form on the cancel-request banner in `/admin/bookings/:id`. Notif failure logged but doesn't abort the decline.
225. ✅ Bulk retry FAILED notifications — admin selects multiple terminal-FAILED rows on `/admin/notifications` and one click retries them all via the new floating bottom action bar. `bulkRetryFailedNotifications({ids, limit=200})` resets `attemptCount=0` + clears `nextRetryAt` + dispatches each. **Per-row failure caught** so a bad row doesn't abort the batch. **Non-FAILED rows in the input silently skip** (no error) — admin who clicks retry on a row another admin just handled doesn't see a confusing error. Returns counters `{requested, eligible, retried, failed, skipped}` so the redirect flash shows real numbers. UI uses an outer `<form id="notif-bulk-form">` + `form="..."` attribute on each row's checkbox (HTML disallows nested forms; the per-row Send buttons inside `<td>` still work). Select-all header checkbox supports indeterminate state. Caps at 200 ids per request to avoid runaway.
226. ✅ Booking tags — `Booking.tags Json` column (migration applied; nullable JSON array). Short uppercase labels (VIP / LANSIA / HONEYMOON / KELUARGA / KESEHATAN / PERTAMA / DIFABEL / PRIORITAS — preset chips) for fast visual identification + future manifest filter. `setBookingTags` writes via `normaliseBookingTags` which uppercases, trims, dedupes, validates `/^[A-Z0-9_-]+$/`, caps each tag at 24 chars + array at 8 entries. **Empty list clears to NULL** (back-compat read path stays simple). **Idempotent re-save → no audit pollution** (skip-when-same convention). Refuses on CANCELLED/REFUNDED (`BOOKING_CLOSED` — tags are an active-booking concern, history is frozen). `POST /admin/bookings/:id/tags` route (`CANCEL_ROLES`). Booking-detail page renders gold pills + a CSV-input form with preset chip buttons that append to the input.
227. ✅ Auto-publish scheduled paket — daily cron flips DRAFT paket to ACTIVE when `publishedAt <= now`. Admin pre-schedules a launch by setting publishedAt to a future date while keeping status=DRAFT; this cron handles the handoff on the day so admin doesn't have to remember to flip the status. **Sanity guards** at query level: departure must still be in the future (no point activating a paket whose trip already happened), `kursiTotal > 0` (can't sell a 0-seat paket), `deletedAt: null`. Per-paket failure caught so a bad row doesn't abort the batch. Silent on quiet days (no candidates → no audit row). System actor uses `id=null` + `email='system'` for the audit row; the durable distinguisher from admin manual activation is `after.autoPublished: true`. CLI `npm run job:auto-publish-paket` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/auto-publish-paket` + jobRunner daily interval.
228. ✅ Pickup info on crew manifest — `/crew/paket/:slug` extends the per-row table with a Pickup column showing each jemaah's chosen pickup label + departure time (TBD amber when unchosen). Adds a `pickupSummary` rollup panel at the top: per-pickup card with pax count + departTime + colour-coded left border (gold for chosen, amber for TBD). **TBD bucket always last** regardless of size (mirrors S205 admin convention) so crew sees the unfinished work clearly. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded — the manifest is "who's actually going", same money-stripped + non-leaking pattern as the rest of the crew view. **Key fix**: `pickupId` scalar must be in the Prisma select alongside the `pickup` relation; missing the scalar collapses all bookings into one bucket with the first row's label (Prisma populates the relation but not the FK column by default).
229. ✅ Manifest tag filter — `filterManifestByTag(result, tag)` narrows the admin manifest table by `?manifestTag=` query param. **Case-insensitive** (lowercase input → uppercase match). Composes with the existing pickup + dietary filters (each shallow-copies the bookings array; filter order doesn't matter). Unknown tags silently return zero-row result rather than falling through to unfiltered — admin who bookmarks `?manifestTag=NONEXISTENT` sees an honest empty list, not a misleading full manifest. Tag dropdown options derived from the **raw** manifest (before filtering) so admin still sees every available tag even when narrowed. Clickable tag pills on each manifest row deep-link to `?manifestTag=<tag>`. Active filter chip + reset link mirror the S215 dietary pattern.
230. ✅ Booking tag aggregate KPI — `getBookingTagRollup()` aggregates active (non-CANCELLED/REFUNDED) bookings across non-archived paket and emits per-tag rows with `{tag, bookings, paxCount, paketCount}`. Sort by `paxCount desc` then `tag asc` so the operationally heaviest labels bubble to the top. **`paketCount` = distinct paket carrying the tag** (a VIP across 3 trips signals different operational planning than a VIP concentrated on one paket). DB-level `tags: { not: null }` filter cuts the result set on the typical case (most bookings untagged). Panel on `/admin` overview between cancel-reason and komisi monthly; renders one card per tag with pax/booking/paket counts. Hidden when nothing is tagged (no real-estate waste on quiet weeks). Best-effort load — query failure dims the panel via null, doesn't 500 the overview.
231. ✅ Booking tags on crew manifest — `/crew/paket/:slug` per-row table renders gold-bordered tag pills below the jemaah name when `Booking.tags` is non-empty. Read-only (admin still owns CRUD via S226 booking-detail) — muthawwif sees VIP/LANSIA/etc. at the curb without leaving the portal. **`tags: true` added to both `select` blocks in crewPortal.js** — `getAssignedManifest` and `buildCrewManifestCsv` (the latter for offline-friendly CSV export). CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings already filtered upstream so they're not visible regardless of tags.
232-234. ✅ Booking tag autopilot — `bookingAutoTag.js` computes 3 tags from data already on the booking: **LANSIA** (S232 — jemaah age ≥ 60 at paket departureDate; birthday-aware), **PERTAMA** (S233 — jemaah has zero prior LUNAS bookings on any paket), **KELUARGA** (S234 — ≥3 active bookings on the same paket share an `emergencyContact`). New `Booking.autoTaggedSeen Json` column (migration applied) tracks which auto-tags have already been computed for a booking. **Additive only** — auto-tag never replaces admin's S226 manual tags, only appends. **"No re-add" rule**: if admin removes an auto-tag, `autoTaggedSeen` still records it; next pass sees it's been computed before and missing now, and respects admin's choice (no fight loop). **KELUARGA retro-tag**: when the Nth booking trips the threshold, `retroTagKeluargaCohort` fans out and tags the prior cohort members with the same EC on the same paket (additive + "no re-add" applies to them too). Auto-tag fires from `createBooking` (fire-and-forget — booking is load-bearing, tag failure logged but doesn't abort). Daily `backfill-auto-tags` cron + CLI `npm run job:backfill-auto-tags` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/backfill-auto-tags` covers missed firings + new signals (e.g. jemaah's first LUNAS retroactively activates PERTAMA on their NEXT booking, not this one). CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings refused (frozen history). Per-row failure caught in batch.
235. ✅ Refund reason code — `Payment.refundReasonCode VARCHAR(40)` column (migration applied; nullable) on the negative-amount refund row. Service-side allowlist (REFUND_REASON_CODES): `JEMAAH_REQUEST / PAKET_CANCELLED / VISA_REJECTED / JEMAAH_ILL / DOCUMENT_INCOMPLETE / NO_SHOW_REFUND / GOODWILL / DUPLICATE_PAYMENT / FRAUD_CHARGEBACK / OTHER`. **VARCHAR not enum** so adding codes later doesn't need a migration. Case-insensitive normalisation; empty string → NULL. `issueRefund` accepts optional `reasonCode` arg, validates against the allowlist (`BAD_REFUND_REASON_CODE` 400 on typo), persists on the Payment row + propagates into the audit row. Refund modal on `/admin/bookings/:id` gets a dropdown above the free-text reason; admin who picks "OTHER" gives the free-text below. Pre-S235 refund rows keep `refundReasonCode=NULL` — back-compat for analytics that bucket NULL as "(tanpa kode)".
236. ✅ Refund analytics by reason code — `getRefundAnalytics` extended with `perReasonCode` rollup: per-code refund total + count + share% of total refunded in the window. **NULL `refundReasonCode` buckets under `__UNSET__` sentinel** (mirrors S175 cancel reason convention) so admin sees the categorisation backlog — pre-S235 rows + skipped-dropdown rows surface as "(tanpa kode)". Sort by refunded desc with `__UNSET__` always last regardless of size, so categorised data dominates the visual ranking. Panel renders below the per-paket + per-agent columns on the existing refund analytics card on `/admin` overview; hidden when nothing refunded (parent panel already handles that gate).
237. ✅ Auto-cancel stale unpaid PENDING — daily cron walks PENDING bookings older than `staleDays=14` with `paidAmount=0` and flips them to CANCELLED via the canonical `cancelBooking` path. Frees kursi for future jemaah without admin intervention. **Sanity guards** at query level: paket must still have future `departureDate` (no point auto-cancelling a booking on a paket that already departed — that's S144 no-show territory), `status` not ARCHIVED, `deletedAt` null. **`reasonCode='PAYMENT_NOT_RECEIVED'`** + reason "Auto-cancel: tidak ada pembayaran setelah Nh" written by the system actor (`id=null`, email='system') so compliance scans can grep `cancelReasonCode + actorEmail='system'` for the auto-cancel cohort. Per-row failure caught so a bad row doesn't abort the batch. Silent on quiet days. Cap 200 candidates per run to avoid runaway. CLI `npm run job:auto-cancel-stale-pending` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/auto-cancel-stale-pending` + jobRunner daily interval.
238. ✅ Jemaah self-service activity timeline — `getJemaahBookingActivity(bookingId)` returns a sanitized timeline of events that affect the jemaah: status transitions (humanised — "Lunas — siap berangkat"), PAID payment rows, REFUND_ISSUED with `refundReasonCode` (S235) translated to Bahasa label, doc verification (VERIFIED emerald + REJECTED amber call-to-action), paket announcements (S192) posted since booking creation, and pickup choice events. **Privacy sanitization**: NO admin emails, NO actor roles, NO internal notes from audit `after` payloads, NO mentions/tasks/notif queue rows, NO tag changes (internal labelling). Ownership enforced upstream by `getMyBooking`'s `jemaahUserId` filter. Renders as a vertical timeline panel on `/saya/bookings/:id` above payment history with gold connector line + per-row icon. Bounded at 50 rows by default; older history rolled up as "+ N aktivitas lainnya".
239. ✅ Jemaah data export ZIP (UU PDP article 5) — `/saya/data-export.zip` streams a ZIP containing profile + bookings + payments + documents (metadata + actual uploaded files) + notifications as CSVs + a MANIFEST.txt. UTF-8 BOM + CRLF on all CSVs (Excel-compatible, mirrors S138/S165 convention). Uses `ZipArchive` from archiver v8 (pure ESM) piped directly to res — no temp file on disk. Per-doc-file failure logged in MANIFEST as "NOT INCLUDED" rather than aborting (partial export better than no export). Filename sanitisation against path traversal. **Ownership**: query scoped by `userId`; the service trusts the caller's role gate (`requireRole('JEMAAH')`). Filename `religio_data_<safeEmail>_<date>.zip`. Surfaced on `/saya/profile` as a gold-bordered "Hak portabilitas data" panel.
240. ✅ Right-to-be-forgotten request flow (UU PDP article 8) — `DataDeletionRequest(userId, requestedAt, requestReason, status, decidedAt, decidedById, decisionReason)` model (migration applied) + `DataDeletionRequestStatus` enum (PENDING / APPROVED / DECLINED). Jemaah submits via `/saya/profile` form (min 10-char reason; only one PENDING per user at a time via `ALREADY_PENDING` 409). Admin queue at `/admin/data-deletion-requests` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN — privacy compliance is top-tier, MANAJER_OPS doesn't decide). Decision requires 3-char reason; PENDING-only transitions (`ALREADY_DECIDED` 409 on second decision). **APPROVED doesn't auto-delete** — actual user deletion is admin's manual action via existing `/admin/users` flow; this table is the formal request trail. Audit row at submit + decide. **EMAIL fan-out**: PENDING submit notifies OWNER+SUPERADMIN; decision notifies the jemaah back. Re-submit after a DECLINED prior is allowed (jemaah's situation may have changed). Profile page shows the latest request state with colored badge.
241. ✅ Agen dietary view — `getAgentDietaryView({agentId, windowDays=14})` mirrors S211/S213/S214 dietary roll-up but **scoped to ONE agen's own bookings**. Groups by paket so agen sees multiple soon-departing trips at once; each row carries `{paket, totalPax, specialPax, tally, specials[]}` (same shape as S214 dietarySummary for view-template reuse). **Sort**: paket with specials first (sorted by departure asc), then paket with only REGULAR — trips needing attention bubble up. Walk-in bookings (`agentId=null`) NOT visible to any agen — that bucket is admin's. CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded. Renders as gold-bordered panel on `/agen?tab=analytics` above the funnel; each special jemaah row carries a wa.me deep link so agen can confirm by WhatsApp before admin briefs the kitchen.
242. ✅ Agen tag rollup — `getAgentTagRollup({agentId})` mirrors S230 `getBookingTagRollup` (admin cross-agen) but **scoped to ONE agen's pool**. Per-tag rows with `{tag, bookings, paxCount, paketCount}`. Sort by `paxCount desc` then tag asc. Active bookings on non-archived paket only. Multi-tag bookings counted under each tag. Panel on `/agen?tab=wallet` above the commission forecast (4-card grid; hidden when nothing tagged). Lets agen plan VIP touchpoints + LANSIA assistance without leaving the wallet view.
243. ✅ Per-paket commission forecast — `getAgentCommissionForecast` extended with `perPaket` aggregation: per-paket rows carry `{paket, rate, bookings, expectedIdr, perStatus}` where perStatus is the nested per-status breakdown for that paket. **Sort by `expectedIdr desc`** so the heaviest-revenue paket lands first. **`rate` reflects effective resolution** (matrix > agentOverride > paketRate > DEFAULT_KOMISI_RATE) — agen sees what rate their forecast actually uses. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded (same gate as the parent function). Top-5 panel rendered inside the existing commissionForecast card on /agen Wallet tab; each card shows departureDate + status mix + rate %. Empty-perPaket shape kept consistent across both empty-agentId and zero-booking early returns.
244. ✅ Crew dietary brief CSV (on-demand) — `/crew/paket/:slug/dietary.csv` mirrors the S211 admin export but **assignment-gated** (404 with `NOT_ASSIGNED` when the crew isn't on the paket — same anti-enumeration pattern as the manifest export). Lets crew pull a fresh brief whenever admin updates dietary info mid-cycle (S213 only fires Monday). Same CSV shape as S211: per-jemaah list of non-REGULAR diets + footer tally including REGULAR (kitchen needs the standard-meal volume too). UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 + CRLF matching the convention. Button "🍽 Diet CSV" appears in the crew manifest toolbar only when there's at least one non-REGULAR jemaah (dietarySummary already gates that signal).
245. ✅ Crew ICE contact book — `/crew/contacts` paginated read-only list of all jemaah across crew's currently-assigned paket. Mobile-first card layout with: jemaah name + paket title + bookingNo + phone (`tel:` + `wa.me` deep links) + pickup label + room + ICE (emergency contact) + passport. `?q=` substring search across name/phone/emergencyContact/bookingNo/paket title. Sorted by paket departureDate asc then jemaah name asc. Money-stripped (no totalAmount/paidAmount/komisi) — same separation of duties as the rest of the crew portal. ARCHIVED/soft-deleted paket excluded; CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded. Pagination clamped (page floors at 1, pageSize caps at 100). Topbar link "Kontak" added between "Notifikasi" and "Keluar".
246. ✅ Crew "Hari ini" dashboard widget — `getCrewToday({userId})` pulls three signals onto the `/crew` hero: (1) **paket departing within 48h** for the crew's assigned trips (`departureDate ∈ [now, now+48h]`, ARCHIVED/soft-deleted excluded), (2) **attendance days that fall on today** — walks crew's active paket within `[now-30d, now+30d]` window and resolves `(departureDate + dayNumber - 1)` to today via `localYmd` comparison, surfacing each as a one-click "Mark sekarang →" CTA, (3) **crew's own OPEN/ACKED incidents from the last 7 days** with status colour-coding (OPEN ruby, ACKED amber). Only the crew's OWN incidents (created by them) — other crew on the same paket don't pollute. Best-effort per slice — any failure logs but doesn't break the dashboard. Panel only renders when at least one slice has content (no empty-panel waste on quiet days).
247. ✅ Per-paket document expiry overview — `getPaketDocOverview({paketSlug})` flat-list of all jemaah-doc rows on the paket's ACTIVE bookings whose `expiresAt < now + 60d`. Three bands: **EXPIRED** (< now), **URGENT** (< 30d), **WARNING** (< 60d). REJECTED + PENDING docs excluded (REJECTED needs resubmission not renewal; PENDING has no real expiry signal). CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded. Sort: EXPIRED → URGENT → WARNING; within band, oldest expiry first (most urgent at top). Panel renders ruby-bordered above the manifest table on `/admin` Manifest tab; counts in header (`N EXPIRED · M <30 HARI · K <60 HARI`); top 30 rows scrollable with deep links to `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`. Hidden when zero rows (no real-estate waste).
248. ✅ Bulk doc verify — admin ticks multiple doc rows on `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit` and one click flips them all to VERIFIED with `verifiedAt + verifiedById` stamps. `bulkVerifyDocs({jemaahId, docIds})` performs **tuple guard** (silently skips docIds belonging to OTHER jemaah — anti-enumeration), **idempotency** (already-VERIFIED docs skipped with `already_verified` reason — no audit pollution), and **REJECTED refusal** (admin should re-handle individually, not bulk-flip rejection). Returns `{requested, verified, skipped, failed, skippedReasons}`. Per-row failure caught — bad row doesn't abort batch. Audit row per actually-flipped doc carries `bulkVerified:true` so timeline scans distinguish from individual SIMPAN-button verifies. UI: per-row checkbox shown only when doc exists + not already VERIFIED/REJECTED; floating bottom action bar appears when ≥1 checked; "✓ Verifikasi semua" button POSTs to `/api/jemaah/:id/documents/bulk-verify`.
249. ✅ Doc submit → admin notification — when jemaah self-submits a doc via `/saya/profile` (either via the form save with `refNumber` OR via file upload), `notifyDocSubmittedAdmin({jemaah, doc, kind})` fans out one EMAIL per ACTIVE OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — verification is ops, not cashier). Uses GENERIC notif type (short body, no template variant per doc type). Subject distinguishes kind: "mengirim PASSPORT" vs "mengunggah file PASSPORT". Body inlines `refNumber` + `expiresAt` when present. **Burst dedupe**: skips when an EMAIL for the same `relatedEntityId=docId` was queued within the last 1h — absorbs the typical jemaah save burst (refNumber → file → notes saves in a 5-min span don't generate 3 notifs) but a genuine resubmission a day later still fires. Wired into both `submitMyDoc` (status transitions to SUBMITTED) and `uploadMyDocFile` (transitions to SUBMITTED via file). Fire-and-forget — notif failure logs but never aborts the doc write.
250. ✅ Multi-paket comparison view — `getPaketComparison({slugs})` builds a side-by-side stat sheet for up to 4 paket. Pulls the same metrics as the S22/S39/S61 leaderboard (revenue, cost, margin, ROI, conversion) laid out as one row per metric × one column per paket. Slug list deduped, capped at `MAX_SLUGS=4`, preserves admin's input order. Unknown slugs silently dropped + reported in `missingSlugs`. Renders at `/admin/paket-compare?slugs=a,b,c,d` with a checkbox picker form at top. Sticky-left metric column + colour-coded margin% / ROI cells (emerald ≥20% / gold ≥5% / amber ≥0% / ruby negative). Sidebar link "Bandingkan paket" in Operasional group.
251. ✅ Network-wide expected revenue forecast — `getNetworkRevenueForecast()` projects gross cash inflow from existing pipeline across all future-departure non-archived paket. Uses same probability heuristic as S99 agent commission forecast (PENDING 0.30, BOOKED 0.50, DP_PAID 0.70, PARTIAL 0.85, LUNAS 1.00). Distinct from S99 — that projects komisi LIABILITY per agent; this projects cash INFLOW total. Returns per-status rollup + per-paket sorted by departureDate asc (imminent cash-flow needs first). Panel on `/admin` overview shows total remaining + weighted expected + per-status table + top-5 paket. Hidden when zero candidates (no real-estate waste).
252. ✅ Per-paket break-even surface on overview — `getNetworkBreakEvenOverview()` walks every ACTIVE future-departure paket with `costPerPaxIdr` set, calls S176 `getPaketBreakEven`, and surfaces those needing attention: (a) **`marginPerPax < 0`** (admin must raise price or cut cost — every LUNAS loses money even if S176 reports `booksNeeded=0` because no LUNAS yet); (b) **`booksNeeded > 0`** (more LUNAS needed but feasible within remaining seats). **Sort**: infeasible (margin negative OR `booksNeeded > seatsLeft`) first, then by `daysToDeparture asc` so the most urgent admin action lands at the top. Capped at 10 rows; hidden when empty. Panel on `/admin` overview between booking tags and revenue forecast.
253. ✅ Global admin search — `searchAdminGlobal({q, limit=5})` unified search across bookings (bookingNo + jemaah.fullName + phone tail), jemaah (fullName + nik + passportNo + phone tail), paket (slug + title), and agen (slug + displayName + whatsapp tail). **MIN_QUERY_LEN=2** to avoid scanning the table on a stray keystroke. **Phone normalisation**: extracts digits-only suffix (last 8) so admin pastes `+62 822-1234-5678` or `08221234` and both match. Soft-deleted paket excluded; AgentProfile lacks deletedAt so filter via `user.deletedAt:null` instead. ARCHIVED paket SURFACES (admin may want to find them — same convention as the bookings search page). Page `/admin/search?q=...` renders categorised result panels with deep links into each entity's edit page.
254. ✅ Admin topbar search bar with autocomplete — debounced (250ms) JSON endpoint `GET /admin/search/autocomplete?q=...` returns top-3-per-category. Dropdown appears below the search input on `/admin` overview; categories rendered as labeled sections; "Lihat semua hasil →" link at the bottom jumps to the full `/admin/search?q=` page. Escape key closes; click-outside closes; no results state shown when total=0. Pure inline JS — no framework, no AJAX library. Bar is part of the existing `.topbar` flex layout so it adapts to viewport width.
255. ✅ Admin recently-viewed trail — `User.recentEntities Json` column (migration applied) stores up to 15 most-recently-opened entities per admin user as `[{kind, id, label, viewedAt}]`. `trackRecentEntity` writes from booking-detail / jemaah-edit / paket-edit GET routes (best-effort `.catch(() => {})` so a tracking failure never breaks the actual entity view). **Dedupe by `(kind, id)`**: re-viewing the same entity shifts the existing entry to the top with updated label rather than producing duplicates. Cap enforced at write (slice to MAX_RECENT=15). Label cleaned + capped at 120 chars. Surface on `/admin` overview as horizontal pill row above the "Kemarin" widget — gold-bordered cards with `KIND · LABEL` deep-linked to each entity's edit page. Hidden when empty (no real-estate waste on a fresh login).
256. ✅ Booking clone for new jemaah — `cloneBooking({sourceBookingId, newJemaah, paxCount, notesPrefix})` creates a new booking on the same paket as the source with a new jemaah profile created inline. Carries over: paket / kelas / agentId / agentSlugCap / currency / source notes (appended after a `[Cloned from <bookingNo>]` prefix). Does NOT carry: paidAmount / cancel/refund fields / tags / autoTaggedSeen / pickupId / roomId / visitor attribution / komisi (per-jemaah, per-booking). New jemaah identity validated (min 2-char name + min 4-char phone). **Refuses on CANCELLED/REFUNDED source** (`SOURCE_CLOSED` 409 — frozen state shouldn't propagate). **Capacity check** against source.paket — kursi tidak cukup if reqPax > seatsLeft. paxCount defaults to source.paxCount; admin can override (e.g. family of 4 instead of single-pax source). totalAmount computed as per-pax average from source × new paxCount (rounded). Audit row carries `clonedFromBookingId + clonedFromBookingNo` so lineage is queryable. CLONE button next to TRANSFER AGEN on `/admin/bookings/:id`. RBAC: CANCEL_ROLES (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS).
257. ✅ Booking group key — `Booking.groupKey VARCHAR(40)?` column + index (migration applied) tags related bookings (family, mahram pair, company group, manasik cohort). Auto-generated by `cloneBooking` (S256): a 6-char base36 key (`G-XXXXXX`) is minted on clone — if the source has no `groupKey` yet, **the clone action also stamps the source with the new key**, creating the group on the fly. Both bookings then share the key. Existing `groupKey` is inherited (never regenerated). `groupCreated` flag in the clone audit row distinguishes "joined existing group" from "created new group" — and when the latter, a second audit row on the source records `groupKeyAssignedFromClone:true + clonedToBookingId`. Booking-detail page shows a gold-bordered "Anggota grup" panel listing siblings (up to 20) with status pills + deep links to each.
258. ✅ Group manifest filter — `filterManifestByGroup(result, groupKey)` narrows admin manifest to bookings sharing a `groupKey`. Composes naturally with existing dietary / tag / pickup filter chain (S229 et al.) — admin can stack `?manifestGroup=G-XYZ&manifestTag=LANSIA` and get the intersection. **Case-sensitive exact match** (group keys are auto-generated uppercase like `G-AB12CD`); whitespace trimmed; unknown keys return empty bookings (mirrors tag-filter pattern — gives admin signal that the key is wrong rather than silently dropping the filter). Group-key dropdown not added to the manifest toolbar (already reachable via "Anggota grup" panel on booking-detail); reset chip in the filter strip when a group filter is active so admin can clear without re-paging.
259. ✅ Manual group assignment — `setBookingGroupKey({bookingId, groupKey})` lets admin link/unlink any active booking to a group without going through the S256 clone path. Three modes via the `groupKey` arg: `null`/`""` clears (booking leaves the group), `"NEW"` mints a fresh `G-XXXXXX`, or an exact `G-XXXXXX` joins that group. `normaliseGroupKey` validates format (`G-[A-Z0-9]{4,12}`), trims, uppercases; lowercase input normalises so admin can paste `g-ab12cd`. **Refuses on CANCELLED/REFUNDED** (`BOOKING_CLOSED` — group state is frozen with the booking). **Skip-audit-on-no-op** for idempotent re-saves. Audit row carries `groupKeyManuallySet:true + groupCreated:bool` so the timeline distinguishes manual links from S257 clone-born stamps. UI: text input + "Simpan grup" + "× Lepas dari grup" buttons in the group panel on `/admin/bookings/:id`, visible on active bookings even when groupKey is null.
260. ✅ Group label/nickname — `BookingGroup(groupKey @id, label, notes)` standalone metadata table (migration applied). **No FK back to Booking.groupKey** since that column isn't unique on Booking — every member shares the same key. Looked up by string. `setGroupLabel({groupKey, label, notes})` upserts the row; `label` capped at 120 chars, `notes` at 4000. **Three-state preprocessor**: `undefined` (omitted) preserves, empty string clears to null, value sets. Pre-create hook in `setBookingGroupKey` upserts an empty row on `groupKey:"NEW"` so admin's form has a row to update. `getBookingGroup(groupKey)` synthesises a default row for pre-S260 groups (clone-born without a metadata row) so they render cleanly. Label surfaces on `/admin/bookings/:id` group panel ("🔗 G-AB12CD · Keluarga Pak Ahmad") so cross-booking navigation reads as human-friendly.
261. ✅ Per-group detail page — `/admin/groups/:key` shows the group's full member roster + combined money totals + label/notes form + CSV export. 6-cell KPI strip: member count / active count / total pax / total billed / total paid / balance. Active = NOT IN (CANCELLED, REFUNDED), same convention as the manifest. Members table sorted by `createdAt asc` (chronological joining order). View role (CANCEL_ROLES + KASIR); label edits gated to OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS. Booking-detail panel's group key link now points at this page instead of the manifest filter (admin can still drill from here into either). `buildGroupCsv` follows the standard convention (UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 + CRLF) with a TOTAL footer summing money — useful for family payment reconciliation.
262. ✅ Bulk cancel group — `bulkCancelGroup({groupKey, reason, reasonCode})` cancels every active member with one shared reason; routes through canonical `cancelBooking` so notif fan-out + seat release + komisi flip + per-member audit row all fire as if each booking were cancelled individually. Reason is prefixed `[bulk group <key>] ` so admin grep finds the cohort. **Per-member failure caught** (`failed[]` reported) — partial completion is better than nothing for a 10-member family booking. **Already-CANCELLED/REFUNDED members silently skipped** with `already_terminal` reason (no audit pollution; admin can safely re-run). One bookkeeping audit row on `BookingGroup` carries `{bulkCancel, requested, cancelled, skipped, failed}` so admin can answer "did anyone bulk-cancel my family?" with one query instead of N. Surface: ruby-bordered "⚠ Bulk cancel grup" panel on `/admin/groups/:key` (hidden when zero active members) with reasonCode dropdown + JS confirm guard. RBAC: OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — outbound state change).
263. ✅ Group needs-attention rollup — `getGroupsNeedsAttention({limit=10})` rolls active bookings carrying a `groupKey` into per-group gap counters: `unpaidCount`/`unpaidBalanceIdr`, `missingPickupCount` (only when paket offers pickup — paket without S196 setup don't generate misleading "missing pickup" flags), `missingDocCount` (passport on profile + required docs VERIFIED via S223 `requiredDocs` — defaults to passport + visa umroh + meningitis vax). **Sort by `gapTotal desc`** (sum of three gap counters) — heaviest backlog bubbles up. **Zero-gap groups dropped** (no real-estate waste). Panel on `/admin` overview with amber left-border, table showing group key + label + member count + per-category counts, deep links to `/admin/groups/:key`. Hidden when zero gaps surface (clean week → no panel).
264. ✅ Jemaah-side group visibility — `getJemaahGroupView({groupKey, currentBookingId})` returns a privacy-sanitized sibling list for `/saya/bookings/:id` so family bookings feel cohesive. **Strict privacy rules**: first-name only via `firstName()` honorific-stripper (`Pak Ahmad Wijaya → Ahmad`, `KH. Mahmud → Mahmud`); NO id (siblings can't navigate to each other's bookings); NO money / contact / docs / notes / tags. CANCELLED/REFUNDED siblings hidden entirely (other family don't need to see "uncle dropped out"). Single-member groups return null (panel hides — no value to viewer). Surfaces as sapphire-bordered "👥 Bagian dari grup 'Keluarga Pak Ahmad'" banner above the info panel with natural-language sibling list (e.g. "Anda berangkat bersama **Aisyah** (QUAD, 1p) dan **Hasan** (DOUBLE, 2p)").
265. ✅ Lead follow-up date — `Lead.followUpAt` column already existed (the kanban was sorting by it since launch) but had no UI to set it. `LeadCreateSchema`/`LeadUpdateSchema` now accept `YYYY-MM-DD` (from `<input type="date">`) alongside ISO datetime via a unified preprocessor; date-only strings get `T00:00:00` appended so `new Date()` parses to local midnight, not UTC. **Three-state preprocessor** (mirrors S5u/S22 convention): `undefined` preserves (PATCH semantics), `null`/`""` clears, value sets. Lead-card overdue indicator: ruby left-border + days-overdue suffix (e.g. "F/U 12 Jun (5h late)"); due-today: gold left-border + "(hari ini)" suffix. New lead modal gets a date input under notes. Kanban already sorted by `followUpAt asc` — switched to `{sort:'asc', nulls:'last'}` so leads without a follow-up sink to the bottom rather than crowding the top.
266. ✅ Lead snooze — `Lead.snoozedUntilAt DateTime?` column (migration applied). When set + in the future, lead is hidden from the kanban via `OR: [{snoozedUntilAt: null}, {snoozedUntilAt: {lte: now}}]` — no cron needed; the lead just naturally returns when the date elapses. **In-modal date input** + **per-card 😴 button**: clicking the button prompts for days (default 7) and PATCHes `snoozedUntilAt` to that future date. Same three-state preprocessor as S265. Re-snooze just overwrites the date.
267. ✅ Agent CRM "Hari ini" widget — `getAgentTodayLeads({agentId, now})` returns the agent's leads with `followUpAt < tomorrow` (overdue + due-today), bucketed as `{overdue, today, total}`. Snoozed leads excluded (S266 — agent explicitly said "not today"). CONVERTED/LOST excluded (terminal). Overdue sorted oldest-first (oldest neglected lead surfaces at the top). Gold-bordered panel above the kanban on `/agen`; overdue items get ruby left-border + days-overdue, today items get gold left-border. Hidden when zero (no noise on clean weeks). Distinct from S46 stalled-leads digest (that's an 08:00 email about `updatedAt > 7 days ago`); this is the inline UI surface.
268. ✅ Per-booking installment schedule — `Booking.installmentSchedule Json` column (migration applied) carries an array of `{id, dueDate (YYYY-MM-DD), amountIdr, status (PENDING|PAID), paidAt?}`. `normaliseSchedule()` validates + sorts by dueDate asc + dedupes ids + caps at 24 entries. `summariseSchedule()` returns `{count, pendingCount, paidCount, totalIdr, paidIdr, pendingIdr, nextDue, nextDueAmount, overdueCount}` for view-side rendering (overdue = PENDING with dueDate < today). **Sum of amountIdr is NOT enforced to equal totalAmount** — admin may set deposit-first plans where the last installment is "to be confirmed" math. `setBookingInstallmentSchedule({bookingId, schedule})` is idempotent (skip-audit-on-no-op); refuses on CANCELLED/REFUNDED (frozen state). UI: admin edits inline `<details>` form on `/admin/bookings/:id` (parallel-array dueDate[]/amountIdr[] inputs); jemaah sees a read-only table on `/saya/bookings/:id` with overdue rows tinted ruby + counter ("2/5 cicilan terbayar · Sisa Rp 15jt"). Hidden on bookings without a schedule (legacy / lump-sum).
269. ✅ Installment auto-reconcile — `recordPayment` now walks `installmentSchedule` and marks next PENDING entries PAID inside the same transaction. `applyPaymentToSchedule(schedule, amountIdr, {now})` is the pure function (single source of truth, shared between recordPayment + future surfaces). **Walks in dueDate-asc order**; marks an entry PAID only when the remaining amount fully covers it (we don't split installments — the agreed schedule is the contract; admin can manually edit when jemaah pays a partial). Already-PAID entries skipped (paidAt preserved). Audit row stamps `installmentsMarkedPaid: N` so the timeline shows the reconcile. Bookings without a schedule are no-ops (back-compat).
270. ✅ Installment-aware payment reminder — `sendPaymentReminders` (S172) now resolves the next-due installment via `summariseSchedule` and threads `nextInstallment: {dueDate, amountIdr, daysUntilDue, overdueCount}` into `notifyPaymentReminder`. Template gains `{{installmentLine}}` variable rendered as `"Cicilan jatuh tempo YYYY-MM-DD (5 hari lagi): Rp 5jt"` (or `"telat 3 hari"` / `"HARI INI"` depending on `daysUntilDue` sign). Overdue counter (`⚠ N cicilan overdue`) appended when prior installments were missed. **Bookings without a schedule fall back to the legacy generic balance message** — empty `installmentLine` renders as nothing in the template. Both EMAIL + WA templates updated; `notifyPaymentReminder` is backwards-compatible (callers that don't pass `nextInstallment` still work).
271. ✅ Installment plan suggestion — `suggestInstallmentPlan({bookingId, count=6})` splits `totalAmount − paidAmount` into N roughly-equal monthly installments ending one month before `departureDate` (or before `manifestClosesAt`, whichever earlier). **Tail-cents rule**: last installment carries the rounding remainder so the sum exactly matches the remaining balance (10M ÷ 3 → 3,333,333 × 2 + 3,333,334). First due ~7 days from now so jemaah has breathing room. Refusals: `BALANCE_ZERO` (nothing to schedule), `BAD_COUNT` (must be 1-24), `DEPARTURE_PAST`, `NO_TIME` (lastDue cutoff already in the past). **N=1 collapses to a single installment on lastDue**. Service returns the proposed array without persisting — caller decides whether to apply via `setBookingInstallmentSchedule`. UI: "↻ Sarankan jadwal" button + count input inside the inline edit `<details>` on `/admin/bookings/:id`; JS fetches `POST /:id/installments/suggest` then populates the parallel-array form rows.
272. ✅ Admin overdue installment digest — daily cron emails OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS with the list of bookings carrying ≥1 overdue installment. `getOverdueInstallmentBookings` aggregates active bookings + their schedules via `summariseSchedule`, returning per-row `{overdueCount, overdueIdr, nextDue, agent, paket}`. Sorted by `overdueIdr desc` so the heaviest leaks bubble to the top. Distinct from S172 jemaah reminder — that's "you have a balance", this is "these N bookings need follow-up by your team". **Silent on healthy days** (no overdue → no email). 24h per-recipient cooldown via the Notification table. New `INSTALLMENT_OVERDUE_ADMIN` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-installment-overdue-digest` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-installment-overdue-digest` + jobRunner daily interval. Top 10 inline in the email body + footer link to `/admin/installments-overdue` for the full queue.
273. ✅ Admin overdue queue page — `/admin/installments-overdue` (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS) renders 3-cell KPI strip (booking count / cicilan overdue count / total nilai) + a sortable table with per-row "✉ Kirim reminder" button. Same source as the S272 digest (`getOverdueInstallmentBookings`), so digest + UI never disagree. Reminder action `POST /admin/installments-overdue/:bookingId/remind` fires `notifyPaymentReminder` synchronously with the S270 installment context — **bypasses the S172 5-day cooldown** since the admin explicitly clicked. Empty state when no overdue (no real-estate waste). Sidebar link in Operasional group between "No-shows" and "Testimonials".
274. ✅ Doc verification queue page — `/admin/docs-pending` (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS) is the cross-jemaah "what needs my attention RIGHT NOW" surface for SUBMITTED docs. Distinct from per-jemaah edit page (which is the detail view). Service `getPendingDocs({docType?, limit=200})` returns SUBMITTED rows sorted by `submittedAt asc` (oldest first) with `ageHours` computed server-side + the jemaah's latest non-cancelled booking attached for trip context. 8-cell KPI strip (one per doc type) doubles as filter — clicking a non-zero count narrows the page. Per-row age cell colour-codes by tier (≥48h ruby + bold, ≥24h gold, else neutral). Sidebar link in Operasional group between "Cicilan overdue" and "Testimonials". Empty state when no pending docs (no real-estate waste).
275. ✅ Bulk doc reject — `bulkRejectDocs({docIds, reason})` flips SUBMITTED docs to REJECTED in one click from the S274 queue. **No tuple guard** (unlike S248 per-jemaah `bulkVerifyDocs`) because admin acts cross-jemaah from the global queue — they own the trust. Non-SUBMITTED rows silently skipped (already-VERIFIED/PENDING/EXPIRED/REJECTED reported in `skippedReasons[]` but the batch continues). **Min 3-char reason required** (admin must justify); reason appended to the doc's `notes` as `[Rejected by admin: <reason>]` so jemaah sees why on `/saya/profile`. Hard cap 500 docs per request. Per-row audit stamps `bulkRejected:true` + reason so timeline scans grep the cohort. UI: floating bottom action bar appears when ≥1 checkbox checked, with reason input + JS confirm guard.
276. ✅ Doc verification SLA digest — daily admin email when SUBMITTED docs sit > 48h awaiting verify. `getStaleSubmittedDocs({budgetHours=48})` returns the cohort sorted oldest-first; `sendDocVerifySlaDigest` fans out one EMAIL per ACTIVE OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — verification is ops, not cashier). **48h budget chosen so Friday submissions don't fire Sunday but DO fire Monday** — pairs with the 24h per-recipient cooldown to give "weekend forgiven, Monday accountable" semantics. Body inlines per-type tally + top 10 stale docs + footer link to `/admin/docs-pending`. Silent on healthy days (zero stale → zero email). New `DOC_VERIFY_SLA_ADMIN` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-doc-verify-sla` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-doc-verify-sla` + jobRunner daily interval.
277. ✅ Crew daily report model — `CrewDailyReport(paketId, crewUserId, reportDate@Date, dayNumber?, mood: GREEN|AMBER|RED, body)` (migration applied) with composite-unique `(paketId, crewUserId, reportDate)` so re-submit upserts. `mood` traffic-light surfaces trip health at a glance; `dayNumber` denormalised from `departureDate + reportDate` for sorting/display. `submitCrewDailyReport({userId, paketSlug, body, mood, reportDate?})` enforces 5-char min, 4000-char max, NOT_ASSIGNED gate (same 404 anti-enumeration pattern as the rest of the crew portal). **Uses `setUTCHours(0,0,0,0)` for `@db.Date` columns** — local-midnight Dates drift across TZ on Prisma findUnique vs upsert lookups (composite-unique failed loudly without it). Crew submit form rendered above the dietary panel on `/crew/paket/:slug` with mood radio + textarea + "✓ HARI INI TERKIRIM" / "⏱ HARI INI BELUM" status pill + collapsible riwayat panel showing this crew's last 10 reports.
278. ✅ Admin views crew daily reports — recent reports panel on `/admin/paket/:slug/edit` lists all crew × all reports for the paket (max 20, newest first) with mood-colored left border + crew name + day-N badge. `getRecentReportTally({days=7})` powers a 3-cell KPI strip on `/admin` overview (GREEN/AMBER/RED counts) — left-border color tracks the worst tier present (any RED → ruby, else any AMBER → gold, else emerald). Hidden when no reports in window (no real-estate waste). Distinct from S65 crew weekly digest (sent to crew themselves) — this is admin visibility.
279. ✅ Crew daily report reminder + missed digest — two related crons. **Evening reminder** (`sendCrewDailyReportReminder`): WA nudge to in-trip crew (today between departureDate and returnDate) who haven't submitted today's report. 12h per-(user, paket) cooldown via Notification table. WA preferred when crew has phone; EMAIL as fallback. **Morning admin digest** (`sendCrewDailyReportMissedAdmin`): lists yesterday's missed (paket, crew) combinations grouped by paket. Fan-out to ACTIVE OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS with 20h cooldown. Both silent when nothing to report. New `CREW_DAILY_REPORT_REMINDER` + `CREW_DAILY_REPORT_MISSED_ADMIN` enums (migration applied). CLIs `npm run job:send-crew-daily-report-{reminder,missed}` + matching HTTP triggers + jobRunner daily intervals.
280. ✅ Booking handover — `handoverBookingJemaah({bookingId, newJemaah, reason, acknowledgeLunas?})` replaces jemaah on an existing booking while preserving paket/kelas/money/agent/room/pickup/notes/group. Common umroh scenario: deposit paid + can't go + sells slot to relative. **Distinct from S256 clone** (clone = NEW booking) **and S21 transferBookingAgent** (transfer = change servicing agent, not jemaah). **Status-tier authorisation** via `resolveHandoverAuthz(status)`: PENDING/BOOKED/DP_PAID → any CANCEL_ROLES; PARTIAL → OWNER+SUPERADMIN only; LUNAS → OWNER only + explicit `acknowledgeLunas` flag (uang sudah lunas, perubahan jemaah harus konfirmasi tertulis). CANCELLED/REFUNDED refused (frozen state). Spawns new JemaahProfile inline + re-points `booking.jemaahId` + clears `booking.jemaahUserId` (so claim flow can re-link if new jemaah registers). No-op detection: refuses if new identity matches current name+phone (almost certainly admin error). Audit row carries full lineage (`previousJemaahId/Name/Phone` + `newJemaahId/Name/Phone` + `reason` + `bookingStatusAtHandover` + `acknowledgedLunas`).
281. ✅ Handover notif fan-out — `notifyBookingHandover` fires `BOOKING_HANDOVER` notifs to BOTH old + new jemaah. **Old jemaah** (when account exists): "Booking X telah dialihkan ke Y" via EMAIL+WA, with `recipientUserId` set so `/saya/notifications` inbox + unread badge pick it up. **New jemaah** (freshly-spawned profile, no user account yet): WA+EMAIL with claim instructions ("claim via /saya/claim with bookingNo + phone"). Best-effort posture — notif failure logs but never aborts the handover (the jemaah swap is the load-bearing change). Skips channel when no contact info (new jemaah typically has no email at handover time). New `BOOKING_HANDOVER` enum (migration applied). Payload carries `kind: 'handover_old' | 'handover_new'` for the queue viewer + drill-down.
282. ✅ Handover lineage panel — `getBookingHandoverLineage(bookingId)` reads handover history from AuditLog (entity=Booking, `after.handover=true`) and returns rows sorted newest-first with `{previousJemaahId/Name, newJemaahId/Name, reason, bookingStatusAtHandover, acknowledgedLunas, actorEmail, at}`. No separate table — audit already captures everything needed. Sapphire-bordered "Riwayat handover (Nx)" panel on `/admin/bookings/:id` between group panel and installment panel; hidden when no handover occurred (90%+ of bookings, no real-estate waste). Each row shows "Old → New" + handover date + status-at-handover + actor email + free-text reason. LUNAS-ack rows get a ruby "⚠ LUNAS ack" tag so compliance scans can spot them.
283. ✅ Per-paket add-on catalog — `PaketAddon(name, priceIdr, sortOrder, isActive)` (migration applied) lets admin curate optional extras per paket: "Extra baggage 30kg", "Room upgrade Suite", "Optional ziarah Madinah". JSON CRUD via `/api/paket/:slug/addons` (3-role gate via paketChildren). **`sortOrder` defaults to max+10** so newly added rows land at the bottom. **`isActive` toggle** removes from new-booking pickers (S284) but keeps existing BookingAddon rows intact — the snapshot is the authoritative price for those bookings. Skip-audit-on-no-op for idempotent re-saves.
284. ✅ Booking add-on attach/remove — `BookingAddon(bookingId, addonId?, nameSnapshot, priceIdrSnapshot, quantity)` (migration applied) attaches one row per attached add-on. **Mutates `Booking.totalAmount` inside the same transaction** so the existing money flow (status transitions, LUNAS-on-paid logic, installment reconcile via S269) all stay correct without changes. Price + name snapshotted at attach time — subsequent catalog edits don't retroactively affect committed bookings. **Quantity capped at 50** + **cross-paket addonId rejected** (`ADDON_PAKET_MISMATCH` 409) + **inactive addons rejected** (`ADDON_INACTIVE` 409). Remove decrements totalAmount + deletes the row; refuses if resulting total would go negative (safety guard). PaketAddon FK uses SetNull so deleted-from-catalog add-ons still appear on booking-detail as "(dihapus dari katalog)" via the nameSnapshot column.
285. ✅ Add-on revenue tally — `getAddonRevenueRollup()` aggregates all `BookingAddon` rows attached to active bookings (NOT IN CANCELLED, REFUNDED) and groups by `nameSnapshot`. Returns per-row `{name, attachCount, totalQuantity, revenueIdr, paketCount}` sorted revenueIdr desc, plus grand totals. **Grouped by name (not addonId)** so deleted-from-catalog add-ons still appear with their historical names — two add-ons with the same name across paket roll up to ONE row (admin can spot typos like "Extra baggage" vs "Extra Baggage"). Panel on `/admin` overview between group needs-attention and crew report tally; gold-bordered with KPI strip + top-10 table. Hidden when `attachCount === 0` (no real-estate waste on a quiet system).
286. ✅ Jemaah-side add-on view — `/saya/bookings/:id` renders a sapphire-bordered "Add-on" panel listing attached add-ons (name, snapshot price, quantity, subtotal) so jemaah sees what they've been charged for. Subtitle clarifies "sudah termasuk di total booking" — the totalAmount already reflects add-ons via S284's transactional bump, so there's no separate "add-on total to pay" line. Hidden when no add-ons attached AND no active catalog (clean booking sees nothing).
287. ✅ Voucher PDF add-ons section — extends S101 voucher PDF (`bookingVoucherPdf.js`) with a per-language "ADD-ON" section between PEMBAYARAN and AGEN PENDAMPING. Each row shows `• name · Qty N · subtotal`; footer line carries `Subtotal add-on: Rp X` in gold. Hidden when no add-ons attached. **Cache invalidation**: `voucherCache.hashVoucher` now includes the addons array (name/qty/price), so attaching or removing an add-on automatically busts the cached PDF on next download.
288. ✅ Jemaah-side add-on request — `requestBookingAddon({userId, bookingId, addonId, quantity})` lets jemaah ask for an add-on from `/saya/bookings/:id` without committing money themselves. Validates: ownership (`booking.jemaahUserId === userId`, 404 anti-enumeration), addon belongs to booking's paket, addon is active, quantity ∈ [1, 50], booking is open. **No DB model** — request IS the admin notification (`GENERIC` EMAIL fan-out to OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS); admin reviews + manually attaches via S284. **Per-(booking, addon) 6h cooldown** via Notification table query (JSON path on `payload.addonId`) so accidental double-submit doesn't spam admin; different addons can be requested in parallel. Form: collapsible `<details>` panel under the attached-addons table on the jemaah view; redirect-after-POST with `?ok=addon_request` flash.
289. ✅ Public inquiry form — `PublicInquiry(paketSlug?, agentSlug?, fullName, phone, email?, message?, status: NEW|CONTACTED|CONVERTED|ARCHIVED)` model (migration applied). Form on `/p/:slug` below the booking CTA — captures curious visitors who aren't ready to book ("tanya dulu, admin akan WA dalam 24 jam"). **Anonymous + low friction**: no account, no booking commit, just name + phone + optional message. **10-min dedup** by `(phone, paketSlug)` — accidental re-submit returns the existing row idempotently. Public POST mounted as `/api/inquiry` with 6/min/IP rate-limit (same convention as S5 booking). On submit, admin fan-out via `GENERIC` EMAIL with `payload.kind='public_inquiry_new'`. Best-effort notif — failure doesn't roll back the inquiry insert.
290. ✅ Inquiry admin queue + convert — `/admin/inquiries` (OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS) lists inquiries by status tab (NEW/CONTACTED/CONVERTED/ARCHIVED/ALL) with phone `wa.me/` deep links + paket cross-links. **Three actions**: (a) "→ LEAD" creates a `Lead` row under the chosen agent (default = inquiry's referral agent if set), flips status to CONVERTED + stamps `convertedLeadId` for backref; (b) "✓ CONTACTED" soft-tag for "admin acknowledged" without converting (NEW → CONTACTED, no further auto-transitions); (c) "× ARCHIVE" terminal for spam/not-interested with optional reason. Sidebar link in admin nav. Pagination 30/page.
291. ✅ Inquiry SLA digest — daily admin email when NEW/CONTACTED inquiries sit > 24h (`getStaleInquiries({staleHours=24})`). Body shows total + breakdown (`NEW count · CONTACTED count`) + oldest age + top 10 stale rows. Fan-out to ACTIVE OWNER+SUPERADMIN+MANAJER_OPS with 20h per-recipient cooldown via Notification table (JSON path on `payload.kind='inquiry_sla_digest'`). **Silent on healthy days** (zero stale → zero email). New CLI `npm run job:send-inquiry-sla` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-inquiry-sla` + jobRunner daily interval. **No new notif enum** — reuses GENERIC so the type list stays lean; digest is admin-side analytics, not a customer-facing pattern.
292. ✅ Jemaah lifetime panel — `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit` shows past bookings + lifetime totals + repeat-customer flag. `getJemaahLifetime(jemaahId)` returns `{profile, bookings (newest-first), totals: {tripCount, lunasCount, cancelledCount, activeCount, lifetimeRevenueIdr, lifetimePaidIdr}, repeatFlag, siblingProfiles}`. **`repeatFlag = lunasCount >= 2`** — the holy-grail metric for umroh agencies. **`lifetimeRevenueIdr` sums LUNAS `totalAmount` only** (cancelled/refunded don't count as real customer relationship). **Sibling profile detection** finds other JemaahProfile rows with phone matching the normalised digits (last-4 DB prefilter + JS exact-match confirm; survives `0xxx`/`+62xxx`/`62xxx` format variations) — these are typically anonymous-booking residuals from pre-claim flows that admin can merge via S5p.2. Panel above the existing S59 archived-leads hint; hidden when zero bookings (no real-estate waste on freshly-registered users).
293. ✅ Post-departure re-engagement — daily cron `sendPostDepartureReengage` finds LUNAS bookings whose `paket.returnDate` is in the ±5-day band around 30 days ago (`[now-45d, now-25d]` to absorb cron-misses), then sends a "how was your trip?" nudge with the agency's next 3 active future paket inline. **Terminal cooldown via Notification table** — once per booking (not per-day or per-N-days; one nudge per completed trip is enough). EMAIL preferred (body has paket list); WA fallback when no email. `recipientUserId` set so registered jemaah see it in `/saya/notifications`. New `POST_DEPARTURE_REENGAGE` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-post-departure-reengage` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-post-departure-reengage` + jobRunner daily interval. **Silent on quiet days** — no candidates → no emails.
294. ✅ Returning customer rollup — `getReturningCustomerRollup({months=6})` returns trailing N-month buckets with `{label, totalLunas, repeatLunas, repeatRatePct}` + grand totals. **Repeat definition**: jemaah whose FIRST LUNAS booking (anywhere in history) was strictly BEFORE the current LUNAS booking's `createdAt` — measured on createdAt (re-book moment) not departureDate (which lags too long). **CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded** from both sides (undone work isn't loyalty). `repeatRatePct=null` when bucket has 0 LUNAS to avoid misleading "0%" reading. Panel on `/admin` overview between cancel-reason and add-on revenue; left-border tier-colours by total repeat rate (≥30% emerald, ≥15% gold, else ruby). Hidden when `sampleSize === 0`.
295. ✅ Per-booking discount/surcharge — `BookingAdjustment(bookingId, kind: DISCOUNT|SURCHARGE, amountIdr, reasonCode, reasonNote?, createdByEmail)` model (migration applied). **Mutates Booking.totalAmount in the same transaction** so existing money flow stays correct. Distinct from S145/S235 refund (post-cancel only) and from S284 add-on (positive line item). **Refuses when DISCOUNT pushes total below paidAmount** (`ADJUSTMENT_BELOW_PAID` 409 — admin must refund first to give money back). Remove is symmetric. UI: dropdown picker on booking-detail with kind/amount/reason/note inputs.
296. ✅ Adjustment reason codes — service-side allowlist: `LOYALTY` / `PROMO` / `GROUP` / `STAFF` / `GOODWILL` / `CORRECTION` / `OTHER`. Case-insensitive input → normalised uppercase. Required on every add — no free-text-only adjustments since analytics rely on the structured code.
297. ✅ Adjustment ledger panel — `getAdjustmentLedger({days=90})` aggregates with two views: `perReason` (split DISCOUNT vs SURCHARGE per code) + `topActors` (top 5 admins by total absolute amount). Grand `netIdr = surcharge − discount`. CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings excluded (adjustment effect is moot on frozen state). Panel on `/admin` overview; left-border emerald when net favours jemaah, ruby when net favours agency. Hidden when `rowCount === 0`.
298. ✅ Quiet hours dispatch gate — `evaluateQuietHours(notif)` defers non-urgent WA messages outside the configured window so jemaah aren't pinged at 3 AM. Configurable via `NOTIF_QUIET_HOURS_START` / `_END` / `_TZ` env (defaults 21:00–07:00 Asia/Jakarta). EMAIL always passes (inbox is async). **Urgent types bypass** (`URGENT_TYPES` set: INCIDENT_REPORTED / INCIDENT_ESCALATED / INCIDENT_SLA_BREACH_OWNER / CANCEL_REQUESTED / PAYMENT_SETTLED_ADMIN / BOOKING_HANDOVER). **Admin-targeted notifs bypass** — admins have own opt-out via S300. Wraps midnight correctly. Deferral bumps `nextRetryAt` to top-of-hour at window end; the existing retry mechanism (S5nn) picks it up naturally. Best-effort: gate failure logs but sends anyway.
299. ✅ Per-recipient daily cap — `evaluateDailyCap(notif)` caps the number of notifs sent to one recipient over the last 24h, per-channel: WA default 5, EMAIL default 15 (env-tunable). Same bypass set as S298. Looks up SENT-status notifs only (PENDING/FAILED don't count toward the cap). Over-cap defers via `nextRetryAt = oldest + 24h + 1min buffer` so the count naturally ages out. Runs AFTER quiet-hours so we don't burn the cap on something we'd have deferred anyway.
300. ✅ Per-admin notif preferences — `AdminNotifPref(userId, type, enabled)` (migration applied; `(userId, type)` composite PK). Absence of a row = opt-in (no breaking change for existing admins). UI: `/admin/notif-prefs` checkbox grid + Save + bulk on/off buttons. **`shouldSkipForAdminPrefs({type, recipientEmail})`** wires into `enqueueNotification` — resolves recipient via email lookup, gates only admin-role + ACTIVE + admin-targeted notif types. Body of the SKIPPED row carries the reason so the queue viewer shows why it didn't fire. Sidebar link added in admin nav.
301. ✅ Cancel notif to agen — when admin cancels a booking that had an agent attached, fire EMAIL+WA to the agent's contact so they don't keep following up with the jemaah. New `BOOKING_CANCELLED_AGENT` enum (migration applied). `notifyBookingCancelledAgent({booking, agent, reason, adminEmail})` resolves contact via `agent.user.email` (EMAIL) + `agent.whatsapp` (WA) — two independent enqueues so a missing one doesn't block the other. **Silent on walk-in cancellations** (no agent → nothing to notify). **Fire-and-forget** posture: notify failure logs but never aborts the cancel transaction (the seat-release + status flip are load-bearing). Body inlines jemaah name + cancel reason + admin email so the agent gets the full context without opening admin UI.
302. ✅ Refund notif to agen — mirror of S301 for refunds. New `REFUND_ISSUED_AGENT` enum (migration applied). `notifyRefundIssuedAgent({booking, agent, amountIdr, partial, adminEmail})` fires after every refund on an agent-owned booking. Body labels "penuh" vs "sebagian" so agent knows whether the booking moved to REFUNDED or stayed CANCELLED with residual paid amount. Same walk-in skip + best-effort posture as S301. Closes the loop on the "agent doesn't know admin processed it" pattern that drove duplicate follow-ups.
303. ✅ Per-agen cancel/refund rate panel — `getAgentCancelRefundRollup({days=90})` returns per-agent rows with `{total, cancel, refund, cancelRatePct, refundRatePct, lowSample}` + grand `overallRatePct`. **Walk-in (agentId null) bucket under `__kp__` sentinel** (mirrors S35/S146 convention) so admin sees Kantor Pusat alongside named agents. **Min-sample guard `MIN_SAMPLE=3`** — agents with <3 bookings in window get `lowSample:true` + null rates (one bad row out of two would show 50% — misleading). Sort by `(cancel + refund) desc` so heaviest leakers surface first. Panel on `/admin` overview between repeat-customer and adjustment ledger; combined rate column tier-coloured (≥25% ruby, ≥10% amber, else emerald) — gives admin an at-a-glance signal of which agents are bleeding bookings.
304-305. ✅ Per-agent cancel + refund reason rollup — `getAgentCancelRefundReasons({agentId, days=90})` mirrors S175 (cancel) and S236 (refund) admin panels but scoped per agen. Returns `{cancel: {total, totalPaidIdr, rows[]}, refund: {total, totalIdr, rows[]}}` — single service powers both lenses since they share the same `__UNSET__` sentinel convention + label tables. **Sort: count desc for cancel, IDR desc for refund, with `__UNSET__` always last** so categorised data dominates the visual ranking. Side-by-side panel on `/agen?tab=analytics` (cancel left, refund right) — hidden when both totals are zero so clean agents see nothing. SharePct tier-coloured (≥40% ruby, ≥20% amber, else neutral). Helps agen self-diagnose ("8 PAYMENT_NOT_RECEIVED → follow up bayar lebih awal" vs "5 DOCUMENT_INCOMPLETE → bantu jemaah collect doc lebih dulu").
306. ✅ Reason rollup in agent weekly digest — extends S36 `buildAgentWeeklyDigest` to attach a `reasonRollup` envelope (`cancelByCode[] + refundByCode[]` with NULL → `__UNSET__`) computed from the same Mon-Sun window as the rest of the digest. `notifyAgentWeeklyDigest` renders the rollup as an inline `{{reasonBlock}}` placeholder (Bahasa labels reused from S304's tables) so agen sees the reason mix in inbox without opening `/agen`. **Silent on clean weeks** — when both rollups are empty, `reasonBlock` is empty string so the template stays string-stable (existing 8-line "BOOKING/LEAD/KOMISI" surface unchanged). Refund grouped by IDR sum to match how the admin S236 view ranks them; cancel grouped by count since the value-per-cancel signal is weaker than for refund (a paid-cancel and unpaid-cancel both block the same kursi).
307. ✅ Birthday greeting cron — daily WA+EMAIL ulang-tahun message to jemaah whose `JemaahProfile.birthDate.month/day === today.month/day`. New `BIRTHDAY_GREETING` enum (migration applied). **Once-per-year cooldown** via Notification table (`createdAt >= now - 360d`) so cron re-runs the same day produce no spam + the cooldown loosens naturally next year. Engagement opt-out (S309) enforced at the query level via `notifEngagement:true` filter — opted-out jemaah never enter the candidate list. Fires both EMAIL + WA when contacts present; each respects per-channel S5jj opt-out via `enqueueNotification`. Silent on quiet days (no birthdays today → no enqueues). CLI `npm run job:send-birthday-greeting` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-birthday-greeting` + jobRunner daily interval.
308. ✅ One-year anniversary nudge — daily cron finds LUNAS bookings whose `paket.returnDate` was 365±3d ago + sends "setahun lalu Anda menyelesaikan umroh" with featured future paket inline. Mirror of S293 post-departure (which fires at 30d) but tuned for the bigger emotional anchor — the umroh agency's biggest repeat-customer trigger is the 1-year mark. New `ANNIVERSARY_REENGAGE` enum (migration applied). **Terminal cooldown via Notification table** — one nudge per completed trip, ever. Engagement opt-out (S309) enforced at query level via `jemaah.notifEngagement:true`. CLI `npm run job:send-anniversary-reengage` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-anniversary-reengage` + jobRunner daily interval.
309. ✅ Engagement opt-out toggle — `JemaahProfile.notifEngagement Boolean @default(true)` column (migration applied) separate from S5jj transactional `notifEmail/notifWa` so jemaah can mute marketing-style touches (birthday + anniversary) without losing payment/status notifs. Surfaces as a checkbox in the `/saya/profile` notif preferences panel below the channel toggles. JemaahSchema 3-state preprocessor: `undefined` preserves (PATCH semantics), explicit `false` clears, `true` re-opts-in. **Form POST normalisation in `/api/saya/profile`** mirrors S5jj — unchecked checkbox absent from req.body becomes explicit `false` so unticking the box actually persists rather than being treated as "no change".
310. ✅ Trip feedback (NPS) — `TripFeedback(bookingId @unique, paketId, score 0-10, comment)` model (migration applied) captures jemaah quality signal post-trip. Distinct from S69 testimonial (public marketing): this is internal-only, never surfaces on `/p/:slug`. Survey at `/saya/bookings/:id/feedback` (chip-grid 0-10 + optional comment); ownership enforced via `jemaahUserId`. **Refuses with 409 when**: booking not LUNAS, paket has future returnDate (no review-ahead-of-trip), cross-user 404 (no leak). **Re-submit upserts in place** — jemaah who change their mind can revise without creating dup rows. NPS bucket helper (`bucketFor`): 9-10 promoter / 7-8 passive / 0-6 detractor (industry-standard). The S293 post-departure re-engage email now also carries the survey link so jemaah see it organically at 30d. CTA on `/saya/bookings/:id` shown only when paket has returned.
311. ✅ Admin NPS aggregation — `getNpsRollup({days=365})` returns overall NPS (`%promoter − %detractor`) + per-paket breakdown + last-10 recent comments. **Per-paket `lowSample:true` flag when sample < 5** — admin sees the row dimmed without a misleading %NPS from one bad review. Sort: enough-sample rows first by npsPct desc, then low-sample rows by total desc. `/admin/nps?days=N` page (window navigator: 30/90/365/730d) renders 4-cell KPI strip (NPS / promoter / passive / detractor counts) tier-coloured (≥30 emerald, ≥0 amber, else ruby) + per-paket table + comment list with left-border per bucket. Hidden when total=0.
312. ✅ Feedback reminder cron — daily nudge at 60d post-return for LUNAS jemaah who haven't submitted TripFeedback yet. **Why 60d not piggyback S293 at 30d**: S293's email plants the link organically, but jemaah at 30d are still adjusting; 60d gives time to reflect. Window `[now-65d, now-55d]` (±5d band). Terminal cooldown via Notification table (`relatedEntity=Booking`). Engagement opt-out (S309) enforced via `jemaah.notifEngagement:true` query filter. New `TRIP_FEEDBACK_REMINDER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-trip-feedback-reminder` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-trip-feedback-reminder` + jobRunner daily interval. **Silent on quiet days** — no candidates → no enqueues.
313. ✅ Per-agent NPS rollup — `getAgentNpsRollup({agentId, days=365})` mirror of S311 admin rollup but scoped per agent (filters TripFeedback by `booking.agentId`). Returns overall NPS + per-paket breakdown with the same `MIN_SAMPLE=5` sample-size guard from S310 (`bucketFor`/`MIN_SAMPLE` re-exported). Panel on `/agen?tab=analytics` below the cancel/refund reason card with 4-cell KPI strip (NPS / promoter / passive / detractor) tier-coloured (≥30 emerald, ≥0 amber, else ruby) + per-paket table. Hidden when total=0. Agents see their own quality signal without seeing other agents' numbers.
314. ✅ NPS block in agent weekly digest — extends S36 `buildAgentWeeklyDigest` to attach `npsRollup` (within the Mon-Sun week, scoped per agent). `notifyAgentWeeklyDigest` renders an inline `{{npsBlock}}` placeholder with promoter/passive/detractor counts + %NPS. **Silent on clean weeks** — empty `npsRollup.total` → empty block (template stays string-stable). Pairs with S306 reason block at the same template position so weekly emails carry both signals.
315. ✅ Detractor alert — when `submitTripFeedback` lands with `score ≤ 4`, fan out EMAIL to ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS (KASIR excluded — recovery is ops, not cashier).
