New `NPS_DETRACTOR_ALERT` enum (migration applied) + template that inlines jemaah identity + paket title + comment + deep link to `/admin/bookings/:id`. **Best-effort** — fan-out failure logs but never aborts the TripFeedback write (the row is the load-bearing artifact). **Comment fallback** when jemaah submitted score-only ("jemaah tidak menulis komentar") so the email still reads cleanly. Closes the loop on unhappy jemaah — silent NPS data isn't actionable; the alert turns a bad score into an admin outreach prompt within minutes.
316. ✅ Detractor follow-up lifecycle — `TripFeedback.followUpStatus` enum (NEW/ACKED/RESOLVED/UNREACHABLE) + `followUpNote/followedUpAt/followedUpByEmail/escalatedAt` columns (migration applied). Service helpers `ackDetractorFeedback / resolveDetractorFeedback / markDetractorUnreachable`. **State machine forward-only** (`NEW→ACKED→RESOLVED|UNREACHABLE`); re-engaging a resolved jemaah opens a new conversation, not a state revert. **Note required (min 3 chars)** for RESOLVED + UNREACHABLE — admin must justify the close; ACKED is a no-note acknowledgement. **Only score ≤6 rows participate** — promoter/passive feedback stays NEW forever (filtered out of the queue). Per-transition audit row stamps before/after `followUpStatus` + `followUpNote` for compliance scans.
317. ✅ Detractor queue `/admin/nps/detractors` — `listDetractorFeedback({status})` returns rows + KPI counts (NEW / ACKED / RESOLVED / UNREACHABLE / Escalated). Default `status='OPEN'` filters to NEW + ACKED (active queue); `?status=NEW|ACKED|RESOLVED|UNREACHABLE|ALL` narrows further. Per-row card colour-coded by status (NEW ruby / ACKED amber / RESOLVED emerald / UNREACHABLE muted) + per-row inline action forms with note inputs + `wa.me/<phone>` deep link to jemaah. Sort: open rows first by status asc then by `submittedAt asc` (oldest within bucket bubbles up). Linked from `/admin/nps` window-nav as "⚠ Detractor queue →".
318. ✅ Aged-detractor escalation — daily cron `escalateStaleDetractors({olderThanHours=48})` finds NEW detractor rows with `submittedAt < now-48h` AND `escalatedAt:null`, fan-outs EMAIL to **OWNER tier only** (tighter than S315's NEW-row fan-out — assumes broader admin desk saw the first alert; this is the "nobody's home" louder ping), then stamps `escalatedAt`. **Set-once** semantics mirror S80 incident escalation — re-running on an already-stamped row is a no-op. New `NPS_DETRACTOR_ESCALATED` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-detractor-escalate` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-detractor-escalate` + jobRunner daily interval. **Silent on quiet days**. Stamp persists regardless of fan-out success (the queue page shows the ESCALATED badge from this stamp; missing emails are retried by the notif queue).
319. ✅ Crew mobile bottom-nav — new `views/partials/crew-mobile-tabs.ejs` mirrors the S13 jemaah `mobile-tabs.ejs` pattern. 4 tabs (Home / Manifest / Kontak / Notif) using the same `.m-tabs` class so all CSS + safe-area handling is inherited. Manifest tab dynamically points to the current `/crew/paket/:slug` when on a paket detail view, falls back to `/crew` root otherwise. Body `class="has-m-tabs"` added to all 6 crew views. Topnav links (Kontak + Notifikasi anchors) marked `c-topnav-link` + a single `@media (max-width: 720px) { .c-topnav-link { display: none !important; } }` rule hides them on mobile (bottom-nav covers them). SOS-fab kept as separate critical surface — always visible above the bottom-nav for emergencies. Active-tab JS uses longest-prefix match so `/crew/paket/:slug/attendance/:dayId` highlights Manifest.
320. ✅ Jemaah "Hari Ini" in-trip hero — `getInTripContext(userId, now)` returns `{booking, paket, dayN, total, todayItinerary, nextItinerary}` when LUNAS booking window covers today (`paket.departureDate ≤ today ≤ paket.returnDate`), null otherwise. Day-number math uses **local-midnight floor** so trip-day boundary lands at wall-clock midnight not UTC. Hero card on `/saya` renders gradient-gold "Hari ke-N dari N" panel + today's itinerary block (extracted from `paket.days[dayNumber=N]`) + tomorrow preview. Hidden cleanly pre-trip/post-trip (no empty-state waste). Last day of trip still counts as in-trip (`today === returnDate` inclusive).
321. ✅ Jemaah SOS-light help request — `JEMAAH_HELP_REQUEST` enum (migration applied) + `submitJemaahHelpRequest({userId, message})` service. Validates: jemaah has active in-trip booking (mirrors S320 window check), message ≥5 chars, **30-min per-booking cooldown** via Notification table query (anti-flood). Fan-outs EMAIL + WA to ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS + assigned MUTHAWWIF crew on the paket (deduped by user id). One notif per `(recipient × channel)` for independent retry. Appends a `[SOS-LIGHT <timestamp>] <message>` line to `booking.notes` so admin sees it in the booking timeline + writes an audit row. Distinct from S5ff cancel-request (different intent: help vs leave) and crew S13 SOS (state-machine queue). Bottom-sheet form on `/saya` Hari Ini hero (rendered only when in-trip).
322. ✅ Itinerary timeline on jemaah booking detail — `getMyBooking` paket select extended with `days[]`. View on `/saya/bookings/:id` renders a vertical timeline with current trip-day computed inline (same local-midnight math as S320). Past days dimmed + emerald dot, current day gold-bordered + pulsing dot, future days neutral. **Pre-trip jemaah see the full upcoming itinerary**; **post-trip sees all days dimmed for reference**. Mockup parity with the `screens/jemaah-app.html` Timeline screen. No backend additions beyond the days select.
323. ✅ Crew "Hari Ini" attendance progress — `getCrewToday` extended with `inTripAttendance[]` slice: for each assigned paket currently in-trip (`departureDate ≤ today ≤ returnDate`), find today's `PaketDay` (computed from days-since-departure) and tally `{presentCount, absentCount, unmarkedCount, totalActive, percentPresent}` via a single `attendanceMark.findMany` + `booking.count`. Crew dashboard widget renders a tap-to-mark card per paket with progress bar tier-coloured (≥80% emerald / ≥50% gold / else ruby) + big touch targets. **CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded from totalActive** — matches the manifest definition of "who's actually going". Hidden gracefully when no in-trip paket (no empty-state waste). Best-effort: query failure surfaces empty array, doesn't break the dashboard.
324. ✅ Crew-authored paket announcements — extends S192 `createAnnouncement` audience to MUTHAWWIF actors via a new `POST /crew/paket/:slug/announce` route. **Tuple guard** (anti-enumeration): route 404s when crew isn't assigned to the paket BEFORE letting them post — same generic 404 convention as the rest of the crew portal. **Reuses entire fan-out chain** (S193 push to jemaah PWA + S216 email fan-out + audit row + `authorId` FK) — jemaah see crew posts the same way they see admin posts. Collapsible `<details>` form on `/crew/paket/:slug` with title + body + optional expiresAt. Closes the comms gap: crew on the ground sees bus delays / schedule changes first; previously the only crew→jemaah channel was SOS for emergencies.
325. ✅ SOS acknowledge loop — closes the S321 workflow. New `JEMAAH_HELP_ACK` enum (migration applied) + `ackJemaahHelpRequest({bookingId, message})` service + `getBookingHelpRequestState({bookingId})` query. **Pending = latest JEMAAH_HELP_REQUEST newer than latest JEMAAH_HELP_ACK** for the booking (no separate model needed; the notif table itself is the source of truth). Admin sees ruby SOS banner on `/admin/bookings/:id` with inline ACK form (CANCEL_ROLES gate). On ACK: fires EMAIL + WA to jemaah (subject "Tim sudah respon SOS Anda") + S93 push to installed `/saya` PWA + booking note append `[HELP-ACK <timestamp>] by <admin>` + audit row. **Push is best-effort** — failure logs but never aborts the ack (email + WA are load-bearing). After ack, banner flips to emerald "✓ SOS sudah di-ACK · <timestamp> · oleh <admin>".
326. ✅ Crew dedicated incident queue — new `/crew/incidents` page + `listMyIncidentsPaginated(crewUserId, {status, days=30})` service. Returns rows + KPI counts (`total / OPEN / ACKED / RESOLVED`) so the strip is honest about queue state regardless of `status` filter. Default `status='ACTIVE'` filters to OPEN+ACKED (active queue); `?status=NEW|ACKED|RESOLVED|ALL` narrows further. Mobile-friendly card layout with status-coloured left border (OPEN ruby / ACKED amber / RESOLVED emerald) + age pill (≥48h ruby / ≥24h gold). Linked from crew dashboard "Riwayat alert" header with "Buka queue lengkap →" button. Mirrors mockup `screens/crew-app.html` Alerts tab. Bottom-nav still present (`has-m-tabs` body class).
327. ✅ Per-role PWA manifest — splits the single `shared/manifest.webmanifest` into `shared/manifest-jemaah.webmanifest` (scope `/saya`, name "Religio Jemaah", theme `#0A0908`) and `shared/manifest-crew.webmanifest` (scope `/crew`, name "Religio Crew", theme `#D4AF6B`, dedicated incident shortcut). `views/partials/pwa-head.ejs` accepts a `pwaRole` variable via include locals — `pwaRole: 'crew'` swaps to the crew manifest + theme + apple-touch-title. **Default ('jemaah')** preserves backward behaviour for views without an explicit role. Invalid pwaRole falls back to jemaah (defensive). Install identity now distinct per portal — a muthawwif who installs the app sees "Religio Crew" branding, not generic "Religio Pro". Single SW (`shared/sw.js`) still services both since manifest identity is independent of SW scope.
328-330. ✅ Jemaah ibadah counters — mockup parity with `screens/jemaah-app.html` Ibadah screen. **Client-side only** (no backend changes) via `shared/ibadah-counter.js` IndexedDB helper (single `state` store keyed by counter id). Three routes: `/saya/ibadah` (S330 hub with last-state cards + progress bars), `/saya/ibadah/thawaf` (S328: 7 putaran tap counter with Hajar Aswad doa inline), `/saya/ibadah/sai` (S329: 7 trip Safa↔Marwah counter that flips direction marker per trip). **Offline-first**: IDB survives app reload + works without internet. **Haptic feedback** via `navigator.vibrate(30)` on supported devices. **Storage failure fallback** — counter operations resolve to null on IDB error rather than throw, so the counter UI keeps rendering even with storage blocked. CTA on `/saya` Hari Ini hero (only when in-trip) deep-links to the hub. Reset + Undo with confirm. Counter caps at 7 — once complete, further taps no-op (state preserved until manual reset).
331. ✅ Help requests admin queue — `/admin/help-requests` lists bookings with pending JEMAAH_HELP_REQUEST > JEMAAH_HELP_ACK. **No new model** — derived from the Notification table itself via `listPendingHelpRequests` which reduces requests+acks+escalations per bookingId. Sorted oldest-first (most urgent at top). KPI strip: pending count, escalated count, ACK-24h count. Each row: jemaah identity + paket + age pill (≥2h ruby, ≥1h gold) + escalated badge + message preview + wa.me deep link + "→ Detail booking + ACK" CTA. The ACK action stays on `/admin/bookings/:id/help-ack` from S325 — queue is a triage surface, not a workflow tool.
332. ✅ SOS SLA escalation — daily cron `escalateStaleHelpRequests({olderThanHours=2})` finds pending help requests older than threshold and fans out EMAIL to **OWNER tier only** (tighter than the S321 initial fan-out — assumes broader desk saw the first alert). New `JEMAAH_HELP_ESCALATED` enum (migration applied). **The escalation notif row itself is the set-once stamp** — no separate column. Re-runs skip bookings where latest ESCALATED >= latest REQUEST (mirrors S80 incident escalation + S318 detractor escalation patterns). **CLI `npm run job:send-help-escalate` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-help-escalate` + jobRunner HOURLY interval** (not daily — SOS is time-critical, the SLA window is 2h). Silent on quiet hours. When OWNERs list is empty, writes a placeholder marker notif so the cron doesn't keep re-flagging the same booking.
333. ✅ Doa harian widget on `/saya/ibadah` — pure client-side `shared/doa-harian.js` cycles through 11 commonly-needed doa (masuk Masjidil Haram, melihat Ka'bah, minum Zamzam, masuk Nabawi, ziarah makam, sapu jagat, dst). **Cycled by day-of-year** so the same jemaah sees a different doa each trip day; rotation covers all entries within ~2 weeks. Each doa carries `{title, arabic, latin, translation}` rendered as gold-bordered card on the hub. **No backend** — entire asset is the static JS file. Pairs naturally with the Thawaf + Sa'i counter cards (same hub page).
334. ✅ Offline read cache for `/saya` — `shared/sw.js` bumped to `rp-v5`. **Stale-while-revalidate** strategy added for `/saya/bookings/` + `/saya/ibadah` paths (serves cache immediately + refreshes in background) — critical for Saudi where flaky signal makes the prior network-first timeout feel slow. Other HTML paths (admin/crew) stay on network-first where freshness matters more. **HTML cache capped at 50 entries** via FIFO eviction (`capHtmlCache` helper) to prevent unbounded growth in long-running PWA sessions. **Cache-hit responses carry `X-SW-Cache: hit` header** so future client JS can show an "offline mode" indicator. The S5xx `/shared/offline.html` fallback still triggers on cache-miss + network-fail.
335. ✅ Push subscribe CTA on Hari Ini hero — when jemaah is in-trip AND `Notification.permission` is `'default'` (not granted and not denied), shows a prominent emerald CTA card "Aktifkan notif tim" on the hero. Click triggers the existing S94 `push-jemaah.js` `enable()` flow via the hidden `#rp-push-enable` button (no duplication of the VAPID subscribe logic). **Hidden when permission is already `'granted'` or `'denied'`** — re-prompting after denial fails silently and just annoys; the canonical push-bar in the dashboard panel handles the granted state. Pairs with S321 SOS + S325 ack + S324 announcements as the "real-time signal in your pocket" story.
336. ✅ Crew push subscribe toggle — adds `/crew/push/{config,subscribe,unsubscribe}` API endpoints + `shared/push-crew.js` client (mirror of S94 `push-jemaah.js` DOM contract). Crew router mount is `/crew` so paths are `/push/*` not `/api/crew/push/*`. **Reuses role-agnostic `webPush.js`** service (`subscribePush`/`unsubscribePush` operate by userId — same `PushSubscription` table services admin + jemaah + crew). Crew need push so they receive ad-hoc admin broadcasts + future incident state pings. Push-bar UI added to `/crew` dashboard above the Hari Ini widget. **`pushToAdmins()` still gates on admin role** — crew subscriptions never receive admin-tier fan-out by accident.
337. ✅ Booking reschedule service — `rescheduleBooking({sourceBookingId, targetPaketId, targetKelas, targetPaxCount?, reason?})` moves a jemaah from one paket to another while preserving payment history + komisi continuity. New `RESCHEDULED` BookingStatus enum value (migration applied) + `Booking.rescheduledToBookingId` self-FK + `rescheduledAt` + `rescheduledByEmail`. Source booking goes terminal with lineage pointer; new booking carries over `jemaahId / jemaahUserId / agentId / agentSlugCap / paidAmount / notes`. **Status inferred from carried paid vs new total** (PENDING / DP_PAID / LUNAS) — admin can adjust via the existing payment-record flow if needed. **Komisi handling**: PENDING re-points to new booking (work-attribution shifts to the new trip); EARNED stays on source (already earned for original sale work — moving would erase that history); PAID never touched. Source kursi pool freed, target kursi claimed in same transaction. Refuses on: terminal source (CANCELLED/REFUNDED/RESCHEDULED), same target paket, target has no seats, target doesn't sell the requested kelas.
338. ✅ Admin reschedule UI on `/admin/bookings/:id` — `⇄ RESCHEDULE` button next to `↪ TRANSFER AGEN` (CANCEL_ROLES gate + not-terminal). Modal carries target paket dropdown (ACTIVE/DRAFT non-archived future-departure, pre-fetched), kelas dropdown populated inline from per-paket PaketHarga map, pax + reason inputs. **Live price-diff hint**: shows source total + new total + paid carried + sisa (color-coded amber when balance > 0, emerald when LUNAS) so admin sees the financial impact before submit. `POST /admin/bookings/:id/reschedule` lands admin on the NEW booking detail page with `?ok=rescheduled_from_<sourceId>` flash.
339. ✅ Reschedule notif fan-out — new `BOOKING_RESCHEDULED` enum (migration applied) + `notifyBookingRescheduled({sourceBooking, newBooking, reason, adminEmail})` helper. **Three channels per reschedule**: jemaah EMAIL (full body with old/new bookingNo + paket dates + balance breakdown), jemaah WA (short summary), agent EMAIL (work-attribution note: PENDING komisi re-pointed, EARNED stays). Best-effort posture — per-channel failure logs but doesn't abort the rest of the fan-out. **Agent skipped when source has no agentId** (walk-in / Kantor Pusat — nothing to notify). Pairs with the S280 BOOKING_HANDOVER pattern as the "same-jemaah, new-paket" workflow complement.
340. ✅ Jemaah reschedule request — `Booking.rescheduleRequested/At/Reason/TargetPaketId` columns (migration applied) + `requestRescheduleByJemaah` service. Mirrors S5ff cancel-request pattern: validates reason ≥3 chars, one pending at a time, optional `targetPaketId` preference (admin still gates). **No `manifestClosesAt` deadline guard** unlike S147 cancel-deadline — reschedule is the opposite of cancel; late-cycle jemaah still benefits from clean handover. `rescheduleBooking` (S337) auto-clears the 4 request fields on successful approval (implicit). Collapsible form on `/saya/bookings/:id` next to existing cancel-request form (sapphire-bordered to distinguish).
341. ✅ Admin reschedule request banner + decline — sapphire-bordered banner on `/admin/bookings/:id` when `b.rescheduleRequested=true` (alongside existing cancel-request banner). Shows jemaah's reason + preferred target paket (if specified). "⇄ RESCHEDULE" button opens the S338 modal **pre-filled** with the requested target paket + reason textarea. Decline path: collapsible form with required ≥3-char reason → `declineRescheduleRequest` service clears the 4 fields + writes audit + notif. `rescheduleBooking` also clears request fields atomically (no need for admin to dismiss separately).
342. ✅ Reschedule request notif fan-out — new `RESCHEDULE_REQUESTED` enum (migration applied) + `notifyRescheduleRequested({booking, reason, targetPaketId, requestedByEmail})` fans to ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS on jemaah submit. Body includes jemaah's preferred target paket label when set, with admin deep-link to `/admin/bookings/:id`. `notifyRescheduleRequestDeclined({booking, declineReason, adminEmail})` mirrors `notifyCancelRequestDeclined` — GENERIC type to jemaah on decline (admin's reason inline). **Admin-targeted on submit (no `recipientUserId`)**, **jemaah-targeted on decline** — same inbox-isolation rule across the loop.
343. ✅ Admin reschedule requests queue — `/admin/reschedule-requests` page + `listPendingRescheduleRequests` service. Lists all bookings with pending `rescheduleRequested=true` AND non-terminal status, sorted oldest-first. KPI strip (pending count, with-target count, no-target count). Per-row: jemaah identity + age pill (≥48h ruby / ≥24h gold) + reason quote + preferred target paket (resolved via batched lookup, no N+1) + WhatsApp deep link + "→ Detail booking + Reschedule" CTA. Operational triage surface beyond per-booking banners — admin no longer needs to scan booking-detail pages to find pending requests.
344. ✅ Reschedule reason code — `BookingRescheduleReason` enum (8 codes: JEMAAH_REQUEST / DOCUMENT_DELAY / HEALTH / FINANCIAL / PAKET_FULL / SCHEDULE_CONFLICT / OPERATOR_INITIATED / OTHER) + `Booking.rescheduleReasonCode` column + index (migration applied). Admin picks from dropdown in S338 modal alongside the free-text reason; service-side allowlist (`RESCHEDULE_REASON_CODES`) validates with case-insensitive normalisation, BAD_RESCHEDULE_REASON_CODE 400 on typo. Persisted on the source booking row + included in audit `after` payload for compliance scans. Nullable so pre-S344 RESCHEDULED rows stay valid (bucket under `__UNSET__` in S345 analytics).
345. ✅ Reschedule analytics — `getRescheduleAnalytics({days=90})` returns three lenses: **perPaket** (in/out/net flow per paket, top 15 sorted by `|net|` desc — biggest imbalances surface), **perReason** (count + sharePct per reasonCode, `__UNSET__` always last per S175 convention), **topPairs** (top 10 source→target paket flows — reveals patterns like "Ramadhan-2026 → Ramadhan-2027" delays). Panel on `/admin` overview above S303 agent cancel/refund panel, hidden when `total=0`. Two-column layout: left = per-paket flow table (out ruby, in emerald, net colour-coded by sign), right = reason breakdown + top pairs list. Header carries link to S343 queue page.
346. ✅ Bulk reschedule service — `bulkRescheduleBookings({sourcePaketId, targetPaketId, targetKelas, reason, reasonCode})` moves all non-terminal bookings from a paket in one operation. Operationally common when ops cancels a paket (vendor failure, visa batch reject) and every jemaah needs to move to a replacement. **Pre-check capacity** (`TARGET_INSUFFICIENT` 409) refuses up front if target can't fit all source paxCount — better than half-fail leaving a mess. **Per-booking failure isolated** via try/catch in the loop; result `{moved, skipped, failed, details}` reports each row. **Sequential not parallel** since each `rescheduleBooking` call touches kursi counts on both paket — concurrent updates could race the capacity guard. Each moved booking gets the standard S337 audit row + a meta `UPDATE entity=Paket` row on source paket summarising the bulk op.
347. ✅ Admin bulk reschedule UI — danger-bordered panel on `/admin/paket/:slug/edit` below the form footer (renders only when source has ≥1 active booking). Target paket dropdown (ACTIVE/DRAFT future, not self) + kelas dropdown populated inline from per-paket PaketHarga map + reasonCode (defaults to `OPERATOR_INITIATED`) + free-text reason + **"type slug to confirm" guard** so admin can't accidentally trigger a 30-booking move. Pre-check booking count visible in the panel header. Form posts to `/admin/paket/:slug/bulk-reschedule`; redirects back with `?ok=bulk_moved_N_failed_N` flash.
348. ✅ Bulk reschedule notif aggregation — `notifyBulkRescheduleAgents({moved, sourcePaket, targetPaket})` groups moved rows by `agentId` and fires **ONE EMAIL per affected agent** listing all their bookings (avoids 20 individual emails flooding an inbox when admin moves a paket-full). Walk-in bookings (agentId=null) bucket together but no notif fires (no agent to notify). `notifyBulkRescheduleAdmins({moved, failed})` fires a single summary email to OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS with moved/failed counts + failed booking list for manual handling. **`rescheduleBooking` accepts a `skipAgentNotif` flag** wired through to `notifyBookingRescheduled` so the per-booking agent notif is suppressed during bulk — jemaah always still get their individual notif since each needs their own info.
349. ✅ Pre-trip countdown panel — H-N hero on `/saya/bookings/:id` renders only when status is non-terminal AND today is strictly BEFORE departure (the S320 hero on `/saya` dashboard covers the in-trip window; this fills the pre-trip gap). Tier-coloured: gold ≥30d / amber 7-30d / ruby ≤7d with matching badge ("URGENT" / "SEBENTAR LAGI" / "DALAM PERSIAPAN"). Pure view enhancement — no backend changes; pulls `b.paket.departureDate` already loaded by `getMyBooking`. Closes a real anxiety point: jemaah want to know "kapan berangkat" prominently, not scroll for it.
350. ✅ Jemaah doc readiness card — exports new `computeReadinessForBooking({booking, departureDate, requiredDocs})` from `src/services/preDepartureChecklist.js` (single-row variant of the S23 admin bulk path). Same 8 checks (passport / 4 docs / room / emergency contact) drive the same `{score, tier, checks}` shape; admin and jemaah see identical numbers. Card on `/saya/bookings/:id` with tier-coloured progress bar + "yang masih kurang" actionable list deep-linked to `/saya/profile`. Hides cleanly when paket has departed or status is terminal. Roommate-style note for `roomAssigned: false` ("kamar diatur admin, bukan jemaah").
351. ✅ H-7 pre-departure readiness reminder — `sendReadinessReminders` daily cron walks active bookings (BOOKED/DP_PAID/PARTIAL/LUNAS) whose `paket.departureDate` falls in `[now+5d, now+9d]` ±2d band, computes readiness via the shared S350 helper, filters to score < 100. **Per-booking 5-day cooldown** via Notification table query (PREDEPARTURE_READINESS_REMINDER notif rows). Fires EMAIL + WA per jemaah (each channel respects per-channel S5jj opt-out) + best-effort push via S93 `pushToUser` to installed PWA. **Engagement opt-out (S309) NOT enforced** — this is transactional/operational ("you're missing X"), not marketing; jemaah needs the heads-up regardless. PENDING bookings skipped (unlikely to fly). New `PREDEPARTURE_READINESS_REMINDER` enum (migration applied). CLI `npm run job:send-predeparture-readiness` + HTTP `POST /api/admin/jobs/send-predeparture-readiness` + jobRunner daily interval.
352. ✅ In-app push toast — `shared/sw.js` push handler now `postMessage`s every client `{kind:'rp-push', title, body, url, tag, ts}` BEFORE showing the system notification (browser-policy requirement keeps the OS notification firing — toast is additive). New `shared/in-app-toast.js` listens for the SW message and renders a gold-bordered top banner via an injected `#rp-toast-host` div; tap navigates to `url`, close button dismisses, auto-dismiss after 8s. **SOS-tagged toasts skip auto-dismiss** (`tag.startsWith('sos')`) so life-safety alerts stick until manually closed (mirrors the SW `requireInteraction` rule for the system notification). Dedupes by `tag` so a stream of same-tag pushes collapses to one visible banner. Loaded from `views/partials/pwa-head.ejs` so every PWA-flavoured page picks it up. `CACHE_VERSION` bumped `rp-v5 → rp-v6` so installed clients pick up the new SW logic on next activation. Closes a common gap — system notifications often get missed when the user is actively inside the PWA.
353. ✅ Web Share API on jemaah booking — `/saya/bookings/:id` crumb gains a "📤 BAGIKAN" button next to the voucher PDF link that **only reveals when `navigator.share` is supported** (hidden via `style="display:none"` by default; JS feature-detect flips it visible). Tapping fires `navigator.share({title, text, url})` with the **public verification URL** built via S197 `buildVerifyUrl(booking.id)` so the recipient lands on the privacy-sanitised verify page (first-name only, no PII leak even if the share is forwarded). Client-side URL builder handles both absolute and relative cases — when the server-rendered `verifyUrl` is path-only (`PUBLIC_BASE_URL` env unset), JS prefixes `window.location.origin`. Best-effort load — `buildVerifyUrl` failure logs but doesn't break the page (button just stays hidden). Native share sheet routes the link through WhatsApp / SMS / email / etc. depending on what the OS exposes.
354. ✅ Quick-contact panel — `/saya/bookings/:id` gold-bordered "☎ Kontak cepat" panel above the readiness card, button-grid with `tel:` + `wa.me/` deep links (64px min-height for thumb-friendly tap targets). Three contact tiers in fixed priority: agen WA (emerald, when `booking.agent.whatsapp` set) → admin WA (gold, from new `PUBLIC_ADMIN_WA` env) → admin phone (sapphire, from new `PUBLIC_ADMIN_PHONE` env). Walk-in bookings show a "tanpa agen, hubungi admin" hint. **Panel hidden on terminal status** (CANCELLED/REFUNDED/RESCHEDULED — those bookings don't need active support). **Panel hidden when no contact configured** (graceful degradation — env unset = no admin buttons, just agen WA if available). Env vars validated via Zod (`PUBLIC_ADMIN_WA` must be 8-15 digits, `PUBLIC_ADMIN_PHONE` min 8 chars). Exposed via `res.locals.publicAdminWa/Phone` in `src/app.js` so any view can pick them up without route changes. Phone-to-WA normalisation (digits-only + `0`→`62`) inline in EJS — mirrors the Fonnte convention.
355. ✅ SOS-light offline queue — `shared/sos-light-queue.js` mirrors the S5xx attendance-queue.js IndexedDB pattern but for `/api/saya/help-request` (S321 jemaah SOS). When jemaah taps "Kirim SOS" with `navigator.onLine === false` OR the fetch throws mid-send, the message is queued in `religio-sos-light.queue` IDB store with `status:'pending'` and a "⏱ Queued (offline)" banner shows. `startAutoFlush` drains on `online` event + 30s interval tick, replays via JSON POST to the same endpoint. **Server idempotency carries the load** — S321's 30-min per-booking cooldown via the Notification table means a long-running outage that produces 5 queued retries still only generates one admin alert (subsequent replays return `ALREADY_PENDING` 409 which the queue treats as success). CSRF auto-attached via the existing `shared/csrf.js` fetch monkey-patch. Toggle button shows "🆘 Minta bantuan (SOS) · N queued" when items pending so jemaah knows a previous SOS is still trying. Critical for Saudi where signal drops in hotel basements / mountain passes / inside Masjidil Haram — without this, a failed POST silently lost the SOS.
356. ✅ Web Share on paket landing — `/p/:slug` sticky nav gains a "📤 Bagikan" button next to the "Pesan" CTA. Hidden via `style="display:none"` by default; JS feature-detects `navigator.share` and flips visible. Tap fires `navigator.share({title, text, url})` with the absolute paket URL **preserving `?a=<agentSlug>` attribution** so referral credit follows the share through WA/SMS/email. Built client-side via `data-paket-slug + data-agent-slug` attrs (no server roundtrip). AbortError on user-dismissed share is swallowed silently. Extends S353 from voucher-only sharing to organic paket marketing — agents/jemaah can share via native share sheet with one tap, agent attribution intact.
357. ✅ Pre-trip push subscribe CTA — `/saya/bookings/:id` emerald-bordered card between the S349 H-N hero and the S350 readiness card. Renders only when paket hasn't departed AND status non-terminal AND `Notification.permission === 'default'` (re-prompting after denial just annoys; granted state has its own toggle elsewhere). Also checks `pushManager.getSubscription()` and skips CTA when already subscribed (covers granted-but-not-yet-shown state). **Reuses S94 push-jemaah.js infrastructure** via a hidden `#rp-push-bar` DOM block — the visible CTA button just proxies its click to the hidden `#rp-push-enable` so push-jemaah.js owns the VAPID subscribe + `/api/saya/push/subscribe` round-trip. Loaded `shared/push-jemaah.js` on jemaah-booking.ejs (was only on jemaah-portal.ejs before). Extends S335 (in-trip CTA on /saya) into the pre-trip window where readiness reminders (S351) + paket announcements (S193) are most useful — converts more jemaah to installed PWA + push-on BEFORE they're stuck in Saudi without signal.
358. ✅ Geolocation tagging for SOS — `submitJemaahHelpRequest` accepts an optional `location` arg validated via `normaliseLocation`: bounds-checked lat/lng, accuracy rounded to whole meters, garbage shapes drop to null. Stored in the EMAIL+WA `payload.location` JSON so admin viewer + state reader (`getBookingHelpRequestState`) + queue (`listPendingHelpRequests`) all surface it without extra columns. Notif body inlines `📍 LOKASI (GPS jemaah)` block with `Maps: https://maps.google.com/?q=<lat>,<lng>` so admin clicks straight from inbox. Audit `after.location` carries the same shape for compliance. SOS form on `/saya` requests `navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition` with **5s timeout + enableHighAccuracy** before POST; permission denial / timeout / GPS unavailable all resolve to null so the SOS still fires (geolocation is opt-in and must never block life-safety). Surfaces in two admin places: ruby-bordered banner on `/admin/bookings/:id` ("📍 Buka di Google Maps →") + per-row gold strip on `/admin/help-requests` queue with both inline coords and a Maps action button. Critical for in-trip jemaah lost in Mecca/Madinah crowds — admin/crew can navigate to the exact location instead of "tanya di telepon, ada di mana?".
359. ✅ Quick photo upload from readiness card — new `quickUploadMyDocByType({userId, type, file})` in `src/services/jemaahDocFiles.js` upserts a JemaahDocument row for `(jemaahId, type)` then delegates to the canonical `uploadMyDocFile` for the file move + status transition + admin notif. **Separate entry point from `uploadMyDocFile`** because the readiness card needs "PASSPORT not present → upload PASSPORT" to work in one tap, but the existing endpoint requires a known docId. **Service-level allowlist** `QUICK_UPLOAD_TYPES` mirrors S223 default required docs + extras (PASSPORT/VISA_UMROH/VACCINE_MENINGITIS/HEALTH_CERT/MANASIK_CERT/MARRIAGE_CERT/FAMILY_CARD/OTHER); `BAD_DOC_TYPE` 400 rejects typos. Route `POST /api/saya/documents/quick-upload/:type` reuses the existing `uploadSingleDoc` multer middleware so the 8MB cap + mime allowlist apply uniformly. Per-row 📸 Foto button next to each "yang masih kurang" item on the readiness card; tap fires a hidden `<input type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf" capture="environment">` so phones open the rear camera (or file picker on desktop). On success, page reloads so the card re-paints with the new check ticked off. Closes the friction gap — pre-S359 jemaah had to navigate to `/saya/profile`, scroll to the doc row, find the upload button.
360. ✅ PWA install funnel KPI — `src/services/pwaInstallFunnel.js` logs install events to AuditLog (no migration — leverages append-only invariant). Event taxonomy: `PROMPT_SHOWN / PROMPT_ACCEPTED / PROMPT_DISMISSED / IOS_HINT_SHOWN / IOS_HINT_DISMISSED / INSTALLED`. **Stored as `action='CREATE', entity='PwaInstall', entityId=<event>`** so the AuditAction enum constraint doesn't need extending; `after.event` duplicates for self-describing payloads. `getPwaInstallFunnel({days=30})` groupBy entityId returns counts + `acceptanceRate` (PROMPT_ACCEPTED ÷ PROMPT_SHOWN × 100, null when denom=0) + `iosCompletionRate` (approximate via `INSTALLED − PROMPT_ACCEPTED ÷ IOS_HINT_SHOWN`, clamped ≥0). **Sample-size guard** `lowSample=true` when both denominators < 5 (rates dimmed in UI). New `POST /api/pwa/install-event` endpoint via `optionalAuth` (anonymous-friendly — most events fire on public `/p/:slug` landing before login); always 204 even on validation failure (fire-and-forget telemetry must never break the client). `shared/pwa.js` fires telemetry on `beforeinstallprompt` (SHOWN), prompt choice (ACCEPTED/DISMISSED via `userChoice.outcome`), `appinstalled` (INSTALLED), iOS hint render (IOS_HINT_SHOWN), iOS hint close (IOS_HINT_DISMISSED). `keepalive: true` on fetch so events fired around navigation survive page unload. Admin overview panel on `/admin` shows two-column funnel (Android/Desktop vs iOS) with tier-coloured rate (≥30% emerald, ≥10% gold, else ruby — iOS tiers tighter at 15%/5%). Hidden when zero events in window. CSRF cookie + shared/csrf.js fetch monkey-patch make POST work from anonymous /p/:slug visitors without explicit token handling.
361. ✅ Crew offline contacts — extends S334 SWR scope with `/crew/contacts` so the `/crew` ICE list survives offline visits (cached HTML served when network fails). **Last-synced badge** below the H1 reads `localStorage['rp_crew_contacts_last_sync']` — updates on every online visit (SWR may have served cached HTML, but a fresh fetch happens in the background → "we'll have current data by next visit" is the signal that matters). When `navigator.onLine === false`: badge flips amber + "OFFLINE · data terakhir Xh lalu" so crew knows the displayed phones might be stale (jemaah swap rooms, new emergency contacts get added). `CACHE_VERSION` bumped `rp-v6 → rp-v7` so installed clients pick up the new SWR scope on next activation. Critical for Saudi hotel basements / mountain passes where calling jemaah's family without signal would be impossible without this cache.
362. ✅ PWA SW update prompt — every `CACHE_VERSION` bump silently activated a new SW via `skipWaiting()` + `clients.claim()`, but open tabs kept rendering HTML from the OLD SW's cache until manually closed (sometimes for days). `shared/pwa.js` now listens for `controllerchange` on `navigator.serviceWorker`; when fired AND a controller existed before (the `hadController` guard skips first-ever install), renders a gold-bordered banner at top of page: "🔄 Versi baru aktif. Refresh untuk muat ulang." Single-click Refresh button reloads via `window.location.reload()`; close button dismisses. **Dedupes by `#rp-sw-update` id check** so concurrent fires (rare but possible with multiple SW updates in flight) don't stack banners. Visible across every PWA-flavoured page (jemaah / crew / admin since all load pwa.js). Closes the staleness gap that bit silently on every deploy — users now know when fresh code is available without admin asking them to "tutup semua tab dan buka lagi".
363. ✅ PWA SOS shortcut — extends `manifest-jemaah.webmanifest` `shortcuts` array with "SOS Cepat" → `/saya?sos=1` as the **FIRST** shortcut so Android long-press on the home icon surfaces it at the top of the menu (browsers show shortcuts in declared order). `/saya` renders the SOS bottom-sheet inside the in-trip block; when `?sos=1` query is present, JS auto-fires `toggle.click()` to reveal the form + `scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'})` to bring it into focus + strips `?sos=1` from URL via `history.replaceState` so page reload doesn't keep re-opening. Pairs naturally with S358 GPS auto-attach — jemaah panic in Mecca crowd long-press icon, tap "SOS Cepat", form pops in 1s, type message, tap send (GPS captured silently), admin gets EMAIL+WA+push with `📍 Buka di Maps` link in <10s. **iOS Safari ignores manifest shortcuts** — Android-only safety surface; iOS users still reach SOS via the form inside `/saya` in-trip block. Pre-trip jemaah with no in-trip block get a clean no-op (no JS error, just nothing happens) since the toggle button isn't on the page.
364. ✅ Crew offline manifest — extends S334 SWR scope with `/crew/paket/` (per-paket manifest with full jemaah roster + room + dietary + tags). Same flaky-Saudi-signal scenario as S361 contacts. Per-slug last-synced badge in `crew-manifest.ejs` reads `localStorage['rp_crew_manifest_last_sync__<slug>']` (per-slug key so each paket tracks its own freshness — crew dampening 2 paket sees independent badges). Goes amber + "OFFLINE · manifest terakhir Xh lalu" when `navigator.onLine === false`. `CACHE_VERSION` bumped `rp-v7 → rp-v8`. Crew now have BOTH cross-paket contacts (S361) AND per-paket manifests (S364) available offline — the full operational picture survives without signal.
365. ✅ Wake Lock for Ibadah counter — `shared/screen-wake-lock.js` wraps the Screen Wake Lock API (Chrome 84+ / Safari 16.4+ / silently no-op below). `acquire()` requests a `'screen'` lock so display stays on; `release()` lets it sleep. **Re-acquires on `visibilitychange`** — OS auto-releases when page hidden (tab switch, app background), without re-acquire jemaah who briefly checked WhatsApp would come back to a dead lock for the rest of thawaf. Thawaf (7 putaran ≈ 25-40 min) + Sa'i (7 trips ≈ 30 min) views both acquire on enter + release on `pagehide` (covers bfcache too; `unload` would leak in bfcache). Best-effort throughout — unsupported browsers + permission denials log silently and the counter still works. Iconic UX — first thing jemaah notice that "this app actually understands ibadah".
366. ✅ App badging for unread notifs — `navigator.setAppBadge(unreadCount)` paints the unread count on the installed PWA's home-screen icon (Chromium-based browsers + some Android launchers; Safari ignores). `/saya` reads server-rendered `unreadCount` (from S5rr `countUnreadForUser`) and calls `setAppBadge(n)` when > 0 else `clearAppBadge()`. `/saya/notifications` always calls `clearAppBadge()` on visit (the page's `markAllReadForUser` already zero'd the server-side count via S5rr; badge needs to match). Best-effort — feature-detects `typeof navigator.setAppBadge === 'function'` + swallows promise rejections. No backend additions: reuses the existing unread count loader and the existing inbox-marks-read flow. Jemaah see the unread number on their home screen icon without opening the app, just like native messaging apps.

## Running locally

Requires **Node ≥ 20.6.0** — every script uses the built-in `--env-file-if-exists=.env` flag, which is only available from that version.

```bash
npm install
npm run db:migrate          # apply Prisma migrations
npm run db:seed             # seed users + paket + bookings + rooms + leads + payments
npm run dev                 # http://localhost:3001 (3000 collides, see .env)
```

Default port is `3001` (set in `.env`) because something else owns `3000` on this machine. `npm run db:studio` opens Prisma Studio.

`npm run db:reset` runs `prisma migrate reset` — **destructive**: drops the schema, re-runs every migration, and re-seeds. Never invoke without confirming with the user.

Tests run via Node's built-in `node:test` (zero deps, ships with Node ≥ 18). `npm test` runs `tests/*.test.js`; `npm run test:watch` re-runs on file change. New tests go in `tests/` as `<topic>.test.js`. Shared fixtures + cleanup hooks live in `tests/_helpers.js` — use `tempJemaah(t, tag)` / `tempPaket(t, tag, {dayCount})` / `tempBooking({...})`, all registered with `t.after()` so they're scoped per-test. Tests share the dev DB but isolate by unique `makeTag()` prefixes — never assert on global counts (seed rows exist), always filter by tag.

Older `scripts/smoke-*.js` are ad-hoc smoke runners predating `node:test` — they still work standalone (`node scripts/smoke-XX.js`) but new coverage should be written as `tests/*.test.js`. Migrating the legacy smokes is incremental, not a flag-day.

The static design package is still served — visit `/`, `/screens/paket-detail.html`, etc. — but Express now sits in front of it and blocks sensitive files (`.env`, `package.json`, `src/`, `prisma/`, `.claude/`, `memory/`). The `uploads/` directory is intentionally **public** (it's part of the static design package — currently holds `Proposal_Religio_Pro.docx`), so never drop secrets or unredacted user data there.

**Windows file-lock gotcha**: `prisma generate` will fail with `EPERM rename query_engine-windows.dll.node` if the dev server is running (`node --watch` holds the file open). Stop the dev process before running migrate/generate, then restart. Killing one npm/node PID isn't enough — the watch parent spawns a child worker; check `tasklist | grep node` and kill all three (npm wrapper, watcher, child) with `taskkill //F //PID …`.

## Backend architecture

- `src/env.js` — Zod-validated env config. Boot fails fast on bad values.
- `src/app.js` — Express factory. Order: JSON body → cookies → request log (dev) → `blockSensitive` middleware → API routes → static design files → 404 → error handler.
- `src/server.js` — Listens, prints banner, handles SIGINT/SIGTERM + Prisma disconnect.
- `src/lib/db.js` — Prisma client **singleton** (HMR-safe via `globalThis.__prisma`). Use `import { db } from '../lib/db.js'`.
- `src/middleware/error.js` — `HttpError` class + handler. JSON for `/api/*`; HTML 401 → 302 to `/login?next=…`; other HTML errors render `views/error.ejs`.
- `src/lib/format.js` — `res.locals.fmt` exposes `rpShort`, `rpFull`, `date`, `dateShort`, `dateLong` to every EJS template + `toNumber()` helper for Prisma Decimal → number.

### Route mounting order

Mount **nested admin sub-paths BEFORE** the generic `/admin` router, otherwise Express short-circuits on prefix match and the catch-all handler can swallow nested URLs. Same rule for `/api/paket/:slug/{hotels,days,rooms}` mounting before the public `paketJsonRouter`. **And: `paymentGatewayRouter` MUST mount BEFORE `paymentsRouter`** — the latter has `router.use(requireAuth, requireRole(...))` which intercepts any `/api/payments/*` prefix and 401s the Midtrans webhook before its signature verify ever runs (caught by HTTP integration tests). Current order in `src/app.js`:

```
/api/paket            → paketChildrenRouter (admin JSON CRUD)
/api/paket            → paketJsonRouter (public read)
/admin/paket          → paketAdminRouter
/admin/users          → usersAdminRouter
/admin/jemaah         → jemaahAdminRouter
/admin/bookings       → bookingsAdminRouter
/admin/payouts        → payoutsRouter
/admin/audit          → auditRouter
/admin/notifications  → notificationsRouter
/admin/payment-intents → paymentIntentsRouter   ← 5tt
/admin/incidents       → incidentsRouter         ← stage 13 (crew SOS queue)
/admin                → adminRouter (overview/manifest/bunking/finance)
```

### Sensitive-path block

`src/app.js` defines `SENSITIVE_FILES` + `SENSITIVE_PREFIXES`. Any new top-level file or directory containing secrets/code must be added there — `express.static` would otherwise expose it.

## Auth & RBAC

- **Token**: JWT (HS256, issuer `religio-pro`). Read order: `Authorization: Bearer …` → `rp_session` httpOnly cookie. Cookie defaults `sameSite=lax`, `secure` from env.
- **Helpers**: `src/lib/jwt.js`, `src/lib/auth.js`, `src/lib/audit.js` (append-only writer — **never updates or deletes**).
- **Middleware**: `requireAuth`, `requireRole(...roles)`, `optionalAuth` in `src/middleware/auth.js`. Use `requireAuth` *before* `requireRole(...)`.
- **Async routes**: wrap with `asyncHandler(fn)` from `src/lib/asyncHandler.js` (Express 4 doesn't catch rejected promises).
- **Rate limit**: `src/middleware/rateLimit.js` with a pluggable store (`src/lib/rateLimitStore.js`). When `REDIS_URL` env is set → Redis store (atomic `INCR + PEXPIRE` via `MULTI`, multi-instance safe). Unset → in-memory fixed-window bucket (single-instance only). **Fails open on store errors** — a Redis outage logs a warning but allows the request through, so a flaky cache never locks legitimate users out of login. Login: 10/min/IP, register: 5/min/IP. Store kind logged at first use (`[rateLimit] store = Redis ...`). Closed cleanly on SIGINT/SIGTERM via `stopRateLimit()`.
- **JSON API** (`/api/auth/*`): `POST /register` (public, creates JEMAAH only), `POST /login`, `POST /logout`, `GET /me`. Login uses generic "Email atau password salah" regardless of email existence.
- **HTML login** (`src/routes/authWeb.js`): `GET /login`, `POST /login` (form-encoded), `POST /logout`. After login, redirects by role:
  - `AGEN` → `/agen`
  - `JEMAAH` → `/saya`
  - `OWNER` / `SUPERADMIN` / `MANAJER_OPS` / `KASIR` → `/admin`
  - others → `/`
- **HTML register** (`src/routes/jemaahPortal.js`): `GET /register`, `POST /register` (form-encoded, JEMAAH role only, rate-limited 5/min). Creates `User` + linked `JemaahProfile` in one transaction, signs JWT, and redirects to `/saya?welcome=1`. The `/api/auth/register` JSON endpoint still exists alongside.
- **Anti-escalation**: SUPERADMIN cannot create/edit `OWNER` users (`guardEscalation` in `src/services/userAdmin.js`). OWNER role option is disabled in the user form for non-OWNERS.
- **Audit**: every LOGIN attempt (success and failure) and LOGOUT writes an `AuditLog` row with IP, user-agent, and `actorEmail` snapshot so deleted-user history survives.
- **CSRF protection**: `src/middleware/csrf.js` runs after cookie + body parsers, before any route. Double-submit cookie pattern — mints a 32-byte hex token in non-httpOnly cookie `rp_csrf`, requires it back on POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE via either `X-CSRF-Token` header OR `_csrf` body field. Bypasses GET/HEAD/OPTIONS, the Midtrans webhook (signed by upstream), and `/api/health`. **Every form POST in `views/` MUST include `<input type="hidden" name="_csrf" value="<%= csrfToken %>">`** (exposed via `res.locals.csrfToken`). **Every page that uses `fetch()` for state-changing calls MUST load `<script src="/shared/csrf.js"></script>`** before the inline JS — that script monkey-patches `window.fetch` to auto-attach the header from the cookie. Missing either → 403 `CSRF_FAILED` (JSON for `/api/*`, plain text for HTML routes).

## Database

- Prisma 6.x, `mysql` provider (MariaDB-compatible).
- Migrations live in `prisma/migrations/`. Never edit applied migrations — use `prisma migrate dev` to create new ones.
- **AuditLog is append-only** — never write code that updates or deletes rows from it. Same for `Payment` history (refund = new row, not edit).
- Money: `Decimal(15, 2)` for IDR amounts; `Decimal(15, 6)` for exchange rates. Non-IDR amounts also store `amountIdrEq` snapshot.
- Identity: 4 profile tables (`AgentProfile`, `JemaahProfile`, `StaffProfile`, `CrewProfile`) one-to-one with `User`. The 8-role RBAC enum is on `User.role`.
- Agent URL slug: `AgentProfile.slug` (e.g. `ahmad-w`) drives the `?a=` query param on auto-generated paket pages. Booking captures both the FK (`agentId`) **and** a snapshot (`agentSlugCap`) so reattribution audit survives slug renames.
- **Lead model** (`Lead`) is pre-booking only (status `COLD`/`WARM`). When converted, status becomes `CONVERTED` and `convertedBookingId` points at the new booking. `LOST` is terminal.
- **Room model** (`Room`) belongs to a paket; capacity defaults from kelas (QUAD=4, TRIPLE=3, DOUBLE=2, VVIP=1) but is override-able. Composite unique on `(paketId, roomNo)`. `Booking.roomId` is the assignment FK (nullable; cancellation sets it to null automatically).
- **JemaahDocument** — 1-per-type per jemaah (`@@unique([jemaahId, type])`). 8 doc types (PASSPORT/VISA_UMROH/MANASIK_CERT/HEALTH_CERT/VACCINE_MENINGITIS/MARRIAGE_CERT/FAMILY_CARD/OTHER), 5 statuses (PENDING/SUBMITTED/VERIFIED/REJECTED/EXPIRED). `upsertDoc` auto-stamps `submittedAt`/`verifiedAt` on status transitions (only on transitions — re-saving the same status does NOT re-stamp). Optional file attachment (5mm): `filePath`/`fileName`/`fileSize`/`mimeType`/`fileUploadedAt`; file lives at `private/docs/<jemaahId>/<docId>__<sanitised-basename>.<ext>`. One file per doc — re-upload replaces the prior file on disk.
- **PaymentIntent** (5pp) — gateway-side state, separate from `Payment` so an intent can fail (EXPIRED/CANCELLED/FAILED) without ever producing a money movement. Lifecycle: `CREATED → PENDING → SETTLED` (happy path) or terminal failure. `paymentId` 1:1 FK fills in only on first SETTLED transition — the guard against double-credit (Midtrans retries webhooks on failure). `orderId` format `PI-<intentId>` is the join key with Midtrans.
- **PaketCrew** (5oo) — M2M between `Paket` and MUTHAWWIF users. Composite PK `(paketId, userId)` makes assign-twice naturally idempotent (upsert). Assignment to ARCHIVED / soft-deleted paket is permitted (admin may want to keep historical record) but `listAssignedPaket` filters them out of the crew dashboard.
- **AttendanceMark** (5ww) — one per `(bookingId, paketDayId)` (`@@unique`), recording who showed up to each itinerary day. `present` Boolean + optional `notes`; `markedByUserId/At` stamps which crew last touched it. Re-marking is upsert — DB rows never duplicate. **No audit log** for these — high-volume per-trip operation; the row itself is the trail. Cascade delete on Booking + PaketDay for cleanup safety.

### Seed credentials & demo data

`prisma/seed.js` is idempotent. Seeded users:
- `owner@religio.pro` / `owner12345` — OWNER
- `kasir@religio.pro` / `kasir12345` — KASIR
- `ahmad@religio.pro` / `ahmad12345` — AGEN, slug `ahmad-w`

Seeded content (all belonging to one paket, `ramadhan-aqsa-2026`):
- 4 hotels (Madinah/Mekkah/Aqsa/Petra), 4 prices (Quad→VVIP, Double featured), 7 itinerary days
- 12 rooms (M-401..408 on lt 4 wing Selatan/Utara; M-501..504 on lt 5 wing Selatan/Eksekutif)
- 5 demo bookings `RP-DEMO-0000{1..5}` for `ahmad-w` (mixed statuses including 2 LUNAS) with Payment rows synced to paidAmount via `gatewayRef=DEMO-PAY-…`
- 6 demo leads (3 COLD + 3 WARM, mixed sources, with `phone` prefix `0888-DEMO-…` for idempotency)

## Public paket landing + booking (step 4)

- `GET /p/:slug` renders `views/paket.ejs` from DB. `?a=<agentSlug>` resolves to an `AgentProfile`; unknown slugs render the page in "no-agent / Kantor Pusat" mode.
- `GET /api/paket/:slug` returns the same data as JSON.
- `POST /api/booking` — public, anonymous, 8/min/IP rate limit.
- **Agent lock-in invariant**: `Booking.agentId` is set only when the slug resolves; `Booking.agentSlugCap` *always* snapshots the slug from the URL — even if invalid. A future audit can prove which URL the visitor came from, even if the slug is later deleted or reassigned.
- **Booking number scheme**: `RP-YYYY-NNNNN`. Generated by counting existing prefix-matched rows; collisions retry up to 5 times (uniqueness enforced by `bookingNo @unique`).
- **`paket.ejs` hotel render quirk**: the landing template explicitly renders only Madinah + Mekkah hotels in the "hotels" section. Hotels in other cities (AQSA, PETRA, ISTANBUL, JAKARTA, etc.) are stored fine but won't appear on the public landing page without a template change.
- **Authenticated self-booking (5t)**: both `GET /p/:slug` and `POST /api/booking` use `optionalAuth`. When the visitor is a logged-in JEMAAH, the form pre-fills name+phone from their `JemaahProfile`, and `createBooking` reuses that profile (no new row spawned) + sets `Booking.jemaahUserId` directly. A "Booking untuk orang lain?" link sends `forceAnonymous=1` in the form body to opt out of the link and spawn a fresh profile for the third-party jemaah.
- **Admin walk-in booking (5w)**: `GET /admin/bookings/new` + `POST /admin/bookings` (4 admin roles incl. KASIR) wraps the same `createBooking` service with an `adminCreator = {id,email,role}` param. When set, the function **forces `loggedInUser = null`** (the admin session is the actor, not the jemaah) — `selfBooked` stays false and `jemaahUserId` stays null so the jemaah can still later register + claim the booking themselves via `/saya`. Audit row marks `after.adminCreated = true` with the admin's actor email/role.
- **Separation of duties for money flow**: roles are split deliberately. `KASIR` records incoming payments + creates walk-in bookings, but **cannot** issue refunds (5m) or disburse komisi payouts (5x) — those need OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS. Don't extend the KASIR role to outbound money without a deliberate decision; the current split mirrors how cash-handling controls work in physical offices.
- **Notification enqueues are fire-and-forget**: every `enqueueNotification` and event-helper call inside `booking.js` / `payment.js` / `payouts.js` is wrapped in try/catch. A failure to insert the notif row (DB hiccup, bad payload, missing template) logs to console but never aborts the transaction that triggered it. The notif row becomes the audit trail of "we tried to tell the jemaah" — even when the actual send fails, the queue + admin viewer surface the gap. **Do not** add notif writes inside the same `$transaction` as money-state writes — the right priority order is "save money state first, attempt notify second".
- **Komisi rate immutability (5u/5v/stage 14)**: when `Paket.komisiRate`, `AgentProfile.komisiRateOverride`, OR `AgentPaketKomisi.rate` changes, **existing `Komisi` rows are NOT recomputed**. The rate at the moment of the LUNAS transition is locked in via the `Komisi.amount` snapshot. This is the right behaviour — historical earnings reflect the contract that was in force when the agent earned them — but means a "global rate change" admin should bump expectations, not historical numbers. Form helper text spells this out for all three surfaces (paket-edit "Komisi agen (%)", user-edit "Override komisi (%)", and the per-agen matrix panel).
- **3-state Zod schema for nullable form fields** — when a form field needs to support "explicit clear" (empty input → `NULL` in DB) vs "leave unchanged" (field not in body), the preprocessor must distinguish three input states: `undefined` (key absent → no DB write), `null` (key present, value empty → clear to NULL), and a real value. Naive `(v) => v === '' ? undefined : Number(v)` collapses the first two, so empty input fails to clear. See `komisiOverridePct` in `src/services/userAdmin.js` for the pattern: `z.union([z.number()…, z.null()]).optional()` paired with a preprocessor that maps the three cases distinctly.

## Agen Portal (`/agen`)

`requireAuth + requireRole('AGEN')`. Single-page with 4 client-switched tabs (state preserved in `?tab=` query param):

- **Leads Pipeline** — 4-column kanban. `Cold` + `Warm` from `Lead` rows (`status IN ('COLD','WARM')`). `Hot/DP` from `Booking` rows (`status IN ('PENDING','BOOKED','DP_PAID','PARTIAL')`). `Lunas` from `Booking` rows with `status=LUNAS`. KPI strip on top. Inline lead create/edit/delete via fetch; **Promote to Booking** modal on WARM cards calls `POST /api/leads/:id/convert` which reuses the public `createBooking()` and sets `Lead.status=CONVERTED + convertedBookingId`.
- **Marketing kit** — list of ACTIVE paket; each card shows the auto-generated link `/p/<slug>?a=<agent.slug>` with copy-to-clipboard button.
- **Wallet & Komisi** — totals + transaction list (komisi grouped by status PENDING/EARNED/PAID/CANCELLED) + read-only payout history table (last 20 `KomisiPayout` rows for this agent, with payoutNo + method + reference for bank-statement cross-check).
- **Analitik** — funnel (5 stages from Cold to LUNAS) + lead source breakdown + 30-day sparkline. Date range filter (`from`/`to` query params, defaults to 30-day window).

All `/api/leads/*` endpoints are scoped to the logged-in agent's profile via `resolveAgent` middleware in `src/routes/leads.js` (ownership enforced by `loadOwnedLead`). Cross-agent access returns 403.

## Jemaah Portal (`/saya`)

`requireAuth + requireRole('JEMAAH')`. Anonymous public bookings each create a fresh `JemaahProfile`, so a returning jemaah usually has multiple profile records floating around. The portal stitches them back together via a **claim** flow.

- **`GET /register`** — public HTML form. Creates JEMAAH user + linked profile; auto-logs-in.
- **`GET /saya`** — dashboard. Shows claim form + list of bookings where `Booking.jemaahUserId = req.user.id`.
- **`POST /api/saya/claim`** — body `{bookingNo, phone}`. Matches `bookingNo` exact + `phone` after stripping spaces/dashes/parens. Generic 404 on any mismatch (deliberate — guards against bookingNo enumeration). 409 if already claimed by a different user. Idempotent if same user.
- **`GET /saya/bookings/:id`** — read-only booking detail (no admin tools). Ownership via `jemaahUserId` filter.
- **`GET /saya/profile`** — form for editing the jemaah's own canonical profile (the one linked via `JemaahProfile.userId`). Fields are the same set admin can edit on `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`; validation reuses `JemaahSchema` from `src/services/jemaahAdmin.js`.
- **`POST /api/saya/profile`** — JSON update for the form above. Audit row uses `actor.role=JEMAAH` as the self-edit signal (no explicit `via` flag needed). Form includes a "Preferensi notifikasi" panel (5jj) with two channel toggles (`notifWa`, `notifEmail`); the route normalises unchecked HTML checkboxes to explicit `false` before calling `updateMyProfile` so opting out actually persists (an unchecked checkbox is absent from `req.body` — without the normaliser the `notifPref` preprocessor reads it as "no change").
- **`POST /api/saya/documents`** + **`DELETE /api/saya/documents/:id`** — jemaah self-submits or removes their own document tracking. Restrictions in the next section.
- **`GET /saya/paket`** (5dd) — browser for ACTIVE paket with a per-card `alreadyBooked` badge based on the jemaah's existing non-cancelled bookings. "BOOK SEKARANG" links to `/p/:slug` where 5t's pre-fill kicks in; the CTA label flips to "BOOK LAGI" when a prior booking exists. Single batched query for the user's bookings (no N+1).
- **`POST /api/saya/bookings/:id/request-cancel`** (5ff) — jemaah submits a cancellation request with a reason. Sets `Booking.cancelRequested = true` + `cancelRequestedAt` + `cancelRequestReason`, but **does NOT change `status`** — admin must still approve via `cancelBooking`. Refuses if booking is CANCELLED/REFUNDED or a prior request is already pending (409 `ALREADY_REQUESTED`). When admin runs `cancelBooking`, the three request fields are cleared in the same transaction (implicit approval — no separate "approve request" endpoint). Admin surfaces: amber banner at the top of `/admin/bookings/:id` info panel, plus a "REQ CANCEL" badge under the status pill in the manifest table.
- **`GET /saya/notifications`** (5ll) — read-only inbox of the jemaah's own notifications. Filtered strictly by `Notification.recipientUserId = req.user.id` (capped at 50, newest first). Channel badge + status pill (PENDING/SENT/FAILED/SKIPPED) + body preview + error message when not SENT. The page links back to `/saya/profile` so an opted-out jemaah seeing rows with `status=SKIPPED, error="recipient opted out of WA notifications"` has a clear path to flip the toggle. Admin/system notifs (e.g. `CANCEL_REQUESTED` fan-out to admin emails) deliberately enqueue **without** `recipientUserId`, so they never leak into any jemaah inbox. **Unread badge (5rr)**: dashboard topbar shows a gold count pill next to the "Notifikasi" link via `countUnreadForUser`. Opening the inbox calls `markAllReadForUser` *after* fetching the rows, so rendered unread rows get a gold left-border + dot affordance on first visit, then the badge clears for next render. `Notification.readAt` is null until first view; admin/system rows (no `recipientUserId`) are never counted.

### Self-submit document rules (5s)

The jemaah-side `submitMyDoc` in `src/services/jemaahPortal.js` enforces tighter rules than the admin's `upsertDoc`:

- **Status is inferred from input, never set directly.** `refNumber` filled → `SUBMITTED`; empty → `PENDING`. Jemaah can never set `VERIFIED` or `REJECTED` — those are staff verdicts.
- **Re-submitting a `VERIFIED` doc resets the verdict**: status drops to `SUBMITTED`, `verifiedAt`/`verifiedById` are cleared. This handles the re-review workflow (e.g. paspor renewed, new ref number).
- **`deleteMyDoc` refuses to delete `VERIFIED` docs** (409 `DOC_LOCKED`) — staff sign-off is a soft lock; only admin can remove a verified record.
- Auth signal in audit: `actorRole=JEMAAH` is sufficient — no `selfSubmit: true` flag needed (though the implementation does add it to `after` for explicit grep).

### Document file uploads (5mm)

Files attach to an existing `JemaahDocument` row (1 file per doc, re-upload replaces). Flow:

- **Storage**: `private/docs/<jemaahId>/<docId>__<sanitised-basename>.<ext>`. The `private/` dir is in `SENSITIVE_PREFIXES` (`src/app.js`) — `express.static` returns 404 for any direct request, files are only reachable via authenticated download routes. **Any new private dir must be added to that prefix list** before being used for uploads, otherwise it leaks.
- **Multer two-step**: `src/middleware/docUpload.js` writes incoming files to OS temp via multer disk storage; the route handler then calls `moveUploadedFile()` in `src/lib/docStorage.js` to relocate them into the per-jemaah dir. This split keeps multer agnostic of `jemaahId/docId` (only known after auth + param resolution).
- **Limits**: 8 MB cap (`MAX_DOC_BYTES`), mime allowlist `PDF / JPG / PNG / WEBP / HEIC` (`ALLOWED_MIME`). Both are enforced in multer's `fileFilter`/`limits` AND re-checked in the service before move — defence in depth.
- **Filename rule**: `sanitiseBasename()` strips path separators, diacritics, and non-portable chars; caps to 100 chars; falls back to `"file"` on empty. Applied to both the on-disk filename AND the `fileName` column used in `Content-Disposition`. **Never trust the user's raw filename for either path or download header.**
- **Status side-effects on upload**: PENDING → SUBMITTED (file presence = "I've submitted it"); VERIFIED → SUBMITTED + `verifiedAt`/`verifiedById` cleared (mirrors `submitMyDoc` re-review behaviour). Other statuses pass through unchanged.
- **Delete coverage**: `deleteMyDocFile` removes the file but keeps the row; `deleteMyDoc` (jemaah) + admin `deleteDoc` both delete the file on disk too (best-effort) so deleting a doc row never leaves an orphan blob. VERIFIED docs refuse both kinds of delete from the jemaah side (`DOC_LOCKED` 409) — only admin can remove.
- **Download routes** (auth + ownership enforced per-request, NOT via static):
  - `GET /saya/documents/:docId/file` — jemaah; ownership = `doc.jemaah.userId === req.user.id`
  - `GET /admin/jemaah/:jemaahId/documents/:docId/file` — admin RBAC + **tuple guard**: rejects with 404 unless `doc.jemaahId === :jemaahId`. The tuple guard prevents enumerating files across jemaah by guessing docIds on a fixed jemaah URL.
- Both responses are `Content-Disposition: inline` with the stored `fileName` — browsers preview PDFs/images directly; users get a sensible "Save as" name.
- **Inline thumbnails (5vv)** — the doc panels (`/saya/profile` + `/admin/jemaah/:id/edit`) render a 56-64px `<img>` thumbnail when `mimeType ∈ {image/jpeg, image/png, image/webp}` (via `isInlineImageMime()` in `src/lib/docStorage.js`); PDF gets `📄`, anything else (HEIC/HEIF) gets `🖼️`. HEIC is deliberately fallback even though it's in the upload allowlist — Chrome/Firefox don't ship HEIC decoders, so an `<img>` tag would render a broken-image square.
- **Server-side cached thumbnails (stage 15)** — uploads now auto-generate a 256-px JPEG thumb at `private/docs/<jemaahId>/thumbs/<docId>.jpg` via `sharp` (`src/lib/docThumbnail.js`). Thumb download routes `/saya/documents/:docId/thumb` + `/admin/jemaah/:jemaahId/documents/:docId/thumb` serve the cache when it exists, **fall back to the full file** when it doesn't (so legacy uploads + non-image mimes keep working without a flag day). Generation is best-effort — sharp throws on a corrupt source don't abort the upload, just log a warning. Thumb is deleted alongside the source on `deleteMyDocFile` / `deleteMyDoc` / admin `deleteDoc` so the thumbs dir doesn't leak. `src` in the views uses `/thumb` for `<img>` (cheap) but `/file` for the click-through `<a href>` + "Lihat" button (full quality). EXIF rotation is honoured (`sharp.rotate()`) so portrait phone photos aren't sideways. Backfill existing uploads with `node scripts/backfill-thumbnails.js` (idempotent — only generates when no cached thumb exists; `--force` to regenerate, `--dry-run` to preview).

### Profile soft-merge on claim (5p.2)

On every successful claim, `claimBooking` runs a soft-merge inside one transaction when the user has their own profile AND the booking points elsewhere. **Order is load-bearing** — re-point booking FIRST so the source's remaining-bookings count is accurate, then merge with knowledge of whether source will be deleted:

1. Re-point `Booking.jemaahId` from the anonymous booking-profile → the user's canonical profile.
2. Count source's remaining bookings (zero ⇒ source becomes an orphan and will be deleted).
3. Run `mergeProfileInto(target, source, { sourceWillBeDeleted })`:
   - **User profile wins** on conflict: copy `nik / passportNo / passportExpiry / birthDate / gender / address / emergencyContact / notes` from source only when the user's field is null/empty.
   - **Defensive @unique check** for `nik` and `passportNo` — excludes both target AND source from the clash query; only a *third* profile counts as a real conflict.
   - **@unique transfer requires source orphan**: when source still has other bookings, we can't take its NIK/passport away (those other booking-profiles would lose the data) — skip the copy, source keeps the value. When source is about to be deleted, NULL its @unique field first (frees the DB constraint), then patch the value onto target.
4. Transfer `JemaahDocument` rows from source → user. **User wins** on `(jemaahId, type)` collision (source duplicate deleted; source unique re-pointed).
5. Delete the source profile if it has zero remaining bookings.
6. Audit `Booking UPDATE` includes `{merged, targetJemaahId, fieldsCopied, docsTransferred, oldProfileDeleted}` summary.

This means a jemaah who has booked 3 paket anonymously, then registers and claims all 3, ends up with a single canonical profile + their docs consolidated — even though the public booking flow keeps creating new profile rows.

After 5t, the merge path mostly handles **legacy** anonymous bookings made before the user registered. New bookings made while logged in already point at the canonical profile (and have `jemaahUserId` set), so the merge becomes a no-op for them.

## Crew Portal (`/crew`)

`requireAuth + requireRole('MUTHAWWIF')`. Read-only workspace for guides/leaders travelling with the jemaah. Login redirect: MUTHAWWIF → `/crew` (added to `redirectForRole` in `src/routes/authWeb.js` alongside AGEN/JEMAAH).

- **`GET /crew`** — dashboard. Lists paket where this user has a `PaketCrew` row, scoped to non-ARCHIVED + non-soft-deleted, sorted by `departureDate` ascending (next trip on top). Each card: title, slug, departureDate, durationDays, booking count, kursi terisi vs kursi total, status badge.
- **`GET /crew/paket/:slug`** — manifest. Returns 404 (generic `NOT_ASSIGNED`) when the crew isn't assigned — anti-enumeration. Includes per-jemaah: `bookingNo`, `kelas`, `paxCount`, `status`, room assignment, jemaah `fullName`/`phone`/`emergencyContact`/`passportNo`/`passportExpiry`, plus `docPills` (5-type curated strip via `pillsForJemaah`). Filters out CANCELLED/REFUNDED bookings — manifest is "who's actually going on this trip".
- **`GET /crew/paket/:slug/export.csv`** (5ss) — offline-friendly CSV snapshot of the same manifest. Built for crew on the road with weak/no signal — open in any spreadsheet app on a phone or laptop. UTF-8 BOM + RFC 4180 quoting (same convention as the admin 5gg export). Filename `crew_manifest_<slug>_<YYYY-MM-DD>.csv`. Same money-stripped column set as the HTML manifest — booking identity, room, and per-curated-doc-type state, **no totalAmount/paidAmount**. Refuses (404 `NOT_ASSIGNED`) when the requesting crew isn't on the paket — the assignment guard is the same as the HTML view.
- **`GET /crew/paket/:slug/attendance`** (5ww) — per-day attendance overview. Lists every `PaketDay` (in itinerary order) with `presentCount` / `markedCount` / `totalActive` so crew sees at a glance which days are unmarked. Active bookings only (CANCELLED/REFUNDED excluded) — matches the manifest definition of "who's actually going".
- **`GET /crew/paket/:slug/attendance/:dayId`** (5ww) — per-day grid: jemaah list + a custom checkbox toggle + free-text notes input per row, POST to `/crew/paket/:slug/attendance/:dayId/:bookingId`. The service `setAttendanceMark` enforces a **tuple guard**: `(dayId, bookingId)` MUST both belong to the assigned paket — cross-paket combinations return 404 (anti-enumeration; same generic 404 as the unassigned case). Each save shows a green confirmation banner, then strips `?ok=saved` from the URL so reloads don't keep flashing it. Admins can audit the resulting marks at `/admin/paket/:slug/attendance` (5zz — see Admin Dashboard sub-pages).
- **Write surface from `/crew`** is deliberately small: attendance marks (5ww) + SOS / incident reports (stage 13). No jemaah / payment / room assignment edits from the portal. Chat from the static `screens/crew-app.html` mockup is a deliberate follow-up.
- **SOS / incidents** — floating ruby pulse button (`partials/sos-fab.ejs`) on every `/crew/*` page opens a modal with type (SOS / MEDICAL / LOST_JEMAAH / SECURITY / LOGISTICAL / OTHER) + optional location + message. POSTs to `/crew/sos` (form-encoded so the no-JS fallback works). `createIncident` in `src/services/incidents.js` enforces MUTHAWWIF role, resolves `paketSlug` to a paketId **only if the crew is actually assigned** (unknown/unassigned slug silently null — the SOS landing is more important than tagging it), and fires a fan-out (`notifyIncidentCreated`) to every ACTIVE OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS via **three channels**: EMAIL (queued, retry-with-backoff), WA (queued, same), and Web Push (real-time, stage 17). Subject prefix `[CRITICAL]` for SOS, `[URGENT]` otherwise. Crew dashboard `/crew` shows the last 10 of their own incidents with current admin status (OPEN / ACKED / RESOLVED) so they can see whether tim sudah respon.
- **Incident state machine** is one-way: `OPEN → ACKED → RESOLVED`. No back-transitions and no re-open — follow-ups create a new incident so the timeline stays honest. Admin queue at `/admin/incidents` (OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS) sorts `[status asc, createdAt desc]` so OPEN bubbles to top. Resolve requires a `resolution` note (min 3 chars, max 2000). Jumping `OPEN → RESOLVED` auto-stamps `ackedAt`/`ackedById` to the resolving admin — the timeline always records both verbs.
- **Notif fan-out invariants for incidents**: `recipientUserId` omitted (admin-targeted; never bleeds into a jemaah inbox per 5ll). Failure to enqueue is logged but does NOT abort the incident write — the SOS row landing is more important than the notification firing.
- **Web Push (stage 17)** — the third fan-out channel. `pushToAdmins` in `src/services/webPush.js` looks up every `PushSubscription` owned by an ACTIVE admin and calls `web-push.sendNotification` per row. Per-device subscriptions are managed from a toggle bar on `/admin/incidents` (`shared/push-admin.js` handles permission → fetch `/api/admin/push/config` for VAPID public key → `PushManager.subscribe` → POST to `/api/admin/push/subscribe`). The SW (`shared/sw.js`) `push` handler shows a Notification; SOS payloads set `requireInteraction:true` so the toast doesn't auto-dismiss. `notificationclick` focuses an existing tab on the target URL or opens a new one. **Self-cleanup**: 404/410 from web-push means the endpoint is dead — the dispatcher scrubs the row so the table stays bounded. **Fake-mode**: when `VAPID_PUBLIC` is absent, `sendOne` logs to stdout instead of calling web-push — subscribe/unsubscribe DB ops still work, so the full surface is testable without VAPID creds. Boot log `[push] sender = web-push` (real) vs `[push] sender = console (VAPID_PUBLIC absent ...)` (fake). To enable in prod: `npx web-push generate-vapid-keys` → drop `VAPID_PUBLIC` + `VAPID_PRIVATE` + `VAPID_CONTACT` into `.env` → restart. **CACHE_VERSION bump in sw.js is required** when push handler logic changes so installed clients pick it up on next SW activation.
- **Money-stripped on purpose**: `getAssignedManifest` does NOT select `totalAmount` / `paidAmount` / `payments`. Crew often help with logistics but cash collection is a separate role (KASIR) — keeping balances out of the crew UI mirrors the existing separation of duties around outbound money (5x: KASIR can't disburse payouts).

Admin manages assignment from `/admin/paket/:slug/edit`: a "Crew (muthawwif)" panel lists currently-assigned users + a dropdown of every ACTIVE MUTHAWWIF for one-click assign. Wire-up via JSON: `POST /api/paket/:slug/crew` (`{ userId }`) and `DELETE /api/paket/:slug/crew/:userId` — both in `src/routes/paketChildren.js` so they pick up the existing OWNER/SUPERADMIN/MANAJER_OPS gate.

## Mobile experience (stage 13)

`/saya` (jemaah) and `/crew` (muthawwif) are PWA-installable. The shell is a thin layer over the existing EJS views — no separate native build — so any backend change is immediately reflected on the installed app.

- **`shared/manifest.webmanifest`** — `start_url=/saya`, `display=standalone`, gold-on-onyx theme, 3 shortcuts (Booking / Profil / Notifikasi). Linked from every mobile-relevant view via `views/partials/pwa-head.ejs` (also drops apple-touch-icon + theme-color meta).
- **`shared/sw.js`** — minimal service worker. Static assets (`/shared/*`, `/uploads/*`, common file extensions) are cache-first with background refresh; same-origin HTML pages are network-first with cache fallback, then `/shared/offline.html` as last resort. **Deliberately skips `/api/*`** — those carry per-user CSRF cookies and stale cached responses would mislead a balance/queue screen. Bump `CACHE_VERSION` to invalidate every entry on next activation.
- **`shared/pwa.js`** — registers the SW + captures `beforeinstallprompt`. Exposes a tiny click handler so any view can wire a `<button data-pwa-install>` to fire the prompt from a user gesture. iOS Safari doesn't fire that event, so the same file injects an **iOS install hint** card (`#rp-ios-hint`) 1.2 s after load: bottom-fixed dismissable banner with Share-icon SVG + "Tap Share → Add to Home Screen" instruction. Suppression: not iOS, in-app browser (FB/IG/Line/CriOS/FxiOS), already running standalone, or previously dismissed (localStorage `rp_ios_install_hint_dismissed`). `body.has-m-tabs` adjusts bottom offset so the hint sits above the bottom-nav instead of overlapping it. All styling injected inline — no view edits needed; no separate stylesheet. Bumping `CACHE_VERSION` in `sw.js` is required when this script changes so installed clients pick up the new logic on next activation.
- **Mobile bottom-nav** for jemaah — `views/partials/mobile-tabs.ejs` (Beranda / Paket / Notifikasi / Profil) shows only at ≤ 720 px. JS-side active-tab via longest-prefix match (so `/saya/bookings/:id` highlights Beranda). Tokens.css scopes the styles + body class `.has-m-tabs` reserves bottom padding so content isn't covered. The 5 jemaah views carry that class; redundant top-bar nav links hide on mobile (`.topnav-link` `display: none`) since the bottom tab bar covers them.
- **Responsive baseline** lives in `shared/tokens.css` under the `@media (max-width: 720px)` block: `h1/h2/h3` clamp, `.wrap` padding shrink, `table { display: block; overflow-x: auto; }` fallback, `.grid-2 / .form-grid { 1fr }`, `.topbar { flex-wrap }`. Per-view `@media` blocks tighten further (tap target ≥ 44 px, card-per-row layouts for dense tables like crew-attendance-day).
- **Sensitive-path block applies to PWA assets too**: don't drop secrets in `shared/` (it's public + cached aggressively by the SW). Per-user data must come via authenticated routes.

### Offline-friendly attendance (5xx field-use)

Muthawwif mark attendance from a phone in a bus or on a mountain pass where signal drops out. A failed POST mustn't lose the mark — `shared/attendance-queue.js` is an IndexedDB-backed queue (`religio-attendance.queue` store) that captures form submits, drains on `online` event + 20 s tick, and updates per-row sync pills (queued / syncing / ok / error) from the queue state.

- **Server endpoint is unchanged**. The `setAttendanceMark` upsert keyed on `(dayId, bookingId)` is already idempotent — replaying the same payload N times leaves the DB in the same state as sending it once. That's the contract the queue depends on; the smoke `scripts/smoke-offline-attendance.js` explicitly verifies "replay × 3 → 1 row".
- **drain() is single-flight** — concurrent calls short-circuit. Status transitions: `pending → syncing → done` (deleted from queue) or `failed` (incremented `attemptCount`, `lastError` set). The DOM updates from the queue's `onChange` notifier — banner state + per-row sync pill paint from the truth, not from optimistic JS state.
- **No-JS fallback path intact** — the same form posts traditionally, the server returns 302 `?ok=saved`, and the visible green banner fires from a URL query check. With JS, the form is intercepted and the redirect-following fetch path takes over.
- **`navigator.onLine === false` short-circuits the fetch** — no point hitting the network when the browser already knows. Optimistic UI (label "Hadir / Tidak hadir") still flips immediately so the crew sees their input acknowledged.

## Admin Dashboard (`/admin`)

`requireAuth + requireRole('OWNER','SUPERADMIN','MANAJER_OPS')` (KASIR can view some pages, see per-route guards). Tabbed single page (`?tab=`):
